# 复兴！乌卢鲁运动会 - Revival! The Uluru Games

## 目录

- RUG-01 翻滚碰碰车 / Roller Coaster
- RUG-02 邻人友爱 / The Lovely Neighbor
- RUG-03 金格！金格！ / Chinga! Chinga!
- RUG-04 后手直拳 / Cross
- RUG-05 漂浮球们 / The Buoy Balls
- RUG-06 涅槃日 / Day of Rebirth
- RUG-07 老火种 / The Old Flame
- RUG-08 火警热线 / Triple Zero
- RUG-09 万事救星 / The Superman
- RUG-10 过家家 / Let's Play House
- RUG-11 玻璃鞋 / Glass Slippers
- RUG-12 千年独行 / Lone Journey
- RUG-13 “永不沉没” / "Unsinkable"
- RUG-14 跑者史诗 / The Epic of Runners
- RUG-15 红岩护卫队 / The Uluru Guardians

## RUG-01 翻滚碰碰车 / Roller Coaster

**答录机**：嗨，你好。这儿是沙丝绒的家。\
**Answering Machine**: G'day, you've reached Desert Flannel.

**答录机**：我现在不在家，又或是没空接电话，如果你想联系我，请在“滴”声后留言。\
**Answering Machine**: I'm not home right now, or I don't have time for calls. Please leave a message after the "beep."

**答录机**：嘿！还有二十分钟比赛就要开场了！你跑哪儿去了？！\
**Answering Machine**: Hello? We've only got 20 minutes before the game starts! Where are you?

**答录机**：如果你不是死了，就快给我滚过来！\
**Answering Machine**: Get your ass here now, unless you're dead!

**答录机**：好吧，好吧，我知道你对运动没什么兴趣，但你起码真的很缺钱——不是吗？！不然你也不会来找我！\
**Answering Machine**: Look, look, I know you're not into these games, but you can really use the money, right? Otherwise, you wouldn't have come to me!

房间中漆黑一片，厚遮光窗帘的那侧是一个漂亮的大晴天。\
Not a single beam of light can pass through the thick blackout curtain. Blocked out by it is a perfect sunny day.

**沙丝绒**：呼……\
**Desert Flannel**: Emm ...

**答录机**：如果你今天放我鸽子，我们两个就都完了！\
**Answering Machine**: If you stand me up again, we're both screwed!

**沙丝绒**：呃……咳咳，吵死了……有什么事儿周四再说……\
**Desert Flannel**: Urrhh ... Emm, whatever ... Just leave it to Thursday.

**答录机**：周四的比赛是最重要的比赛，我一定会因此被开除的——求你了，该死的……快点儿过来！\
**Answering Machine**: The game on Thursday is crucial. I will get expelled if I mess it up! I'm begging you, d**n it! Just come over NOW!

**沙丝绒**：周……四？\
**Desert Flannel**: Thur ... Thursday?

鼓囊囊的被窝与床铺夹层之中，两足行走的动物将自己从梦境的泥潭中拔出。\
Between the quilt and the bed, the bipedal animal is struggling to come back to the waking world.

**沙丝绒**：等等——周四？！\
**Desert Flannel**: Wait. It's Thursday?!

惊吓如同迎头而来的一盆冷水。\
The word is like a head-on shocking blow.

她错过得太多了。\
She has missed out on so many things.

“错过”是一件很容易的事情。\
A similar misfortune befalls someone else, too.

**维尔汀**：……我们错过了正确的路口，这和地图上写的不一样。\
**Vertin**: We missed the right junction. The roads are different from the map Mr. Slouch Hat gave us.

**维尔汀**：宽檐帽先生给我们的地图太老了，已经不能用了。\
**Vertin**: It's too outdated to provide any useful information.

**兔毛手袋**：很好。又一次。我们已经走错了……嗯，四次。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Terrific! We've gone wrong again. This is like ... yeah, the fourth time.

**兔毛手袋**：鉴于我短暂的生命需要为这个世界所有活物创造巨大价值——\
**Medicine Pocket**: Since my short life is supposed to be spent in creating huge value for all the living things in this world ...

**兔毛手袋**：圣洛夫应该为我找个更靠谱点的保镖，也让澳大利亚的接洽人准备一份更合理的地图！\
**Medicine Pocket**: The Foundation should have sent me another bodyguard—a more reliable one! And the contact here should have offered us a more reliable map!

**维尔汀**：我就是那儿最好且唯一能保证你安全的“保镖”。\
**Vertin**: I am the one and only reliable "bodyguard" who can keep you safe among all the others in the Foundation.

**维尔汀**：拉普拉斯很重视你，他们不想让你经历……任何危险。\
**Vertin**: You are of great significance to Laplace. They don't want you to take any risks.

城市变化得很快，地图也一样。\
Cities always change, and maps are supposed to follow them in step.

**维尔汀**：我们可以退回上一个路口，或者继续向前，300米后有一条小路，能够直达翻滚鳄书籍专卖店。\
**Vertin**: We can go back to the last junction or keep going forward. There is a trail about 300 meters ahead, and it leads all the way to the Rolling Croc Bookstore.

**维尔汀**：你需要看看地图吗？\
**Vertin**: You want to check the map?

**兔毛手袋**：以科研者的身份出发，一个方法行不通，就换下一个——\
**Medicine Pocket**: When things don't work out one way, a researcher will find another.

**兔毛手袋**：噢，这不就来了！\
**Medicine Pocket**: See, there comes another way!

打街拐角冒出头来的小姑娘被拦个正好。\
The girl coming around from the corner is the perfect choice.

**兔毛手袋**：嘿！等一下——可……燃点小姐，对吧？\
**Medicine Pocket**: Hey, wait! Ms. Spa-Spathodea, right?

**可燃点**：唔——嗯？你是谁？\
**Spathodea**: Umm ... Hmm? Who are you?

**可燃点**：……我们——我们认识吗？\
**Spathodea**: Umm, do I know you?

她的鼻尖有汗，两只脚依然保持着运动的姿态。\
With sweat on the tip of her nose, she keeps hopping on the spot.

一枚写着名字的“好朋友徽章”别在她的胸前，她显然没意识到这一点。\
A Bestie Badge with her name on it is pinned to her chest. Clearly, she is not aware of what gives her away.

**维尔汀**：我们刚到达澳大利亚不久。\
**Vertin**: We arrived in Australia not long ago.

**兔毛手袋**：但我们已经迷失了很久-很久，太久了。久到对人类产生危害。\
**Medicine Pocket**: But we've been lost for way too long, so long that the human society has begun to suffer economic losses because I've been loafing around.

兔毛手袋将手臂搭在女学生的肩膀上，轻微地摇动着她的身体。\
Medicine Pocket holds the girl on her shoulders and slightly shakes her body.

**兔毛手袋**：而你，可以使用你生命中不值一提的几分钟或几小时为全人类带来帮助——带我们去找“翻滚鳄”。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Now, you are given an opportunity to help the whole of humanity, and it only takes a few minutes, well, maybe hours, of your meaningless life—Take us to the Rolling Croc.

**维尔汀**：很抱歉打扰你，我们在找一家书店。\
**Vertin**: Excuse us, we're looking for a bookstore.

**维尔汀**：它的名字叫翻滚鳄，在招牌上悬挂着一只鳄鱼皮制的手鼓。\
**Vertin**: It's called the Rolling Croc, with a hand drum made of crocodile skin hanging on the signboard.

**兔毛手袋**：而其中，藏着我所需要的菌菇类魔药分析残本。\
**Medicine Pocket**: And that very store has the fragment of the fungus potion analysis report I want.

**兔毛手袋**：如果不是为了那个——没有人想来这么一大块儿空地上散步。更何况这里也没有飞盘。\
**Medicine Pocket**: If it weren't for that, no one would've taken a walk on this ridiculously vast land, no one! Besides, there is no Frisbee here.

**可燃点**：翻滚鳄？翻滚……啊！我在晨跑训练时会路过那间店！\
**Spathodea**: The Rolling Croc? Rolling ... Oh! I pass by that store every morning when I exercise!

**可燃点**：从这里向前走，绕过一家橘色招牌的咖啡馆，从右侧巷子进去就能找到它了！但得注意低头，那儿的招牌可容易撞到人的脑袋了——\
**Spathodea**: Go straight ahead, turn right into the lane after passing by a cafe with an orange signboard, and there it is! But do keep your heads down, or you'll be hit by the signboards there.

**可燃点**：如果你们担心的话，我可以带着你们……啊！不好！\
**Spathodea**: I can take you there if you need ... Oh, shoot!

“滴。滴滴。”\
Beep. Beep beep.

**可燃点**：我的热身时间快结束了！我得走啦，我的教练还等着我做挥拳训练呢——抱歉了，希望你们一切顺利！\
**Spathodea**: Warm-up time is almost over. I have to go! My coach is waiting for me for the punching exercise. Sorry guys, hope you find the store!

**维尔汀**：谢谢你……嗯？\
**Vertin**: Thank you. Hmm?

**沙丝绒**：让开！让开！让出一条路来——！\
**Desert Flannel**: Make way! Make way! Move aside!

**可燃点**：不用谢，只是一点儿小忙！\
**Spathodea**: It's okay. Don't mention it!

那模糊的声音逼近的同时，面前的年轻姑娘留下一声清脆的回答，继续踏上训练的路途。\
The girl is setting out again. Her crisp voice overlaps the approaching shouting.

**维尔汀**：等等！\
**Vertin**: Wait!

**维尔汀**：拐角后面好像有个人——小心别撞——\
**Vertin**: Someone's at the corner! Watch ...

**沙丝绒**：呃啊啊——！\
**Desert Flannel**: Errrahh!

**可燃点**：救、救命啊……！呜哇！\
**Spathodea**: H-Help! Urgh! Ugh ….

**维尔汀**：唔……\
**Vertin**: Ugh ...

**可燃点**：……火？着……火了……\
**Spathodea**: ... Fire? I'm ... on fire ...

**维尔汀**：意识不清，生命体征微弱……我们得把人带回拉普拉斯去。\
**Vertin**: Confusion and weak pulse ... We have to take her to Laplace.

**可燃点**：我——呜……呃……\
**Spathodea**: I ... Mmm ... Uhh ...

**可燃点**：我、我没事儿……！我不会有事儿的——\
**Spathodea**: I-I'm fine! I'm always fine.

**可燃点**：呼……哈……\
**Spathodea**: *deep breath*

辗转反侧。\
Tossing and turning.

**可燃点**：我……到底是怎么了呀……难道我真的撞坏了身上的什么地方吗？\
**Spathodea**: What happened to me? Did I really break some part of myself?

**可燃点**：虽然他们说我晕倒了，可我一点儿感觉都没有呀……除开衣服弄脏了之外，浑身上下也没有一个地方是痛的……\
**Spathodea**: They said I passed out, but it doesn't feel like that to me. My vest is dusted, but I don't feel any pain at all.

一遍又一遍，年轻的小姑娘把床单搅得像一团皱褶的纸巾。\
She tosses around in bed, crumpling the bed sheet like wadded-up tissues.

**可燃点**：或许我需要更多冰水？\
**Spathodea**: Maybe I need more ice water?

她灌下几口冰水。\
She gulps down some cold water.

**可燃点**：呜——不对，或许我需要一些热茶……\
**Spathodea**: Mmm. No, maybe it's hot tea that I need.

她又啜饮了几口烧得翻滚的红茶。\
And takes a sip of boiling hot black tea.

**可燃点**：呃……真讨厌，这一点儿用也没有！\
**Spathodea**: Uh ... Shoot, it's not working at all!

**可燃点**：早知道我就该和那些奇怪的人一起去什么“拉普拉师”检查一下身体，我记得他们给我的名片还在……不，不对！\
**Spathodea**: I should have gone to that "Lap-lettuce" with those wacky people and had a physical examination. Let me see, their card is in ... Wait, no!

**可燃点**：我都那样拒绝过了，如果这时候去找他们……呃呜……这太丢人了。\
**Spathodea**: I've turned them down. If I go back to them, ugh, that will be super embarrassing!

**可燃点**：而且——我撞到的是头，现在不舒服的却是胃，这一定只是……巧合而已。\
**Spathodea**: Besides, I bumped my head on the ground, but it's my stomach that is feeling sick now. I'm sure this is just a coincidence.

**可燃点**：我——我很少吃垃圾食品，也一直不懈怠校队的训练，我了解我的身体，它健康！而且强韧！\
**Spathodea**: I-I seldom have junk food, and never miss the training at school! I know my body well. It's healthy! And tough!

年轻姑娘甩了甩脑袋，自我安慰着从枕头下抽出一本相册。\
She says so to comfort herself, shaking her head and pulling out a photo album from under the pillow.

**可燃点**：我已经吃了胃药了，只要休息一会儿，转移开我的注意力……\
**Spathodea**: I already took the medicine for stomach pain. Now just take a break and distract myself from it.

硬纸壳向两侧摊开，有风从其中吹出。\
The moment she opens the album, a breeze blows out from it.

**可燃点**：……呼，泥土与矿物的味道，还有炭火与金蒲桃的味道。\
**Spathodea**: *deep breath* The smell of soil, mineral, burning coal, and the golden penda.

**可燃点**：总感觉闻到这股味道，就已经好受多了。\
**Spathodea**: That already makes me feel much better.

每个人都有自己的放松方式。可燃点也是。\
Everyone has their own way to chill out, so does Spathodea.

她吮吸着相册中的微风，手指顺着相片的边缘抚摸。里头乘着扫帚飞在空中的神秘学家面颊绯红，正为自己的胜利高声欢呼。\
She eagerly draws in the breeze, running her finger along the edge of the photos. In one of the photos, an arcanist with rosy cheeks is flying on a broom, cheering for her victory.

**可燃点**：这是……我的第一张收藏。妈妈在我五岁生日时送给我的。\
**Spathodea**: This is the first photo in my collection. Mom gave it to me for my fifth birthday.

**可燃点**：1884年的神秘学家中正流行越树跳高，那是所有乌卢鲁运动会中树木最多的一场。\
**Spathodea**: In 1884, Branch Vault was very popular among arcanists. The Uluru Games that year had more trees than that in any other years.

**可燃点**：然后是1900年，圣洛夫基金会接手了乌卢鲁运动会。\
**Spathodea**: Then in 1900, St. Pavlov Foundation took over the Uluru Games.

**可燃点**：为了安全考虑，他们停止了三分之一的危险运动，并为留存的项目增添了许多规范。琼斯在这场比赛上拿下了第一名。\
**Spathodea**: Out of security concerns, they abolished one third of the events that involved dangerous actions and imposed a lot of regulations on the rest. Jones got first place in the game that year.

**可燃点**：然后是……1938年，圣洛夫基金会接手后最成功的一届“乌卢鲁运动会”。\
**Spathodea**: Then, the Games in 1938. It was the most successful one ever since the Foundation took over.

**可燃点**：几乎所有人都以为它将被复兴，重新回到大家眼前，直到……\
**Spathodea**: It was so successful almost everyone thought the Games would be revived and brought back to the public, until ...

可燃点小声地叹息一声，不厚的相册已翻到了最底页。\
A slight sigh escapes her mouth. Now, she is looking at the last page of the thin album.

**可燃点**：哪怕只去一分钟也行，我也想亲眼看看乌卢鲁运动场。\
**Spathodea**: I wish I could see the Uluru Stadium with my own eyes again, even for just a minute.

**可燃点**：就像……就像……就像我从前在里头主持开幕式时一样。\
**Spathodea**: Like ... like how I used to host the opening ceremonies in there.

**可燃点**：那时候，我站在最高的高台上，用香膏浸染炙热的火焰，坐在红木树枝上推行木舟。\
**Spathodea**: Back then, I stood on the highest platform, igniting a flame from the wood saturated by ointment, and then flew on a rosewood branch, following a canoe in water and gently pushing it forward.

**可燃点**：而火焰与我争辩，我愤怒得浑身发抖，因为……因为她不讲道理，是一个讨厌鬼，紧接着，我的眼前只剩下漆黑——\
**Spathodea**: But the flame had a fight with me. I trembled with anger because ... she was such an unreasonable blockhead. Then, my sight was filled with darkness.

**可燃点**：我？\
**Spathodea**: My sight?

**可燃点**：……我？！\
**Spathodea**: MY SIGHT?!

可燃点不自觉地挠了挠胸口，紧接着是喉咙。\
Spathodea unconsciously scratches her chest, and then her throat.

**可燃点**：我刚刚说了什么？那些东西怎么在我脑袋里——那是？幻想吗？\
**Spathodea**: Did I just say something? What are these things doing in my head? Are they illusions?

**可燃点**：我什么时候去过沙漠了？什么时候又——呜——咳咳咳……\
**Spathodea**: When did I go to the desert? Since when did I ... ugh ... *coughs*

一股瘙痒带着热度，从胃里爬上胸腔，正挤入喉管。\
A warm touch of itch climbs up from her stomach to her chest, squeezing itself out of her windpipe.

就像是一只毛茸茸的鸟，正扑腾着被打湿的羽毛，拼了命地想从她身体中钻出来。\
Like a bird fluffing its damp feathers, struggling its way out from her body.

**可燃点**：嗯……是药起作用了吗？感觉胃里已经好受多了，只是喉咙，好像……又烫又痒……\
**Spathodea**: Mmm. Is the medicine working? My stomach is much better now, but my throat ... It's, burning and itchy.

**可燃点**：呃——咳咳，呼——哈——\
**Spathodea**: *retches* ... *coughs and gasps*

**可燃点**：咳咳——呃，呜呜……咔——！\
**Spathodea**: *coughs* ... Ughhh ...

**可燃点**：哇呕——\
**Spathodea**: *vomits*

**可燃点**：我……我妈妈……\
**Spathodea**: M-Mom ...

**可燃点**：可从来都没和我说过……我我我们家有喷火红龙的血统呀……\
**Spathodea**: M-M-Mom never told me ... w-w-we are descendants of the Red Dragon ...

**可燃点**：不——不、不不不……我现在就得去看医生！\
**Spathodea**: No ... No no no no! I need to see the doctor right now!

## RUG-02 邻人友爱 / The Lovely Neighbor

**维尔汀**：让我们梳理一下现在的情况。\
**Vertin**: Now, let's summarize what happened.

**维尔汀**：你在昨日因磕碰晕厥16分30秒，而后苏醒，身体并无不适。\
**Vertin**: You fell into a coma for 16 minutes and 30 seconds yesterday due to external impact. Then you woke up and found yourself fine.

**可燃点**：没错。\
**Spathodea**: That's right.

**维尔汀**：当天夜里，你感到“异样的灼烧感”从胃部延伸到食道与喉咙，脑中出现了奇怪的幻想……\
**Vertin**: On that night, you felt an "unusual burn" coming up to your throat from your stomach. At the same time, you had weird illusions ...

**维尔汀**：……最终吐出了，一团火。\
**Vertin**: ... And at last, you vomited, a ball of fire.

**可燃点**：没错——没有错，就是这样！\
**Spathodea**: Yes, that's right, exactly!

**维尔汀**：最后一点……\
**Vertin**: For one last time ...

**维尔汀**：你确定你的家庭中并没有携带喷火红龙血统的亲族吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you sure no one in your family is related to the Red Dragon?

**可燃点**：千真万确，我翻遍了所有的家庭合照和病历本！还和我爸爸妈妈通了电话——他们都说没有过！\
**Spathodea**: One hundred percent positive! I checked all the family photos and medical records, and even rang Mom and Dad! They denied every possibility of it!

**维尔汀**：这是一种相当罕见的状况。\
**Vertin**: This symptom is really rare to see.

**可燃点**：对呀！所以你们……你们可别不管我呀……！\
**Spathodea**: I know! So, don't walk away on me!

可燃点左右两手分别攥着一只手腕，将在场的三人连成了一条泳池内的漂浮球线。\
Each of her hands clenches one wrist from the other two, joining them together like a floating buoy line in a swimming pool.

**沙丝绒**：你相信了？\
**Desert Flannel**: Are you really buying that?

**维尔汀**：我不怀疑她。\
**Vertin**: I don't doubt it.

**沙丝绒**：那你可真是个天杀的傻帽。你在街上多走两圈，恐怕连衣服帽子都会给人骗得精光。\
**Desert Flannel**: Then you're a f**king doughnut. Would have lost all your clothes to any rorter that comes up to you if you wandered long enough on the streets.

**沙丝绒**：还有你——我警告你，把你这力大无穷的小爪子松开！现在就放我走！\
**Desert Flannel**: And you—I'm warning you—take your little claws off me! Let me go NOW!

**可燃点**：嘿！是你忽然冲出来撞倒了我，现在我的脑袋坏了——你也有责任！\
**Spathodea**: Hey! You were the one who burst out of nowhere and knocked me over! Now my brain is not working right, and you are responsible for it!

**沙丝绒**：得了吧，这就是一团“不灭的火”而已！神秘学家谁没见过这样的小把戏，随便找个工坊不出两天就能做出二十团！想骗我，你还早了一百年呢！\
**Desert Flannel**: Yeah? You mean this smidge of zombie fire? You reckon this is the first time an arcanist sees it? Can get you twenty of these in two days in any workshop! You gotta try harder if you wanna fool me!

**可燃点**：哇啊？！我没骗人！那团火就是我吐出来的！\
**Spathodea**: Whoa whoa whoa?! I'm not a liar! I saw that ball of fire come out of my mouth!

小姑娘被质疑激怒，一把将火苗塞入了口中。\
Irritated by their skepticism, she shoves the fire into her mouth.

**可燃点**：李康！它，根本不会，烧桑我——！窝才不四骗子！\
**Spathodea**: Hee? It, doen't, vurn ee, at all! I am o a iar! (See? It doesn't burn me at all! I am not a liar!)

**沙丝绒**：骗子每天都在更新自己的花招，“没有花招，没有面包”，没听说过吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: You frauds never stop coming up with new scams. "No cheat, no eat," heard that before?

**沙丝绒**：带着你的假火回家去吧，继续骗人的话，当心本耶普顺着下水道爬进你的卧室！它们最喜欢吃的就是谎言，保准会吃掉你的舌头！\
**Desert Flannel**: Go home with your fake fire. If you continue doing this, be careful of the Bunyips! They will crawl into your house through the sewage and take your tongue, because lies are their favorite food!

**维尔汀**：但是，你并没有证据证明这是一个可疑的骗局。\
**Vertin**: But there is no evidence to prove that she's telling a lie.

**沙丝绒**：证据？我有一大堆这姑娘“可疑”至极的证据了！\
**Desert Flannel**: Evidence? I have more than enough evidence to prove she's not some innocent lamb!

**沙丝绒**：她半夜爬到树上，在我的卧室窗户外大喊大叫。等我一开门，就不由分说地像拎购物袋一样把我拎到了这儿。\
**Desert Flannel**: She climbed up the tree outside my window and was shouting and screaming there in the middle of the night. The moment I went outside, she took me here like she was carrying a bag of groceries.

**维尔汀**：……忽然吐出火焰，会令人受到惊吓，从而……做出一些异常的举动。\
**Vertin**: ... One may infer that she was shocked by the fire-vomiting and thus ... displayed abnormal behaviors.

**沙丝绒**：天啊……你爸爸妈妈没教过你吗？！\
面对深夜出现的陌生人——我们永远得保持最高的警惕！\
**Desert Flannel**: My God! Don't you have adults at home to put some senses in your head?!\
Haven't they taught you not to trust the strangers' words, especially if they show up at late hours?!

**可燃点**：——陌，陌生人？！\
**Spathodea**: S-Stranger?!

**可燃点**：虽然我撞坏了脑袋，甚至有点记不清自己到底是谁了——但是你也不该忘记我呀！\
**Spathodea**: I know something's wrong with my head, and I'm not even sure who I really am anymore, but you shouldn't have forgotten me!

**可燃点**：我们是邻居！沙丝绒！我就住在三条街之外，还和你打过招呼呢……！\
**Spathodea**: We're neighbors, Desert Flannel! I live three streets away. I even said hello to you!

**沙丝绒**：三条街？你管那叫“邻居”？\
**Desert Flannel**: Three streets away? How does it make us "neighbors"?

**沙丝绒**：我可不觉得满街垃圾的地方和修着白色喷泉与小花园的漂亮街区是邻居，也不记得我有个富有而悠闲的移民家庭。\
**Desert Flannel**: And I don't think our litter-covered street is a part of your fancy community, where people sit by the white fountains and walk in the street gardens. The last time I checked, I was not from some rich immigrant family.

**沙丝绒**：我不管你是为了零花钱还是刺激，如果我这个月还交不上房租，就要滚出去盖着报纸睡觉了！快——放我——走！\
**Desert Flannel**: No matter what you're looking for, for money or for fun, I couldn't care less about it. The only thing I care about is my landlord will kick me out if I fail to pay my rent this month! So, let, me, go!

沙丝绒扭动着身体，强行拔出手臂，扭头便跑。\
Desert Flannel struggles, pulls her arm out of the grip, and storms off.

**可燃点**：啊！你不能走！\
**Spathodea**: No! You must not leave!

可燃点从沙发上跃起，抓住沙丝绒后领的衣服，重心一歪，向后倒去。\
Spathodea jumps up from the sofa and grabs Desert Flannel's collar roll, but loses her balance.

三点一线聚拢，稀里糊涂地撞成一团。\
Like toppling dominoes, the three of them fall over each other and tumble down on the ground.

**维尔汀**：……唔！\
**Vertin**: ... Uh ...

**沙丝绒**：嘶……我想我好像撞到你的牙齿了……\
**Desert Flannel**: Ah! Hiss ... I think I just nicked you in the teeth ...

**可燃点**：你不能走！至少——至少在搞清楚我到底怎么了之前，你不能走！\
**Spathodea**: You must not leave! At least not before I figure out what happened to me!

**可燃点**：我脑子里一会儿是过去，一会儿是现在，我记得我会唱歌，但我很快就忘了怎么唱——\
**Spathodea**: Things are flashing in my mind now! Sometimes the past, sometimes the present. I remember I can sing, but soon I forget how to do that.

**可燃点**：我能想起无数人在我面前屈膝跪拜，想起我在很像乌卢鲁运动场的地方奔跑，想起一丛火热的——火热的……火热的篝火？那是篝火吗？\
**Spathodea**: I remember the crowd who worshiped me on their knees, the run in somewhere like the Uluru Stadium, and something hot ... a hot bonfire? Is that a bonfire?

**可燃点**：好吧——不论那是什么！我只是个生活在世纪末的普通人，我的脑子里不应该有这些东西的呀！\
**Spathodea**: Anyway! No matter what it is, I'm just an ordinary person like anyone else living at the end of the century! These things shouldn't be in my mind!

**可燃点**：我肯定是哪儿出了问题！或许是脑袋，或许是其他地方！\
**Spathodea**: There must be something wrong with me! With my head, or other parts!

**可燃点**：我不能现在就变成一个傻瓜呀，我的锻炼计划都乱套了……呜，我在年底还有一场比赛呢……\
**Spathodea**: I can't just go nuts now! My training plan, it's-it's all ruined. *sobs* I even have a game to play at the end of the year.

**维尔汀**：先别紧张，这些症状未必会持续下去。神秘学家感受到“灵兆”并非一定是危险的表现。\
**Vertin**: Relax, the symptoms may not last. Sensing "omens" doesn't always mean danger to arcanists.

**维尔汀**：情况复杂，你需要一个更全面的体检来厘清状况。\
**Vertin**: Given the complexity of the situation, I think you need a more detailed physical examination to find the crux.

**维尔汀**：我们会帮助你，也会为你的情况负责。\
**Vertin**: We will help you and take care of you ...

**维尔汀**：直到你康复，或是完好无损为止。\
**Vertin**: Until you completely recover, or say, become completely normal again.

**可燃点**：你……呜——太好了，还有一个人是靠谱的！\
**Spathodea**: You ... *sobs* Thank goodness, at least I can count on you!

**可燃点**：我爸爸妈妈都不在家，现在只有我自己了，万一我的脑袋恶化了就完蛋啦……电视里都是那么演的！\
**Spathodea**: Both my mom and dad aren't home right now. I'm on my own. It's all over for me if the condition gets worse—at least that's how it goes on the TV.

**维尔汀**：先别往坏处想，跟我来吧。\
**Vertin**: Don't jump to the worst conclusion yet. Follow me.

**可燃点**：好，谢谢你……\
**Spathodea**: Okay. Thank you.

年轻的女孩抹了一把眼角的泪水，跟着引领向前几步，但三点一线的末尾依然停留在沙发上。\
Spathodea wipes off the tears in her eyes and keeps up with Vertin. But soon they both stop and turn back to the one still on the sofa.

**沙丝绒**：……\
**Desert Flannel**: ...

**沙丝绒**：……干嘛？为什么都看着我？\
**Desert Flannel**: What? What are you staring at?

**沙丝绒**：只是体检而已，我也要跟着去吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: She's having a body check-up. Do I have to tag along?

**可燃点**：你打算偷偷跑掉，跑去“打工”，对不对？\
**Spathodea**: You are going to sneak away for those "part-time jobs," aren't you?!

**沙丝绒**：好吧，被你猜中了——我认输。\
**Desert Flannel**: Fine, genius. You win.

极其不情愿地咕哝几声，沙丝绒跟上了前行的队伍。\
Murmuring something, Desert Flannel unwillingly follows the team.

**沙丝绒**：对了，提箱子的，你有没有什么门路，能让我在这儿工作的？这儿看起来工资真的很高……\
**Desert Flannel**: Oi, you with the suitcase. Do you know how I can get a job here? Looks like they pay their employees well.

## RUG-03 金格！金格！ / Chinga! Chinga!

**医护人员**：这是可燃点小姐的体检报告，请您过目。\
**Medical Staff**: Here is Ms. Spathodea's physical examination.

**兔毛手袋**：哦，真贴心，他们还给你准备了鼠尾草佐匹克隆贴剂。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Oh, how sweet. They even got you the Salvia Zopiclone patches.

**兔毛手袋**：当你感到“幻觉”过强，影响到睡眠的时候就用这个。\
**Medicine Pocket**: If the "illusions" get too real and you can't sleep, use them.

**可燃点**：好吧，谢谢你……\
但我得给我的教练看过之后才能确定我是否能够使用它。\
**Spathodea**: Okay, thanks.\
But I need to ask my coach if I can use it.

**兔毛手袋**：你们可以放心，它通过了坎贝尔新派的核验标准。鼠尾草、薄荷和致幻泡水很好地中和了副作用。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Don't worry. It's been approved by the Therapeutic Goods Administration of Campbell. The ingredients include salvia, mint, and a hallucination potion. They can neutralize the side effect perfectly.

研究员翻开病例，将贴剂顺着桌面滑到小姑娘面前。\
The researcher opens the girl's medical record, takes off the patch sticking to the cover, and slides it to the girl.

**兔毛手袋**：但你还是很幸运的。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Actually, you are quite the lucky one, you know.

**兔毛手袋**：从老地图上我们可以得知，你摔倒的地方曾有一段超过百节的长楼梯，多亏你生对了年代，不然你就要从上头滚下去了。\
**Medicine Pocket**: That old map shows there used to be stairs where you fell down, with over 100 steps. Thank goodness you live in the right time; otherwise, you would have tumbled all the way down there.

**兔毛手袋**：到时候——你的脑子要出什么问题，是吐水还是吐火，可就没人知……嗯？\
**Medicine Pocket**: In that case, no one can tell what you would vomit, fire, or maybe something even worse. Hmm?

快活的声音如同熄灭的灯一般暂停。\
Medicine Pocket's voice dies down like a flame being blown out.

一阵沉默后，兔毛手袋利落地收起桌面上的文页，向门口走去。\
Muted for a while, Medicine Pocket briskly collects the files on the table and walks towards the door.

**兔毛手袋**：在这儿等等。我得找个人过来。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Wait here. I need to get someone.

**兔毛手袋**：虽然那是个货真价实的怪人，但这个问题给他负责更好。\
**Medicine Pocket**: A weirdo for sure, yet the best person we can turn to for this problem.

**可燃点**：……？\
**Spathodea**: ...?

**沙丝绒**：好吧……我发誓这是我从医生嘴里听到的最令人不安的话。\
**Desert Flannel**: Aaaaalright. I think that's the last thing I'd like to hear from a doctor.

**沙丝绒**：但是你必须得松松手，小姑娘，不然我的手就要缺血坏死了。\
**Desert Flannel**: Would you just let go of my hand, sheila? Or the good doctor here will have to cut this hand off later because of necrosis.

**可燃点**：好，好吧……！但你能让我再牵一会儿吗？我有点紧张……\
**Spathodea**: I-I will! But can I hold it for another five minutes, please? I'm sort of nervous.

焦急的时间总是度过得很慢。\
Time spent in anxiety feels like a year.

**可燃点**：……呼，哈……呼，哈……\
**Spathodea**: *deep breath*

**沙丝绒**：没错，深呼吸，深呼吸，然后松开点儿手，我也是个有血有肉的人……亲爱的。\
**Desert Flannel**: That's right, breathe in, breathe out. Then unbend the fingers. I'm also human, I feel pain too, sweetheart.

门外的走廊中，备受期待的脚步声逐渐清晰。\
The footsteps of the mysterious guest coming from the hallway are getting closer and closer.

**？？？**：难得的一例，学界已经数十年未曾见过鲜活的样本了！\
**???**: I can't believe how lucky I am. We haven't seen a living case for decades!

**？？？**：这真是太令人兴奋了，谢谢你通知我过来，兔毛手袋。\
**???**: This is exciting. Thank you for letting me know about this, Medicine Pocket.

**兔毛手袋**：别和我客气，爱兹拉，我的朋友。我不会忘记你那些奇怪的小蘑菇，但下次递交给我的时候，最好能绕过拉普拉斯的记录……\
**Medicine Pocket**: Not at all, Ezra, my dear friend. See, I always keep you and your weird little mushrooms at the back of my mind, so it'd be best if you could give them to me without leaving any records in Laplace's system next time.

**兔毛手袋**：算了——这个我们以后再详谈。去看看她吧，她会对你的神秘学论文很有帮助的。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Anyway, we can talk about that later. Now, go check out the girl. She might be very useful for your paper on arcanum.

**爱兹拉**：好的，我这就去。多谢你的贴心，我简直要等不及了。\
**Ezra**: Of course, I'll tend to her in a moment. I just want to tell you how much I appreciate your thoughtfulness. I've been waiting for this for too long.

爱兹拉调转方向，直冲着可燃点而来。\
Ezra turns directly to Spathodea.

**可燃点**：什么？\
**Spathodea**: What?

年轻的脸上带着笑容，步速不快也不慢，稳定得像一艘小舟。\
The young researcher walks to her, as steady as a boat floating on the water, smiling.

**可燃点**：……我？你们说我吗？\
**Spathodea**: Me? You mean, me?

**爱兹拉**：当然。可燃点小姐，我就是为你而来的。\
**Ezra**: Certainly, Ms. Spathodea. I came for you.

**爱兹拉**：我已经看过了你的病例与火焰成分化验清单，对火种内部的温度、燃材与你近期的体征表现都有了解。这是我为你草拟的记录清单，请看。\
**Ezra**: I've been briefed on your case and had a basic understanding of the inner flame temperature and the fuel through the laboratory report. Here is a list summarizing all the conditions. It's still a draft, but please take a look.

一张墨迹还未干的清单，密密写着无数记录事项。\
She sees a list with dense writing in ink that has barely dried.

**爱兹拉**：鉴于你当前的表现状况较为稳定，且仍处于生长发育期，我推荐你使用更温和，也更富有香气的方法进行测验。\
**Ezra**: Since your condition has stabilized and, as a teenager, you're still in a developmental stage, I'd recommend you to run a test which is more friendly and pleasant to your nose.

爱兹拉从背后巨大的怪包掏出了一只双头金属叉与一块白色的棉质物，小心翼翼地翻开，摊在手心。\
Ezra grabs a Y-shaped metal rod and a piece of cotton-like material and holds them in his palm.

**爱兹拉**：来。请对着这寻水杖眨眼三次，而后在这里尽可能轻地吹一口气。\
**Ezra**: Now, please blink three times at this dowsing rod and blow on it as lightly as possible.

**可燃点**：这，这是什么东西？\
**Spathodea**: Wh-What's this?

**爱兹拉**：哦，不……不是这样，你需要轻一些……小声一些，不要吹散这片滤网上的孢子。\
**Ezra**: Oooh, no, not like that. Just be gentle with it. Lower your voice so that you don't blow away the spores on the filter.

白色的滤网与温柔的引导几乎贴到鼻尖儿上，令人难以拒绝。\
The white filter paper almost touches the tip of her nose. She can't say no to such a gentle and soft request like that.

于是可燃点闭起眼睛，压低又压低了声音，自言自语地重复着。\
So she closes her eyes, lowers and lowers her voice, and repeats the instruction to herself.

**可燃点**：好，好吧……\
先眨三下眼睛……然后，吹气……呼——\
**Spathodea**: O-Okay.\
Blink three times ... and blow ... phew ...

滤网上泛着荧光的孢子迅速卷曲起来，变成了喜人的赭红色。\
The fluorescent spores on the filter paper curl immediately and turn a cheery ember color.

**爱兹拉**：然后把它卷起来，固定在寻水杖上……好了，我们只要再等一段时间就好。\
**Ezra**: And we're going to roll it up and fix it on the dowsing rod. Now, time will do its magic.

**可燃点**：医生，我的脑袋还有救吗？嗯？我好像……闻到了一股蘑菇的气味儿……？\
**Spathodea**: Doctor, is there a cure for my head? Wait, is that the smell of mushroom?

**爱兹拉**：这的确是蘑菇的一部分，但我并不是一位医生。\
**Ezra**: It is related to mushrooms, and I'm not a doctor.

**爱兹拉**：抱歉，可燃点小姐。我实在是太高兴了，忘记了自我介绍——\
**Ezra**: Please forgive me, Ms. Spathodea. I was so overjoyed. I forgot to introduce myself.

**爱兹拉**：你好，我是爱兹拉。\
**Ezra**: Hello, I'm Ezra.

**爱兹拉**：拉普拉斯澳大利亚分部所属的人类研究员，主要负责的方向为本地蘑菇与真菌的多样性研究。很高兴认识你。\
**Ezra**: I'm a human researcher at Laplace Australia Branch. My research is mostly on the diversity of local mushrooms and fungi. I'm very thrilled to meet you.

**可燃点**：你不是医生？你只是一个研究员……还是人类研究员？\
**Spathodea**: You are not a doctor? Just a researcher and a human?

**可燃点**：研究的方向是……蘑菇？\
**Spathodea**: And you are working on mushrooms?

**爱兹拉**：没错。虽然很遗憾我没能成为神秘学研究组的一员，但我也很喜欢蘑菇。我很喜欢我的工作。\
**Ezra**: That's right. It's a shame that I didn't become a member of the Arcane Study team, but I'm equally interested in mushrooms. I enjoy this job.

可燃点捧着自己苍白的脸，不敢置信地后退了两步。\
Spathodea turns pale holding her face, and steps back in horrified disbelief.

**可燃点**：那——那他们让你来给我看病，就……就代表着……\
**Spathodea**: So, they get you here to treat me, which means ...

**可燃点**：我没有喷火红龙的血统，但是我有……蘑菇的血统？我是一个喷火的蘑菇人？！\
**Spathodea**: I am not a descendant of the Red Dragon, but that of mushrooms? I-I'm a fire-breathing mushroom girl?!

**爱兹拉**：不——我并不是来为你看病的，可燃点小姐。\
**Ezra**: No, I'm not here to diagnose your abnormality, Ms. Spathodea.

**爱兹拉**：你的身体非常健康，脑部CT显示正常，身体强而有力。严格来说，你几乎是我见过最健康的人。\
**Ezra**: You're perfectly healthy. Your brain CT result looks normal, and I can see you're in good shape. In a stricter medical sense, you're almost one of the healthiest people I've ever seen.

**沙丝绒**：哈！看起来这儿还是有明白人的！\
**Desert Flannel**: Ha! Finally, someone has a sharp eye!

**沙丝绒**：既然小骗子已经被拆穿了，没有什么幻觉，也没什么奇怪的、难以理喻的喷火怪谈……\
**Desert Flannel**: So the truth has been unraveled—there has never been any illusions, nor is anybody putting on some strange, absurd fire-spitting show, and …

**爱兹拉**：不，她从未有过欺瞒。请看这里。\
**Ezra**: But she did not lie. Please take a look at this.

**爱兹拉**：分析显示，这团火焰核心的黑曜石碎片平均地分为二十二层。\
**Ezra**: According to the analysis, the core of her fire consists of an obsidian gravel that has 22 evenly distributed layers.

**爱兹拉**：这样的结构并非现代所有，而是来自数千年前的远古时代。\
**Ezra**: This is no modern thing. It's old, dating back thousands of years.

**沙丝绒**：你……这是什么意思？你到底是站在哪一边的？\
**Desert Flannel**: What ... what do you mean? Whose side you're on?

**爱兹拉**：嗯……这让你难以理解吗？\
**Ezra**: Emm. Have I made it difficult for you to understand?

**爱兹拉**：耳听为虚，眼见为实。请给我五分钟的时间。\
**Ezra**: Well, you'll know when you see it. Please bear with me for five minutes.

手持金属叉，拨弄按钮，身体背后的工具包内繁密的苔藓呼吸耸动起来，一阵潮湿的雾气从其中流淌而出。\
Holding the metal rod, Ezra switches the buttons on the machine. The moss in the backpack exhales, letting out a cloud of mist.

**爱兹拉**：各位听说过“轮回者”吗？\
**Ezra**: Have you heard of the "reincarnators"?

爱兹拉揭开棉网，手持金属叉分支的两端。\
Ezra unfolds the filter paper and holds the two ends of the rod.

**爱兹拉**：一种罕见的神秘学家血脉，由于触发方式、触发时间与触发的几率充满了随机性，从而极少被发现和观测。\
**Ezra**: It's one of the arcanist's lineages, a rare kind. Since this power can only be randomly triggered, and its manifestation could happen anywhere, anytime, and in any fashion, it is hard to identify them when there is one.

**爱兹拉**：其中最广为世人所知的案例为居住在伦敦的多萝西。\
**Ezra**: The most well-known case must be Dorothy of London.

**爱兹拉**：她由自家楼梯跌下，失去呼吸、心跳和一切已知的生命体征，而后她又一次醒来，变成了古埃及的本特莉施提。\
**Ezra**: She fell down the stairs in her own house and lost every vital sign. But she woke again and became the ancient Egyptian Bentreshyt.

**沙丝绒**：你——你该不是想说……\
**Desert Flannel**: You ... you are not saying that she's ...

**爱兹拉**：可燃点小姐是一名“轮回者”。\
**Ezra**: Ms. Spathodea is a "reincarnator."

**爱兹拉**：而那些所谓的幻觉并不是脑部损伤，而是真实发生过的，属于她的过去。\
**Ezra**: Those so-called illusions are not the result of any brain damage, they were once real. It's her past.

**爱兹拉**：根据过往的经验来看，她会经历一些混乱，一段或长或短的犹豫期，最终彻底地成为她——过去的她。\
**Ezra**: Based on the past cases, she'll go through a period of mental turmoil. That could be short or longer than anyone could expect, but eventually, she will become herself again—the old self.

**沙丝绒**：怎么可能？人人都知道的，“轮回者”只是报纸上一个哗众取宠的骗局——\
**Desert Flannel**: But how is that possible? Everybody knows that the "reincarnators" are just some lousy, made-up tabloid stories.

**爱兹拉**：没错。一场作秀，这正是当下主流对“轮回者”所下的结论。\
**Ezra**: That's right. Sensationalism—that's the mainstream opinion about the "reincarnators."

**爱兹拉**：多萝西的埃及语学习经历和考古学者身份让她的血统众说纷纭，而公众也多年未见到过另一位“轮回者”，这是相当合理的导向。\
**Ezra**: In Dorothy's case, her experience of learning Egyptian and her career as an archaeologist also caused controversies over her true lineage, which is understandable since people haven't seen any "reincarnator" in years.

**爱兹拉**：但在20世纪初，多萝西由那命运般的长楼梯坠下的同时……拉普拉斯科算中心于澳大利亚成立研究分部，展开了关于本地生物菌群的调查计划。\
**Ezra**: But at the beginning of the 20th century, when Dorothy fell down the stairs which decided her fate, Laplace Scientific Computing Center established its Australia Branch, carrying out studies of local fungi.

**爱兹拉**：另一条全新的通路，如澳大利亚蜜环菌的菌落般在人们看不到的土壤之下悄悄开展。\
**Ezra**: The fungi study is a brand new direction, and it has been secretly developing next to the public since, like the Australian honey fungus, growing without getting anyone's attention.

**爱兹拉**：事实胜于雄辩，请让我证明给你看。\
**Ezra**: The facts will speak for themselves. Please allow me to prove it to you.

**爱兹拉**：兔毛手袋，请帮我关一下灯。\
**Ezra**: Medicine Pocket, could you please turn off the light for us?

**爱兹拉**：谢谢你。\
**Ezra**: Cheers.

昏暗的房间中，金属叉伸出的长杆微微颤动，如同悬停的小蜂。\
The poles of that metal fork sway in the dark room, letting out a buzzing sound like a bee floating in the air.

**爱兹拉**：当我们讨论轮回时，实际上我们想要讨论的往往是“灵魂”是否存在。\
**Ezra**: When we talk about reincarnation, the real question behind it is whether the "soul" exists.

**爱兹拉**：因为只有“灵魂”才能够成为一个人的载体，当他的肉身死灭后，往复存在于这张巨大的网罗中。\
**Ezra**: Because the "soul" is commonly considered to be the essence of what makes a person who he or she is. If a person dies, his or her soul will return to the ever-circulating network.

**可燃点**：网？什么网？\
**Spathodea**: Network? What network?

**爱兹拉**：自《论作为几何学基础的假设》延伸而来的研究学说将世界比喻为一片恒定、广阔、无处可见而又无处不在的隐秘的网状物。\
**Ezra**: A theory developed from Riemann's On the Hypotheses Which Underlie Geometry described the world as an eternal, vast, invisible, yet ubiquitous net.

**维尔汀**：而“轮回者”……在新闻中被称为“人的‘灵魂’从A点下落，又毫无理由自B点出现”的奇迹。\
**Vertin**: And as the news story described, a "reincarnator" is a miracle where a "soul" disappears from point A and shows up at point B without any clear reasons.

**爱兹拉**：没错，维尔汀小姐！想不到你也对“轮回者”如此了解！\
**Ezra**: Exactly, Ms. Vertin! I'm amazed that you know so much about the "reincarnators"!

星点荧光飘浮在湿润的空气中，相互接触而后交织。\
The sparkling spores, floating in the humid air, slowly approach each other and intertwine.

**爱兹拉**：那篇报道形容“轮回者”为不可思议的、充满不确定性的，但实际上，只是我们的目光仍未走近它，观察它，难以看清其中的原理。\
**Ezra**: That report described the "reincarnators" is incomprehensible and spontaneous, but the truth is, we have never gotten close enough to observe and study them.

**可燃点**：唔……嗯？我的手指上怎么沾着发光的碎屑……\
**Spathodea**: Mmm. Hmm? What's this shiny powder on my fingers?

可燃点抬起头，看向空旷的白色屋顶，紧接着小声惊呼起来。\
Spathodea looks upwards and can't help from letting out a small cry.

**可燃点**：天啊，它就像是……我在教科书上看见的神经图……\
**Spathodea**: Gosh, it's like the neural network I read in the textbook!

**爱兹拉**：敏锐的直觉，不愧为神秘学家！菇类菌落与人脑神经的相似性正是菌菇学术界最新的研究方向，我们已在其中取得了不少进展。\
**Ezra**: You have a sharp sense. You arcanists never cease to amaze me! The latest studies have shown that the working mechanism of mushroom flora may be similar to the brain's, and we have made some progress from that.

**爱兹拉**：这正是蘑菇研究的重要性，它们帮助我们不走近，也能观察其中奥秘缘由。\
**Ezra**: This is why the study of mushrooms is important; it enriches our understanding of the "reincarnators," for they are hard to find.

**可燃点**：你的意思是，空中这些东西……是蘑菇？\
**Spathodea**: You mean, these things floating in the air are mushrooms?

**爱兹拉**：土壤之下的菌落，澳大利亚蜜环菌。\
**Ezra**: The Australian honey fungus, the mushrooms living beneath the ground.

**爱兹拉**：一种植物病原菌，可造成植物根系腐败，最早被发现于澳大利亚东南部的桉树种植园中。\
**Ezra**: It's a pathogenic gem that causes the roots to rot. It was first discovered in a Eucalyptus plantation in southeastern Australia.

**爱兹拉**：1970年代末，拉普拉斯研究员介入环境维护，发现其并非通过孢子传播，而是潜藏于泥土之下的根系中，以菌丝遍布森林。\
**Ezra**: At the end of the 1970s, Laplace researchers who intervened in the local environment protection found that, unlike other fungi which reproduce through the spreading of spores, the honey fungi spread by the growth of their underground mycelia all over the forest.

**维尔汀**：你认为它如同那张“隐秘的网”？\
**Vertin**: You think it's like that "invisible net"?

**爱兹拉**：是的。隐没于土壤之下，从A点下落，又毫无理由自B点出现的奇迹。蜜环菌完整地符合了“轮回者”的需求。\
**Ezra**: Yes. A net hiding underground, in which you see an object disappear at point A and magically emerge again at point B. The "reincarnators" are very similar to Australian honey fungus in this aspect.

**爱兹拉**：而可燃点小姐所呼出的气息、少量的唾液搭配以寻水杖，便可以描绘出属于她的网，与她在其中的行进路径。\
**Ezra**: And with her breath, a small amount of her saliva, and the dowsing rod, we will be able to find her net and map her movements on it.

**爱兹拉**：再之后，她专注的凝视点燃了引路者巢状类脐菇……\
**Ezra**: And when her gaze emblazes the Omphalotus nidiformis ...

**沙丝绒**：巢……巢什么？这不是幽灵蘑菇吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Ompha ... Omphalotus what? Isn't that the ghost fungus?

**爱兹拉**：没错，就是幽灵蘑菇。它挥发着荧光，在夜中闪烁。\
**Ezra**: Yes, the ghost fungus. The mushrooms that glow in the dark.

**爱兹拉**：在更古老的历史中它也被称为“金格”，意为精神与灵魂，即人脑中闪烁的神智之火光。\
**Ezra**: They're called Chinga in older times, which means spirit and soul, the sparkle of ideas in human minds.

**维尔汀**：蘑菇模拟出了属于可燃点的“网”，那这两个光点就是……\
**Vertin**: If the mushroom has simulated Spathodea's "net," then these two light spots are ...

**爱兹拉**：距离我们更近的这颗来自于现在的可燃点小姐，而更远、更明亮、更深的那一颗，造成了她当下的症状。\
**Ezra**: The one closer to us represents the current Ms. Spathodea, and the farther and brighter one is what put her through the changes now.

**可燃点**：也就是说，那是过去的我……？\
**Spathodea**: So, that's me in the past?

**可燃点**：而，而我……会渐渐地变成……她？\
**Spathodea**: And I-I will gradually turn into her?

灯光重新亮起。诊疗室内的通风系统连续发出了两次提示音，荧光与湿气一同被抽入了漆黑的方框。\
The light is back in the room. The ventilator emitting two consecutive notifications as it extracts the sparkling lights out together with the heavy moisture in the air.

**爱兹拉**：五分钟到了，我的时间恰巧足够。\
**Ezra**: Five minutes, we are right on time.

**爱兹拉**：沙丝绒小姐，请问你感觉……\
**Ezra**: Ms. Desert Flannel, how do you feel ...

**沙丝绒**：该死，如果她摔出了这么严重的问题，我得赔多少钱啊……难道我后半辈子都要这么过了吗？！\
**Desert Flannel**: D**n it! If she's so badly injured, how much would the compensation be? Is this how my life will be? Being heavily in debt?

**爱兹拉**：沙丝绒小姐？你正在啃指甲，那会让你受伤的，请停下来。\
**Ezra**: Ms. Desert Flannel, you're nibbling at your nails. You will get hurt from it, please stop.

**沙丝绒**：我？我没事儿，你——你叫我有什么事儿吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Me? I'm fine. You ... are you talking to me? You were saying ...?

**爱兹拉**：是的。我想请问你感觉如何？我的讲述方式清晰吗？\
**Ezra**: Yes. I was asking how you are doing. Did you get my drift?

**沙丝绒**：我……我觉得……\
**Desert Flannel**: I ... I think ...

**沙丝绒**：虽然我们都知道这家伙家里从没抱过一颗龙蛋，但有没有可能是蜥蜴呢？某种远古蜥蜴——反正！反正不会是“轮回者”！\
**Desert Flannel**: Well, I know it's highly unlikely that this little girl was hatched from a dragon's egg, but is it possible that she's just some kind of uncommon lizard? You know, the really ancient ones? Any, anything but a "reincarnator"!

**爱兹拉**：可……这些论证是毫无道理的……\
**Ezra**: But ... but what you said doesn't make sense ...

**沙丝绒**：什么是毫无道理？这家伙嘴里吐出了一团火！\
**Desert Flannel**: What do you mean "it doesn't make sense"? There was fire coming out of her mouth!

沙丝绒指着被放置在沙发上的火苗，把自己手中电子宠物的机器晃了又晃。\
Desert Flannel points at the fire "placed" on the couch, which is still burning, and shakes her digital pet machine.

**沙丝绒**：而我现在唯一的家人是只像素组成的鸸鹋——这世界没什么不可能的！\
**Desert Flannel**: And my only family here is a pixel emu. Does it make sense to you?

**爱兹拉**：我……我已经开始听不明白你的话了……\
**Ezra**: I don't follow ...

**爱兹拉**：我明白这不是你的错，是神秘学家的天性造成了你更容易受情绪控制，引发癔症和幻觉的问题……\
**Ezra**: I know this is not your fault. It's just your arcanist nature taking over. It's very normal if you got too carried away by your emotions and became delusional and hysterical.

**爱兹拉**：请拉住我的手，我学习过如何安抚神秘学家的课程，跟着我一起深呼吸，请吸气——呼气——\
**Ezra**: Please take my hand. I was once trained to help arcanists calm down. Now breathe with me, in ... and out ...

**沙丝绒**：我？我才没有癔症！\
**Desert Flannel**: Me? I'm not hysterical!

备受冒犯的人。\
Said the hysterical girl with offense.

**可燃点**：嘿！你又懂什么神秘学家了！你甚至都不是一个神秘学家！\
**Spathodea**: Hey, what do you know about arcanists? You're not even one of us!

拍案而起的围观者。\
Said the outraged bystander.

白房间内，吵嚷声如同雪团般越滚越大，掩盖下了那股尚不明晰的焦糊味。\
In the white room, the argument snowballs tumbling out of control, letting a wisp of smoke slither across the room unnoticed.

**维尔汀**：各位……\
**Vertin**: Everyone ...

**爱兹拉**：请相信我并无恶意，可燃点小姐。我只是想帮助你们。\
**Ezra**: Please believe me that I meant you no harm, Ms. Spathodea. I was only trying to help.

**可燃点**：帮助？什么帮助？帮助就是说别人是疯子吗？\
**Spathodea**: Help? How? By calling us delusional?

**可燃点**：我最讨厌你们这样满口说别人“过于情绪化”的人类了！\
**Spathodea**: There is nothing I hate more than humans like you saying that others are "over-emotional"!

**维尔汀**：各位。\
**Vertin**: People.

**爱兹拉**：不，不是这样的，可燃点小姐。我并非想要指责任何人，只是生物学上神秘学家更加敏感，容易被影响。\
**Ezra**: No, nothing like that. Ms. Spathodea. It is not my intention to criticize anything or anyone. It's just, biologically, arcanists tend to be more sensitive and easily affected.

**爱兹拉**：我喜欢神秘学家，就像是喜欢菌类一样，我对此有所研究……唔？\
**Ezra**: I also like arcanists, almost as much as I'm interested in mushrooms, that's why I study them ... Hmm?

**爱兹拉**：你们……有没有闻到一股烟味？\
**Ezra**: Do you smell something burning?

灼热的火焰吞没了沙发，吞没了地面，也完全吞没了外出的门户，以可怖的速度扑面而来。\
Before they realize it, the flame "placed" on the couch has already devoured its seat and the floor, spread to the door, and completely blocked their way out. The burning heat is approaching at a terrifying speed.

**可燃点**：火苗？！这是我的火苗——它，它什么时候烧得这么大了？！\
**Spathodea**: A fire?! It's the flame I spat out! Wh-When did it grow so large!?

**维尔汀**：我试图提醒过你们。\
**Vertin**: I tried to warn you.

**维尔汀**：那团火在“蜥蜴论证”中越烧越大，很快，拉普拉斯的护卫就会破门而入。\
**Vertin**: It has grown larger and larger as your "lizard hypothesis" heated up. I'm sure the guards of Laplace will break in soon.

**拉普拉斯安全员**：拉普拉斯附属医院护卫队已入场，请患者与无关人员跟随我的疏散退离危险房间！\
**Laplace Security**: Security of Laplace Research Center Hospital taking over. All patients and non-staff, please follow me to evacuate the room!

**拉普拉斯安全员**：判定为……二级火情，执行灭火处理。\
**Laplace Security**: Evaluating fire level ... Level 2. Extinguishing the fire.

**拉普拉斯安全员**：火源方向已确定，申请使用袋鼠泡沫三号灭火喷剂！\
**Laplace Security**: Source of ignition confirmed. Request for permission to use Kangaroo Foam Fire Extinguisher III!

**可燃点**：啊——等等——等一等！我们不能让火苗熄灭！\
**Spathodea**: Whoa! Wait wait wait! You can't put out my flame!

**可燃点**：这很重要，很……重要，我不知道为什么，但是我知道这很重要！那些泡沫袋鼠看见火就会逮着它揍的！这可不行呀！\
**Spathodea**: It's important for me, very, very important! I don't know why, but its importance is for sure! Those bubble kangaroos will kick its butt once they see the flames! I don't want that!

**维尔汀**：我会帮你保护它的，别担心。\
**Vertin**: I'll protect it for you. Don't worry.

**医护人员**：好了。您身上已经没有绒毛泡沫了。\
**Medical Staff**: There you go. Now you're free from the fuzzy foam.

**可燃点**：太好了，谢谢你——虽然……虽然我闻起来还是像一只小袋鼠……但现在已经好多了。\
**Spathodea**: Thank goodness, uh, I mean thank you. Though I still smell like a joey, I'm much better now.

**医护人员**：在神秘学唤起初期，神秘学家的能力失控率高达74.3%。\
**Medical Staff**: In the early stages of arcane ability awakening, the rate of arcanists losing control can reach 74.3%.

**医护人员**：但这不意味着您可以在拉普拉斯附属医院的诊疗室内纵火，并为了“保护火焰”与拉普拉斯安全员发生冲突。\
**Medical Staff**: But it doesn't mean that you can set a fire in the clinic of the Laplace Research Center Hospital, or fight the security to "protect the flame."

**可燃点**：呜……是的，对不起。我不是故意的，我也不知道为什么火苗它会忽然……忽然变得这样大，它从来都没有这样过……\
**Spathodea**: *sobs* I know. I'm sorry. I didn't mean to do this, and I have no idea why my flame grew so ... so large all of a sudden. That never happened before.

**可燃点**：当然，我应该负责看好它，早点发现它的异常。我……我当时太专注于吵架了……\
**Spathodea**: I know I should have been responsible and noticed the anomaly earlier. I-I was completely lost in the argument.

双手交叠在面前，头越埋越深，几乎快钻进地板里去。\
She buries her face in her hands and is still trying to bury it even deeper.

**医护人员**：……不幸中的万幸，由于火情尚可控制。他们使用的是袋鼠泡沫灭火剂，本次骚乱没有造成任何伤亡。\
**Medical Staff**: The silver lining is, as the fire was still under control, they used the Kangaroo Foam Fire Extinguisher, and thus it didn't cause any casualties.

**医护人员**：请把您在事发期间出现的情绪变化与肢体反应记录在这张纸上。我们会对您的身体健康进行持续的信息追踪。\
**Medical Staff**: Please write down your emotional changes and physical reactions that occurred during the incident on this sheet of paper. We'll keep tracking your physical health information.

**医护人员**：为您准备的凝神泡剂在那张小桌上，桌下的矮柜中有毛毯与Ⅱ型安全PMMA塑封盒。请将危险源封存保管。\
**Medical Staff**: The Concentration Potion is on that table, and there are blankets and Type II PMMA safety boxes in the cabinet under the table. Please keep the hazards sealed for safekeeping.

**可燃点**：好的……我明白了。\
**Spathodea**: Okay. Got it.

**医护人员**：您仍处于不稳定状态中，请在这里好好休息，不要随意走动。\
**Medical Staff**: You are still in an unstable state. Please have a rest here, and don't move around.

**医护人员**：如果有任何需求，请按下您左手边的呼唤铃，我们的护理人员会为您提供帮助。\
**Medical Staff**: If you need anything, please press the call bell on your left, and our nursing staff will come to help.

医护人员收走托盘，房间内再度归于安静。\
The medical staff collects the tray and walks out of the clinic, leaving the room in silence again.

**可燃点**：嗯……好吧，为了避免再烧坏一个房间……\
**Spathodea**: Hmm. Well, in case we burn another room ...

**可燃点**：我想她说的盒子，就在……啊，在这儿……\
**Spathodea**: The box she mentioned is ... Oh, here it is.

**火苗**：*燃烧*\
**Flame**: *burning*

打开透明盒子，可燃点靠近小小的火焰。\
She opens the transparent box and leans in towards the little flame.

**可燃点**：我知道自由是很重要的，火苗。\
**Spathodea**: I know freedom matters, little flame.

**可燃点**：但我们别无他法，对不起了，兄弟！\
**Spathodea**: But we have no choice. Sorry, buddy!

**火苗**：*燃烧*\
**Flame**: *burning*

将火焰推入盒中，她小心翼翼地调整着角度。\
She reaches out a hand to push the flame into the box with great caution.

**可燃点**：嘿，听我说，我听老师说过，火得有氧气才能燃烧，所以我会给你留一个小小的气口……\
**Spathodea**: All right, listen, my teacher said fire needs oxygen to burn, so I'll leave a small window for you to breathe.

**火苗**：……我，一直……想——\
**Flame**: I ... have ... always ... wanted ...

**火苗**：来……见你……\
**Flame**: to ... see ... you ...

**可燃点**：——嗯？！\
**Spathodea**: What?!

**火苗**：回……\
**Flame**: Go ...

**可燃点**：你……你在说话？天啊——呼唤铃，呼唤铃在哪里——\
**Spathodea**: Are-Are you talking?! Gosh! The call bell! Where's the call bell?

**火苗**：……回到……乌……\
**Flame**: Go ... back ... to ... Ulu ...

**火苗**：必须回到……乌卢鲁，运动会……\
**Flame**: We must ... go back to ... Uluru ... Games ...

**可燃点**：……！\
**Spathodea**: ...!

**可燃点**：乌卢鲁……乌卢鲁运动会？你是说——乌卢鲁运动会？！\
**Spathodea**: Uluru ... Uluru Games? You mean, the Uluru Games?

**可燃点**：说清楚点儿啊，火苗，说清楚点儿！乌卢鲁运动会它怎么了——\
**Spathodea**: Make it clear, little flame, make it clear! What's going on with the Uluru Games?

可燃点手忙脚乱地抓起火苗。\
Spathodea grabs the flame in a hurry.

星星点点的红火攀上她的手掌。\
The sparkling flame starts devouring her palm bite by bite.

**可燃点**：——哎呀！这些火……火怎么都烧到我身上了？！这和过去感觉不同，这一次，它好……烫……\
**Spathodea**: Ah! The fire ... It's burning on me?! It feels different this time. It's so hot ...

火焰的蔓延速度极快，不到片刻之间，可燃点的呼救声就消失在了赤红中。\
Far faster than expected, the flame spreads over her, and her cry for help fades into the burning red.

## RUG-04 后手直拳 / Cross

**沙丝绒**：这就是拉普拉斯科算中心处理突发事件的风格吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Is this the Laplace fashion of dealing with emergencies?

**沙丝绒**：我可以用我的人格保证——如果有任何人路过这里，哪怕是小屁孩或是流浪汉，他们的目光都能立刻杀死我的所有尊严。\
**Desert Flannel**: I swear, if anyone walks past us now, schoolers or derros, I will be instantly killed by their silent judgment.

**爱兹拉**：实际上，当患者或研究目标出现不稳定状况时，第一时间隔离引发源是正确的处理手法……\
**Ezra**: As a matter of fact, when the patient or the subject becomes unstable during contact, it is necessary to isolate them from the triggering cause immediately.

**爱兹拉**：只不过……常用的隔离室正是被我们烧毁的那一间。\
**Ezra**: But, we just burnt down the isolation room.

**爱兹拉**：……茱蒂丝护士长的愤怒是情有可原的。\
**Ezra**: No wonder Head Nurse Judith was so angry.

**袋鼠**：嘎啊！\
**Kangaroo**: URAGH!

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**爱兹拉**：维尔汀小姐，你还好吗？\
**Ezra**: Ms. Vertin, are you alright?

**爱兹拉**：那只袋鼠正在……拳击你的鼻子。\
**Ezra**: That kangaroo is ... punching your nose.

**维尔汀**：我很好。\
**Vertin**: I'm fine.

**袋鼠**：嘎啊啊啊啊！！！\
**Kangaroo**: URAGH!

**维尔汀**：……它也很好。\
**Vertin**: So is the kangaroo.

**维尔汀**：我想兔毛手袋很快会给我们送来凝神泡剂的。\
**Vertin**: I'm sure Medicine Pocket will bring us the Concentration Potion soon.

**沙丝绒**：最好如此，我们现在看起来像是袋鼠，闻起来像是袋鼠，摸起来像是袋鼠——\
**Desert Flannel**: They'd better. We look like a bunch of kangaroos, feel like kangaroos, and even smell like kangaroos!

**沙丝绒**：明天一早，《澳大利亚叮当快报》上就会写满三只袋鼠深夜徘徊于公共绿地的新闻。到时候我就会从社会意义上变成一只袋鼠。\
**Desert Flannel**: We will make tomorrow's headline of Australian Nagger and become "the three kangaroos hanging out on a public lawn at midnight." That'd be the end of our social lives as humans and the beginning of a life as kangaroos.

**爱兹拉**：上报纸？……啊，我明白了。请不要担心。\
**Ezra**: Make the headline? Aah, I see. Please don't worry.

**爱兹拉**：虽然兔毛手袋的确是报纸上的常客，但凝神泡剂并不是它的作品，而且也并没有使用任何新技术……\
**Ezra**: Although it's true that Medicine Pocket is a frequent celebrity on the news, the Concentration Potion is not their work. Besides, we didn't use anything new in its development ...

**沙丝绒**：我说的不是那家伙，是我。有记者跟着我呢。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm not worried about that guy. I was talking about myself. There are paparazzi following me around these days.

**维尔汀**：我不知道你是一个知名人物。\
**Vertin**: I didn't know you were famous.

**沙丝绒**：……我不出名，但有人打心底里想要我臭名远扬。如果你们也得罪几个八卦记者就会知道他们有多糟糕了。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm not. It's just that someone wants my name spread in a bad way. Trust me, you should never piss off the paparazzi.

**爱兹拉**：你应该寻求警察的帮助。\
**Ezra**: You should turn to the police for help.

**沙丝绒**：得了吧，有那个时间，你们还不如帮我盯着点四周。\
**Desert Flannel**: Yeah yeah, just shut up and keep your eyes peeled for anything suspicious.

**沙丝绒**：一旦发现那些个该死的跟踪狂记者，立刻就把他们的鞋子丢到电线上去……\
**Desert Flannel**: I will toss his shoes on the power lines, if I found him here.

**爱兹拉**：沙丝绒小姐，小心背后！\
**Ezra**: Ms. Desert Flannel, watch your back!

**沙丝绒**：什么，是那些家伙又来——啊，哇哇啊！好烫！\
**Desert Flannel**: What, are those paparaz- ... Aaah, waaaah! It burns!

灼热的温度让年轻姑娘从长椅上一跃而起，尖叫起来。\
The young girl leaps to her feet, letting out a scream as the bench beneath her turned scorching hot.

**爱兹拉**：这是——火？沙丝绒小姐，那里有湖水，请跳进湖水里去！\
**Ezra**: Is this ... fire? Ms. Desert Flannel, the lake is over there! Get in there!

**沙丝绒**：我——我不会游泳啊！\
**Desert Flannel**: Lake? I ... I can't swim!

**袋鼠**：嘎啊啊！啊啊啊！啊啊啊啊！\
**Kangaroo**: URAAGH!AHHH!!

场面混乱，火舌四溅。\
There are people shouting, feet running, sparks flying.

**沙丝绒**：啊——这袋鼠踩到我的眼睛了，好痛！让开，让开，我看不见湖在哪儿了！\
**Desert Flannel**: Aaah! This stupid kangaroo kicked me in the eye, ouch! Move, move! I can't see where the lake is!

**维尔汀**：等一下，别急！\
**Vertin**: Wait, calm down!

**维尔汀**：你没有危险，有危险的应该是她。\
**Vertin**: You are not in danger. She is.

**沙丝绒**：别开玩笑了！我都要烧伤了——嗯？不对，我一点儿都没烧伤……？\
**Desert Flannel**: Are you joking?! I was getting burned. Emm? There's nothing on my skin.

不速之客喘息着，真正被灼伤一般地难耐。\
The unwanted visitor stands in front of them, panting as if she's burning from her body temperature.

湖水倒映出她金红色的身影，摇曳晃动。\
Her golden reflection sways in water like real flames.

**可燃点**：……哈，哈啊……\
**Spathodea**: *deep breath*

**可燃点**：奔行。\
**Spathodea**: Race.

火焰燃烧的路径是一条跳跃的线，由沙丝绒去往了爱兹拉。\
The burning flame bounces from Desert Flannel to Ezra.

**爱兹拉**：……唔！\
**Ezra**: ... Uh ...

**爱兹拉**：它们没有伤到我的皮肤，只是烧掉了泡沫，这是什么新型的驱散药剂的方式吗？\
**Ezra**: It didn't cause any damage on me, just burning the foam on my skin. Is that some new method developed to get rid of the potion?

**爱兹拉**：但可燃点小姐怎么在这里，护士长不应该允许情况不稳定的人外出的……她，她是单独跑出来的吗？！\
**Ezra**: But what is Ms. Spathodea doing here? The head nurse shouldn't have let an unstable patient walk around freely. Did, did she sneak out?!

**沙丝绒**：天啊——老兄，她着火了！她瞧起来像是稳定的人吗？！\
**Desert Flannel**: Gosh! Mate, she's on fire! Does she even remotely look stable to you?

**可燃点**：奔行，如兽豸奔行……踏于藤与木的红土上……\
**Spathodea**: Race, like a deor ... stepping on the red soil where vines and woods grow ...

强烈的光与热如同浪潮。\
The glare and heat rush through her, like waves.

遍布火焰的可燃点带着眼中、口中、心中与肺腑中灼热的温度逼近，将距离自己最近的沙丝绒抱入怀中。\
Spathodea, engulfed in flame, approaches Desert Flannel, with fiery eyes, mouth, heart, and body, and takes her into her arms.

**沙丝绒**：呃呜——！\
**Desert Flannel**: Urrah!

**沙丝绒**：该死！热滚滚的，像是个煮汤的锅子！我们可不能让她继续发疯下去了！这股热度过不了多久就会把她的小脑瓜给煮熟的！\
**Desert Flannel**: Aah, f**k me dead! She's as well heated as a boiling pot! We can't let her go on like this! Her brain is going to be roasted in that little head!

沙丝绒奋力挣扎着，冰冷的双手拍打着可燃点的脸颊。\
Desert Flannel strives to get out of her control, patting Spathodea on the cheeks with her cold hands.

**沙丝绒**：松开手，可燃点！你太烫了，你必须得冷静点了！\
**Desert Flannel**: Let go, Spathodea! Your temperature is dangerously high. Chill out!

**可燃点**：我……不是蜥蜴……而，而……\
**Spathodea**: I'm not ... a lizard ... and ...

**可燃点**：2号混凝土与奶油，是美味的餐点和最好的导管素材！\
**Spathodea**: Concrete No. 2 with cream is the best dish and pipe material!

**维尔汀**：可燃点陷入混乱了，或许是火苗影响了她。\
**Vertin**: Spathodea is suffering confusion. It's probably the flame's doing.

**维尔汀**：我们得先把她们分开。\
**Vertin**: We need to separate them first.

**爱兹拉**：分开……分开！维尔汀小姐，请后退一些！\
**Ezra**: Okay ... okay! Ms. Vertin, please step back!

一股绿松石般的雾气迎向姑娘们。\
A mist with the color of turquoise blows toward the girls.

**沙丝绒**：喂！你在喷什么东西呢——我还在这儿呢！喂——\
**Desert Flannel**: Oi! What are you sprayin- ...?! I'm still here! Hey!

沙丝绒抗议的声响与可燃点的呓语很快都平息了下去。\
Soon, both Desert Flannel's complaints and Spathodea's sleep talk quiet down.

**爱兹拉**：只是一些蘑菇孢子，沙丝绒小姐，请放心。\
**Ezra**: This is just some spores, Ms. Desert Flannel, worry not.

**爱兹拉**：它们具有镇定作用，能使当地的野兽放松精神，失去攻击力，常常作为早期神秘学家捕猎和安抚的道具使用。\
**Ezra**: They are the tranquilizer that the locals used to pacify animals and was once widely used among arcanists in early times for hunting.

**爱兹拉**：只要可燃点小姐安静下来，我们就能把她带回——哇啊！\
**Ezra**: As long as we calm her down, we can bring her back to ... Whooaa!

如同火团的姑娘再一次将面前的人们撞得东倒西歪。\
However, that fireball girl hits everyone in front of her like knocking down all the pins in a row.

好一场精彩的保龄球赛。\
A perfect bowling strike.

**可燃点**：运动会……运动会！运动会！我们需要一场真正的运动会！\
**Spathodea**: Games ... Games! Games! We need the real Games!

**可燃点**：竞技的精神当在此处兴起……年轻人们，年轻人……们……\
**Spathodea**: This is where sportsmanship originates ... Young people, young ... people ...

**可燃点**：年轻的人们需要猫咪！需要草莓果——果酱！需要猫咪果酱！\
**Spathodea**: Young people need cats! And strawberry ja- ... jam! Cat jam it is!

**爱兹拉**：难道是我用错了蘑菇吗？！可燃点小姐的表现更加狂躁了！\
**Ezra**: Did I use the wrong mushroom? Ms. Spathodea has become even more restless!

**爱兹拉**：那沙丝绒小姐呢？沙丝绒小姐她——\
**Ezra**: What about Ms. Desert Flannel? Is she ...

爱兹拉从地上爬起来，顾不上掸去身上的灰尘，望向绿色的烟雾。\
Ezra manages to get up, looking at the turquoise green mist without dusting himself off.

**维尔汀**：不，你没用错。她和你说的一样。\
**Vertin**: No, you didn't. She's behaving exactly the way you described.

**爱兹拉**：啊……沙丝绒……小姐？\
**Ezra**: Aah ... Ms. ... Desert Flannel?

**沙丝绒**：……嘿嘿。\
**Desert Flannel**: ... Heh-heh.

他们凶悍的朋友脸上堆笑，如同吸了薄荷草儿的猫一样满地打滚。\
Their fierce friend, with a smile on her face, is rolling on the ground like a cat getting high on catmints.

双手虚幻地伸向空中，不断抓取着什么。\
She keeps reaching her hands to the sky as if she is trying to catch something.

**沙丝绒**：这间房子是……打算送给我吗？嘿嘿，哦……哈哈……\
**Desert Flannel**: Is this ... the house for me? Heh heh, oh ... Haha ...

**沙丝绒**：那我是不是就……再也不用付房租啦？嘻嘻……\
**Desert Flannel**: Does this mean I don't have to ... pay rent anymore? Heh heh ...

**维尔汀**：看来这就是她放松精神的方式。\
**Vertin**: Looks like this is how she has her mental break.

**爱兹拉**：我会立刻为沙丝绒小姐解除状态，她很快就能恢复，只需要，不到五分钟……但是，但是可燃点小姐好像要开始发动下一轮攻势了！\
**Ezra**: I will bring her back to normal immediately. It won't take mo-more than five minutes. But I think Ms. Spathodea is going to attack again!

**可燃点**：汝等需要的是灼热的门扉再度开放，是……\
**Spathodea**: What ye need is the reopening of the gate to the scorching land, and ...

**可燃点**：是——那巨石再被寻着……呜……\
**Spathodea**: And ... the retrieval of the rock ... Ugh ...

**爱兹拉**：而且她身上的火焰更剧烈了——不好，快蹲下！\
**Ezra**: And her fire is getting stronger ... Get down!

两人猛地蹲下身体，炙热的火焰擦着头顶撩过。\
The moment they duck, the scorching hot fire flies over the top of their heads.

**维尔汀**：已经没有时间了，让我们解决这里的问题吧。\
**Vertin**: We are running out of time. Let's deal with the burning issue first.

爱兹拉深吸一口气，握紧了背包的系带。\
Taking a deep breath, Ezra grabs the straps even tighter.

**爱兹拉**：……好的！我会尽力的！\
**Ezra**: I will! I will try my best!

**可燃点**：……呜，我这是在哪儿？\
**Spathodea**: Ugh, where am I?

**可燃点**：为什么你们都在我面前，你们不是被赶……走了……吗？\
**Spathodea**: What are you doing here, guys? I thought you were driven away?

**爱兹拉**：太好了，她清醒过来了！\
**Ezra**: Great, she's back to normal!

**可燃点**：啊……我想起来了……\
**Spathodea**: Oh ... I remember it now ...

可燃点的双腿发软，身体摇晃着，噗通一声倒了下去。\
Spathodea can't maintain her balance and falls to the ground.

**维尔汀**：可燃点！\
**Vertin**: Spathodea!

**可燃点**：运动会……\
**Spathodea**: The Games ...

可燃点艰难地抬起手臂，拉住了面前的袖口。\
She raises one arm with all her strength and grasps the cuff of the girl standing in front of her.

**可燃点**：必须重新……举办，乌卢鲁运动会……\
**Spathodea**: We must revive ... the Uluru Games ...

**可燃点**：因为……石头在膝盖上，响动……\
**Spathodea**: Because ... the rocks, rumble on the knees ...

**医护人员**：……事情的过程我已经听明白了。\
**Medical Staff**: I've heard what's going on.

**医护人员**：在返回拉普拉斯后，我们会优先检查她的脏器是否因为高温受伤。明天中午十一点以后再来探视。\
**Medical Staff**: We will check if her organs are injured by the high temperature after returning to Laplace. You can visit her tomorrow after 11:00 a.m.

**爱兹拉**：嗯？我们还可以去探视她吗？我还以为您会让可燃点小姐进入十三层的病房……\
**Ezra**: Emm? Can we visit her? I thought you would send her to the wards on the 13th floor.

**医护人员**：……疏通优于堵塞。\
**Medical Staff**: Go with the flow when you can't fight it.

**医护人员**：强行阻拦你们见面，将她独自安排在房间的结果我们已经见识到了。而且，拉普拉斯也不能再失去更多的诊疗室了。\
**Medical Staff**: We've now understood what will happen if we separate you and keep her alone some place else. What's more, Laplace can't lose another clinic.

**爱兹拉**：太好了，谢谢您！\
**Ezra**: I see, this is great! Thank you!

雪白的医疗车消失在街头的另一端。\
The white ambulance drives away from the street.

**沙丝绒**：所以……你那些蘑菇，确定不会对我的脑子和身体造成什么危害吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: So, are you sure those mushrooms won't cause any damage to my brain and body?

**沙丝绒**：比如智商降低、肺部患病、皮肤过敏之类的……\
**Desert Flannel**: Like lower IQ levels, lung diseases, or skin allergy ...

**爱兹拉**：嗯……如果需要，我可以陪你去拉普拉斯进行后续检查！\
**Ezra**: Emm. If you think it's necessary, I will accompany you to Laplace for some follow-up check-ups!

**爱兹拉**：当然啦，其中费用会从我的薪水里扣除的，请不要顾虑这方面的问题～\
**Ezra**: Of course, you don't have to pay for the tests. The fee will be deducted from my salary. Please don't worry about the money.

**沙丝绒**：停——停停停！我相信你！我还没坏到要诈骗一个小孩子的钱——而且……\
**Desert Flannel**: Okay okay! Enough! I trust you! I don't need a kid to pay the doctor for me. Besides ...

**沙丝绒**：……被蘑菇迷晕已经够丢人了，因为这个进医院——我这根本就是在给那个家伙机会害我……\
**Desert Flannel**: It's embarrassing enough to be put down by mushrooms, not to mention that I'll be giving that guy the story they carved if I was hospitalized.

**爱兹拉**：“那个家伙”？\
啊……你是指，跟着你的那位记者……\
**Ezra**: "That guy"? Ah, you mean, the journalist following you.

**爱兹拉**：唔——\
**Ezra**: Emm ...

**沙丝绒**：闪光灯？！该死……说什么就来什么，真倒霉。\
**Desert Flannel**: Was that a flash?! Speak of the devil ... B****r!

唾骂一声，沙丝绒紧绷着脸，扫视过隐没于黑暗的树丛。\
Silently cursing, Desert Flannel scans the bush in the dark with a serious look on her face.

**沙丝绒**：在我去揪着你的尾巴之前，自己滚出来。\
**Desert Flannel**: Come out yourself. Don't make me force you!

树丛摇曳着，几秒钟后，半个人影从其中探出，黑色的衣服和黑夜相融，看起来就像是单独飘在空中的一张脸。\
The bush rustles. Seconds later, a man stands up. His black shirt indistinguishable from the darkness, making his face appear as if it were floating in the air.

**？？？**：……呵。\
**???**: Heh.

**沙丝绒**：马科尔，你不能扯无关的人进来。这是我俩之间的事儿。\
**Desert Flannel**: Makower, don't you dare involve others. This is between you and me.

**马科尔**：我早就说过了，我会让你品尝与我相同的痛苦。我一直跟着你，为的就是现在，就是这一天……！\
**Makower**: I've told you long ago that one day I will make you feel the same misery that I did. I've been following you all the time, and this is the moment, the moment of vengeance!

**马科尔**：呵呵，现在，我的素材已经足够了……\
**Makower**: Heh-heh, now, I have more than enough photos.

**马科尔**：至于有谁受害……我可从不记得你是个这么善良的人。\
**Makower**: As for these "other people" ... You didn't strike me as such a kind-hearted person.

**沙丝绒**：我从前可不知道你是个这么无耻的人！\
**Desert Flannel**: I didn't know you are so shameless!

**马科尔**：期待明早的报纸吧，摄影好手。\
**Makower**: Let's see what tomorrow's newspaper has to say about this, Ms. Photographer.

飘浮着的脸露出一个狰狞的笑容，转身消失在黑夜中。\
A hideous smile forms on that floating face. Makower then disappears in the shadow.

**沙丝绒**：不行，不能就让他这样跑了，他拍了我们的照片！\
**Desert Flannel**: No, we can't let him get away. He has a photo of us!

**爱兹拉**：那是你的敌……嗯，严谨地来说，应该是仇家吗？你们之间发生了什么？\
**Ezra**: Is he your enemy ... emm, maybe archenemy? What happened between you two?

**沙丝绒**：如果你不想作为一只“燃烧的袋鼠”登上八卦报纸的话，闭上嘴，立刻追上去！\
**Desert Flannel**: If you don't wanna be one of the "burning kangaroos" on the headline tomorrow, shut up and start running!

**维尔汀**：我们得阻止他。\
**Vertin**: We have to stop him.

## RUG-05 漂浮球们 / The Buoy Balls

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

立起衣领，压低脑袋，悄无声息地站在报刊亭侧门边。\
Collar raised and head lowered, standing silently by the side door of the newsstand.

**？？？**：老板，给我一份最新的《叮当快报》。\
**???**: G'day, you got the latest Australian Nagger here?

**报刊亭老板**：好眼光，客人。今天所有人都在讨论着这份——嗯？\
**Newsstand Owner**: Nice choice. Everyone is talking about ... Hmm?

奇怪的客人劈手夺走小报，一头扎进去读了起来。\
The strange customer snatches the paper from the newsstand owner and lapses into reading.

**？？？**：“昨晚夜间，我市公园出现奇怪集团聚会……”\
**???**: "A strange party held in the City Park last night …"

**？？？**：“……滚烫的袋鼠、沉溺于蘑菇的翻滚鳄与青少年纵火犯一同共舞，隐藏于绿地中的秘密，必将复兴的乌卢鲁运动会……”\
**???**: "... The witness claimed to see the burning kangaroos, mushroom-intoxicated rolling croc, and the teenage arsonist dancing together ... A secret event on the public lawn ... The revival of the Uluru Games …"

紧握的手指开始颤抖，报纸上出现皱褶、破洞和更大的……破洞。\
Fingers clutching at the newspaper tremble. The newspaper wrinkles, breaks ...

**？？？**：“我们必须承认，当下的经济颓势与居住支出走高显然已经击溃了一部分年轻人的内心，以致于……他们爬行在深夜的公园……”\
**???**: "It saddens us to admit that the recession and inflation have walloped some young adults ... They were ... crawling in the park at night …"

**？？？**：“如同野兽一般地嘶哑呻吟，滚动，甚至失去神智……”\
**???**: "Groaning and moaning like beasts, dragging themselves along, and losing consciousness …"

熟悉的声音，熟悉的身形，熟悉的脾气与反应。\
The voice, the figure, the temper, and the reaction all seem familiar.

**报刊亭老板**：等等，这个声音……难道你是……\
**Newsstand Owner**: Wait, your voice ... Are you ...

**沙丝绒**：……你必须现在打扰我吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Do you have to talk to me right now?

纸张哗哗作响，熟悉的脸从后升起，紧皱的眉头下是一双带有血丝的眼睛。\
Behind the rustling newspaper is a familiar face with frowning eyebrows and bloodshot eyes.

**沙丝绒**：我正忙着憎恨我的人生，没空和你闲聊。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm busy hating my life. I don't have time for your little chit-chat.

**报刊亭老板**：天啊，沙丝绒——居然真的是你！\
**Newsstand Owner**: No way, Desert Flannel. It's really you!

**报刊亭老板**：现在所有人都在讨论你呢，猜什么的人都有。有人说你们是疯子，也有人说你们是和外星人战斗的英雄……\
**Newsstand Owner**: Everybody is talking about you right now! And they can really imagine. Some say you're mad, some say you're the hero fighting against aliens ...

**报刊亭老板**：当然，最主流的说法还是那个——那个运动会，你们真的要重新举办那个运动会吗？\
**Newsstand Owner**: Well, the most known story is "that event." Is it real that you're going to restart the Games?

**沙丝绒**：那运动会和我可一点儿关系都没有！都是那个女初中生搞的事儿——我只是倒霉而已！\
**Desert Flannel**: I have nothing to do with it! It was all that junior's fault. I was just unlucky!

对折、打开、对折、打开、对折，又打开。\
Fold, and open, and fold, and open.

如同动物园内焦虑的动物，沙丝绒一面反复翻弄手里的报纸，一面在地面上打转。\
Desert Flannel leafs through the newspaper, pacing back and forth like an animal trapped in the cage of the zoo.

**沙丝绒**：我倒霉撞上了那些奇怪的家伙，倒霉地跟他们去了医院，又倒霉地惹上了马科尔那个混蛋。\
**Desert Flannel**: It was pure bad luck that I ran into those weirdos, got taken to the hospital, and let Makower get what he wants.

**沙丝绒**：我不该跟丢他的，如果我还能再抓住他一次，我发誓，我会把他的舌头拉出来缠在他脖子上……！\
**Desert Flannel**: I shouldn't have let him get away. If I see him again, I swear, I will pull out his tongue and tie it around his neck!

**沙丝绒**：你瞧瞧这家伙写的都是什么——他说我们是食用下水道里本耶普的瘾君子，说我们是燃烧的袋鼠，还说我因为房租发疯！\
**Desert Flannel**: Look at this gibberish. He said we are the d**eheads who eat Bunyips from the sewage, a burning kangaroo, and I am a nutter because I can't find a way to afford rent!

**沙丝绒**：天啊——我还不如就成为一只袋鼠算了！\
**Desert Flannel**: This is great. I might as well be a kangaroo!

**报刊亭老板**：至少你为房租发疯这件事儿属实。\
**Newsstand Owner**: At least it's true that you're banging your head against the wall for rent.

**沙丝绒**：……\
**Desert Flannel**: ...

**沙丝绒**：你说得对，现在，猜猜激怒一个“发疯的家伙”会有什么后果？\
**Desert Flannel**: Yeah, be mindful that you're talking to a nutter.

在锐利的目光下，报刊亭老板将自己过于探出的身体缩回了柜台后方，双手老老实实地铺在膝盖上。\
Glared at by those sharp eyes, the newsstand owner withdraws behind the counter and puts his hands on his knees like a good boy.

**沙丝绒**：哈……反正我马上就会被辞退，失去我所有的兼职工作，身无分文地被踢出我奶奶租了数十年的房子……\
**Desert Flannel**: Ha, whatever. I will soon lose my part-time jobs and be kicked out of the house where my granny lived for decades.

皱巴巴的报纸被甩回报刊亭的台面，沙丝绒两手插回口袋。\
The crumpled newspaper is thrown into the newsstand and Desert Flannel puts her hands back in her pockets.

**沙丝绒**：我回去了。如果你有任何赚钱的工作都可以联系我，我什么都能做好，只要钱够……算了，只要有钱就好。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm heading back. Let me know if you know any job vacancies. I can do a lot of things, as long as the money is good ... no, as long as I'm paid.

**报刊亭老板**：等等，沙丝绒。你……过来看看这个。\
**Newsstand Owner**: Wait, Desert Flannel. Come and take a look at this.

一只精巧的小木盒放在皱报纸上方，里头装着一张张画着火焰图纹的长纸片。\
A delicate wooden box is placed on the crumpled newspaper, with a lot of tickets inside.

**报刊亭老板**：今早有无数人来我这儿打探过乌卢鲁运动会，而一个小时前……小剪刀杰瑞给我拿来了这个。\
**Newsstand Owner**: So many people came here this morning, asking about the Uluru Games. And one hour before, the Scissors Jerry brought me this.

**沙丝绒**：这是……乌卢鲁运动会……预售票？\
**Desert Flannel**: This is ... a pre-sale ticket to the Uluru Games?

**报刊亭老板**：已经卖出去五十多张了，一张能要到……这个价。\
**Newsstand Owner**: I've sold over 50 tickets, at a unit price of ... this much.

四下张望几秒，老板比出一个手势，沙丝绒的嘴巴张开，形成了一个漂亮的O形。\
Looking around to make sure that there is nobody nearby, the owner makes a gesture. Desert Flannel's jaw drops.

**沙丝绒**：……啊？\
**Desert Flannel**: Huh?

她低下头，报纸上“乌卢鲁运动会”几个字变得那样鲜活而甜美。\
She lowers her gaze to the newspaper. In a lively font, the headline reads: "Uluru Games."

**报刊亭老板**：它停办了很久，每个人都以为这个社会已经忘了它。\
**Newsstand Owner**: It has been suspended for too long, so long that everyone thinks society has forgotten it.

**报刊亭老板**：但我们都记得，我们的祖辈如何对我们形容那些神奇而富有乐趣的项目，那个漂亮与广阔的运动场。\
**Newsstand Owner**: But we remember—our ancestors told us about those amazing and funny sports, that big, wide, and fancy Stadium.

**沙丝绒**：人们都记得它，期待它，哪怕是如此明显的假票也能炒上高价……老板，你这儿还有其他帮派放的票吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: They all remember it, even looking forward to it, and even bid up for a fake ticket. Mate, did you get more of these from the other gangs?

**报刊亭老板**：还有两盒。\
**Newsstand Owner**: Two boxes left.

将香烟夹在手指上，报刊亭老板蹲下身去。\
Holding the cigarette between the knuckles of his index and middle fingers, the owner squats down behind the counter.

他的手臂从下头伸出来，两个更大、更重的木盒落在桌面上。\
His hands lift up, holding two even bigger and heavier boxes. His voice comes from below.

**报刊亭老板**：它们来自机灵鬼和桉树兄弟会。\
**Newsstand Owner**: These are from the Slicky and Eucalyptus Brotherhood.

**沙丝绒**：桉——什么，桉什么？我没听清楚……对了，你还记得我之前买过的薄荷糖吗？销量不好，你放在箱子最下头的那种。\
**Desert Flannel**: Eucalyptus and what? Didn't catch that name. Oh, do you have the mints that I bought from you before? The least purchased ones. You always put them at the bottom of your box.

一阵翻找东西的声响后，报刊亭老板灰头土脸地钻出柜台，将一只掉了色的铁盒拍在桌面上。\
After the sounds of struggled searching, the owner at last pops his head back up, now covered with dust, and throws a faded iron box on the counter.

**报刊亭老板**：好了！把我的票还回来，我得把它们收回去，我可不想被人发现我同时接了三个帮……沙丝绒？\
**Newsstand Owner**: Alright! Now, give my ticket back, and I'll put it away. I don't want any of the gangs to find out I'm dealing with the oth- ... Desert Flannel?

报刊亭前空无一人。\
In front of him is an empty counter.

一个零钱包放在被遗弃的报纸中心，里面一分钱也没有，只是塞满了灰褐色的羽毛。\
A coin purse has been placed on the abandoned newspaper, holding no coins but instead gray feathers.

**报刊亭老板**：我早就说过了。\
**Newsstand Owner**: That's what I keep telling everyone.

一声叹息。如同长兄与父亲的朋友点起一支新的香烟。\
Letting out a fatherly sigh, the newsstand owner lights up another cigarette.

**报刊亭老板**：……这个坏姑娘最擅长的就是把清水搅得一团浑浊。\
**Newsstand Owner**: Muddying the water is what this bad girl does.

**马科尔**：没错。沙丝绒带走了小剪刀、机灵鬼和桉树兄弟会的假票。\
**Makower**: That's right. Desert Flannel has taken the fake tickets with her—the ones from Clippy, Slicky, and the Eucalyptus Brotherhood.

**马科尔**：她已经离开了……不，她并没有前往地下市场。\
**Makower**: She's gone ... no, not to the black market.

**马科尔**：……\
**Makower**: ...

**马科尔**：先生，我听说本耶普们又开始陷入躁动了，这是真的吗？\
**Makower**: Sir, I heard that the Bunyips are getting restless again, is that true?

电话的另一侧，香烟熄灭的嗤声与笑声同时传来。\
On the other end of the phone comes the noise of pinching a cigarette followed by laughter.

躲藏在阴影中默不作声，年轻姑娘的身影飞快地从他身旁掠过。\
Hiding in the shadows in silence, the young girl darts past him.

**沙丝绒**：哈——这下我一定会大赚一笔！\
**Desert Flannel**: Ha! I'm gonna make a fortune out of it!

**沙丝绒**：我能买下那栋房子，还能添置一个新烤炉，一些新衣服，我还可以给波拉比买上一个羊绒制的大号宠物窝！\
**Desert Flannel**: I will be able to buy that house, get myself a new oven, some new clothes, and that giant wool nest for Plappy!

掀开的井盖倒向一边，漆黑湿润的怪物甩动着皮肉，爬上人行道。\
In a crash, some wet, black monsters flip over the well lid and crawl onto the road.

**沙丝绒**：该死，那些本耶普又爬出来了，它们已经很久没出来过了，我得赶紧……\
**Desert Flannel**: Urh, those Bunyips are out again. Haven't seen them out in the sun for a while now. I must hurry ...

**沙丝绒**：……等等，它们怎么过来了？！\
**Desert Flannel**: Wait, are they coming my way?!

**马科尔**：我已经看见它们了，它们比起我更关注她。\
**Makower**: I've got my eyes on them. They are more interested in her than in me.

**沙丝绒**：也难怪，现在乌卢鲁运动会的事情闹得满城风雨，到处都是人在关心这件事儿！最喜欢“流言蜚语”的水怪本耶普怎么会缺席呢？\
**Desert Flannel**: Well, this makes sense. Since the Uluru Games have made the biggest news of the week, the people are going on and on about it all day! And where else will the rumor-loving Bunyips go at this point?

**沙丝绒**：哈啊～上次见到这样的场面还是在飞机头叔叔传丑闻的时候呢～！\
**Desert Flannel**: Hah! The last time I saw something like this was when that scandal of Mr. Pompadour broke!

**马科尔**：如同那些伤患的膝盖总在雨天前发疼，这一定会是个大新闻的。\
**Makower**: It will be a big story, almost as certainly as a cut will bleed.

**马科尔**：我会停止所有的拍摄目标，全力追踪这个项目。\
**Makower**: I will pause my other projects and focus on this one.

**马科尔**：……多谢您的赏识。\
**Makower**: This is very kind of you. I really appreciate it.

**沙丝绒**：没人——也没神秘学生物能挡我赚钱的路子，而且你们现在也没吃够流言蜚语，变成多手多脚三层楼那么高的怪物！\
**Desert Flannel**: Nobody, nor any arcane creatures, can stop me from getting rich! Let alone that you haven't eaten enough rumors to grow into a three-floor high and multi-legged gigantic monster!

**沙丝绒**：比比-啵啵-啦——波拉比，出来帮帮忙！\
**Desert Flannel**: Bo-bo-bo-bo ... Plappy, give me a hand!

灵巧地后退几步，沙丝绒按下电子宠物的开机按钮，一只巨大的鸸鹋抖动着羽毛从像素块中跳出。\
She swiftly takes a few steps back and presses the ON button on the digital pet device. A giant emu jumps out from the pixels, fluffing its feathers.

**波拉比**：——呼咕！\
**Plappy**: Coo!!

**本耶普**：嘶嘶——嘎！\
**Bunyip**: Sss ... GARH!!

**沙丝绒**：哈！喜欢这些满是“假消息”味道的票匣子吗？喜欢就来拿吧！\
**Desert Flannel**: Ha! Like that "smell of rumors" from this ticket box? Come get it yourself!

**可燃点**：我都说过了，我健康得不得了！你们现在就应该放我走！\
**Spathodea**: Told you I'm super healthy! You should let me go now!

**爱兹拉**：可是你还需要我们的照顾，可燃点小姐。\
确认神秘学家的安全和稳定也是医院的责任之一。\
**Ezra**: But you need our care, Ms. Spathodea. It's also our responsibility to make sure that you're safe and stable.

**爱兹拉**：神秘学家在获得神秘术能力初期，往往会迎来长达4～12周的不稳定期，在这期间你有可能陷入混乱、情绪崩溃、剧烈的幻觉或是频繁的昏厥……\
**Ezra**: When arcanists were first introduced to their power, they would experience a 4-to-12-week adjustment period, during which they may suffer emotional breakdown, strong hallucinations, or frequent comas.

**可燃点**：嘿，等等——等一下！我现在真的有很重要的事情要做！\
**Spathodea**: Hey, stop, stop it! I have something very important to do right now, I mean it!

**可燃点**：我不会在这里浪费时间！也不会陷入混乱——不会情绪崩溃，更不会揣想那幻觉或是走在路上就昏倒！\
**Spathodea**: I'm not gonna waste my time here! I'm fine! There will be no more confusion, mental breakdown, hallucination, or coma!

**维尔汀**：很重要的事情？那是什么？\
**Vertin**: Something very important? What is it?

年轻姑娘的目光在爱兹拉脸上停留了许久，最终神神秘秘地开口。\
The young girl stares at Ezra for a doubtful long time and finally talks.

**可燃点**：昨晚，我听到火苗开口说话了。\
**Spathodea**: My flame talked to me last night.

**火苗**：呼……呼……\
**Flame**: *steady breath*

火苗起伏跳跃，年轻姑娘伸出手抚摸它，像是抚摸一只卷成团的猫儿。\
The flame keeps hopping at a steady pace. Spathodea pets it like petting a curled kitty.

**可燃点**：现在……它睡着了，昨晚和我一起上蹿下跳，它好像累坏了。\
**Spathodea**: Now, it's asleep. I think it's exhausted after our rampage last night.

**维尔汀**：那些谈话和你的变化有关？\
**Vertin**: Is the conversation about your changes?

**可燃点**：当然了！我一碰到它，那些火就顺着我的手臂，从嘴巴——爬回了我的胃里！\
**Spathodea**: Of course! The moment I touched it, it crawled along my arm to my mouth and went back to the stomach!

**可燃点**：而我的眼前……只剩下一面黑色的墙。\
**Spathodea**: And-and all there's left in front of me was a black wall.

**维尔汀**：抱歉……我不太明白。或许，你能和我们谈谈当时发生的事情吗？\
**Vertin**: Sorry, I'm not quite with you. Perhaps you could start from what happened then.

**可燃点**：没问题！虽然我记得没那么清楚……\
**Spathodea**: Sure! I don't remember it well, though.

**可燃点**：它们很模糊，就像是站在30层毛玻璃后看一盘培根煎蛋，我只能从缝隙里勉勉强强地感受到一点点。\
**Spathodea**: They were blurry memories. Imagine you are looking at a plate of bacon and eggs through 30 layers of frosted glass. I had to get close to the glass to barely feel them.

**可燃点**：但是除开你们，我的面前还有一扇装着清晰玻璃的窗户。\
**Spathodea**: I remembered you were there, and there was also a clear window.

**可燃点**：里面总体来说是一片黑暗，但偶尔又会闪过一些画面……\
**Spathodea**: I saw complete darkness in the window for most of the time, but there were pictures flashing by sometimes.

**爱兹拉**：我想那正是属于“轮回者”的记忆！这和记载里的情况一样！\
**Ezra**: I believe that's your memory as a "reincarnator"! Just like what's written in the books!

**可燃点**：嘿！别打断我！\
**Spathodea**: Hey! Let me finish!

**爱兹拉**：啊……对不起，我只是第一次看到和书本里一样的画面出现在我面前。请继续。\
**Ezra**: Ah, sorry. I was too excited because this is the first time I see a valid proof of "reincarnation." Please continue.

**可燃点**：咳咳——！\
**Spathodea**: Ahem!

**可燃点**：我想，那是关于我“轮回者”的记忆。\
**Spathodea**: I think that's my memory, as a "reincarnator."

**可燃点**：我在那扇窗里看见我的身体，就像是我现在低头看见的我自己。\
**Spathodea**: I saw my own body in that window, just like the one I'm looking at here.

**可燃点**：我看见许多火焰，许多摇晃的光，许多人——\
**Spathodea**: I saw a lot of flames, wobbling lights, and people ...

年轻活泼的姑娘深深地吸了一口气，掌心压上自己的胸膛。\
The lively young girl takes a deep breath and presses her palm against her chest.

**可燃点**：我的心从未跳得那样快过，而那团火在我的身体里，毫无异样，就像它天生就应当带着我这样燃烧……\
**Spathodea**: My heart has never beaten that fast, yet the fire in my body seemed completely natural, as if it was destined to burn inside me.

**可燃点**：它对我耳语，一次又一次，只有一个词。\
**Spathodea**: It whispered just one phrase to me, again and again.

**维尔汀**：就像是你昨晚所说的……\
**Vertin**: Like what you mentioned last night.

**可燃点**：是的，“乌卢鲁运动会”。我必须重新举办乌卢鲁运动会。\
**Spathodea**: Yes, the Uluru Games. I must revive the Uluru Games.

**爱兹拉**：可是……你要怎么做呢？\
**Ezra**: But, what are you going to do?

**爱兹拉**：撇去申请文书、安全维护与官方许可的复杂流程不谈。\
**Ezra**: Let's not get to the paper work of applications, security arrangement, and permission from the local government just yet.

**爱兹拉**：乌卢鲁运动会的入口行踪不定，只能由部分神秘学家寻着入口，且只允许神秘学家进入。从没有人类见证或是参加过这场比赛。\
**Ezra**: The location of entrance to the Uluru Games was never fixed. Only few arcanists could find it, and the Games are for arcanists only. There has never been a human athlete in there.

**爱兹拉**：而它停止举办的原因是……它于1942年的战争中彻底地遗失了。至今为止，都没有人能找到它的踪迹。\
**Ezra**: And they have been canceled for all these years because they were completely lost in the war in 1942. Nobody has found them since.

**可燃点**：但我能找到它，因为我是我，我是现在“这个”世界上唯一踏足过那处土壤的人……而我的火焰，它是我的指南针。\
**Spathodea**: But I can find it, because I have found my ancient self. I'm the only person in "this time" who has been to "that land" and my flame is my compass.

可燃点掀开软被，从病床上坐起身子。\
Spathodea throws back the covers and sits up on the bed.

**可燃点**：虽然我还是没弄明白，为什么我的记忆中充满了我与它争吵的画面，可是我们一同燃烧时，我感到我变得如此完整——\
**Spathodea**: Though I have not yet figured out why my memories are all about the conflicts with the flame, I felt so whole again when we burned together.

**可燃点**：我相信它会帮助我，它会与我联合，因为它是如此信任我，以致于跨越那样漫长的黑暗和雨季，从我嘴里冒出来。\
**Spathodea**: I'm sure it will help me and unite with me, because it trusts me so much that it traveled all the way here through the endless darkness and rainy seasons to come out of my mouth.

**可燃点**：它是为我而来的，它将要带我去某处。\
**Spathodea**: It's here for me, and now it's going to take me somewhere else.

**可燃点**：我会去那儿。\
**Spathodea**: I'll follow wherever it goes.

可燃点的双手捏着探视者的衣袖，大大的眼睛里满是期望。\
She seizes the cuff of the visitor, looking at her with her puppy dog eyes.

**可燃点**：……所以，维尔汀，你说过你会对我负责的——你能和我一起走吗？\
**Spathodea**: So, Vertin, you said you would take care of me. Would you come with me?

**可燃点**：我需要一支“复兴小队”，我需要朋友，就像是我与火焰一样，我们会互相支撑，互相理解！到时候你也会进入运动场，一起奔跑！\
**Spathodea**: I need a Revival Squad and friends who understand and support each other, just the way the flame and I do! By then, you'll go to the Stadium too, and we'll run together!

**可燃点**：我发誓，那儿多美好，不会让你后悔——你一定会喜欢乌卢鲁运动会的！\
**Spathodea**: I promise it will be a wonderful place where you'll never regret going. You will enjoy the Uluru Games!

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：很久以前，我曾在校图书馆里看过珍藏的乌卢鲁运动会的照片。\
**Vertin**: I have seen pictures of the Uluru Games in the school library collection a long time ago.

**维尔汀**：尽管我并不热衷于例行的体能测验，但如果能亲眼见到旧日运动盛会的重现……我想，不会有神秘学家选择拒绝。\
**Vertin**: I was not a fan of the routine physical fitness test at school, but I don't think any arcanist would say no to witnessing the revival of the once magnificent Games.

**可燃点**：……哦？你的意思是？\
**Spathodea**: Oh, so?

**维尔汀**：我很高兴加入你的计划，这会是一个很好的新开始。\
**Vertin**: I'm more than willing to join you in bringing back the Games. It will be a wonderful new beginning.

手与手交握，示意着成功的合作。\
A handshake is offered and accepted to symbolize their successful cooperation.

**可燃点**：哇——太好了，谢谢你！\
**Spathodea**: Wow! Yes! Thank you!

**爱兹拉**：原来如此，可燃点小姐你的确有着非常重要的使命……我会为你申请出院手续的！茱蒂丝护士长那边我也会处理好的！\
**Ezra**: I see. You're shouldering extremely important responsibility, Ms. Spathodea. I will apply for you to be discharged and explain all these to Judith!

**可燃点**：太好了！也谢谢你——爱兹拉，我不会忘记你对乌卢鲁复兴事业做出的帮助！\
**Spathodea**: Oh! And thank you Ezra! I won't forget your contribution to the revival of the Uluru Games!

**爱兹拉**：能够帮助到你，我感到非常的荣幸。\
**Ezra**: I'm deeply honored to have this chance to help.

**爱兹拉**：那么，我现在就去办理手续，而后尽快去收拾我的行李。\
**Ezra**: Then, I will get the paperwork done and go pack.

**可燃点**：嗯？你为什么也要收拾行李呀？\
**Spathodea**: Hmm? What's that for?

**爱兹拉**：因为我需要携带更多蘑菇，好在路上为你们提供可能需要的帮助。\
**Ezra**: I need to prepare as many mushrooms as possible so that I can better assist you on the way.

**可燃点**：你？路上？\
**Spathodea**: You? On the way?

可燃点的手指，指指自己，又指指面前的爱兹拉。\
She points at herself and then at Ezra.

**可燃点**：你也要一起来……？\
**Spathodea**: You're coming, too?

**爱兹拉**：当然。我与大家一起经历了许多事，难道我不是复兴小队的一员……吗？\
**Ezra**: Of course. We've been through so many things together. Am I not part of the team?

**可燃点**：不——当然不是了！你怎么能加入复兴小队呢？！\
**Spathodea**: No, of course not! How can I take you in the Revival Squad?!

**可燃点**：那是神秘学家的运动会，你也看过资料的，从过去到现在，人类做出了无数次尝试，一次都没有找到过乌卢鲁运动场的入口——那不是人类能去的地方！\
**Spathodea**: The Games is meant for arcanists. You've read the documents, right? Since the very beginning of history, humans have made countless attempts to find the entrance to the Stadium, yet none of them made it—it's just not for humans!

**可燃点**：如果你喜欢运动比赛，那就去看人类办的运动比赛吧！明天墨尔本还有一场拳击赛呢，就在弗林德斯公园国家网球中心！\
**Spathodea**: If you are a fan of sports, you can totally watch those held by humans! There will be a boxing event in Melbourne tomorrow, at the National Tennis Center at Flinders Park!

**爱兹拉**：不，你误会了，可燃点小姐，我对运动并没有兴趣，我需要与你们一起行动是因为你的症状还未康复，需要我的帮助。\
**Ezra**: No, no, Ms. Spathodea. I'm not interested in any games. The only reason why I'm coming along is because you haven't fully recovered and still need medical care.

**爱兹拉**：而另一点，我也希望从你身上得到更多关于“轮回者”的观察信息。\
**Ezra**: Besides, I hope to collect more information about "reincarnators" from you.

**爱兹拉**：我不会打扰你们对乌卢鲁运动场的寻觅的，请允许我加入复兴小队吧，这是我们之间的双赢，是一件非常好的事儿。\
**Ezra**: I will not disturb your mission searching for the Stadium. Please, let me come with you. It's going to be good for both of us.

**可燃点**：观察信息？你在观察……和记录我？\
**Spathodea**: Collect information? You're monitoring me?

**可燃点**：你——你什么时候得到过我的许可，可以研究和记录我了？！我可从来都没同意过你这么做！\
**Spathodea**: Sin-Since when did I grant you the permission to do that?! I never said yes!

**可燃点**：我才不愿意被研究，被带到报纸上展示——就像你说的那个“轮回者”一样！\
