**Spathodea**: I don't wanna be studied or published on newspaper, like the "reincarnator" you talked about!

**爱兹拉**：研究不一定意味着上报纸，我们可以选择更安全、更低调的方式。\
**Ezra**: Our research does not need to be published on the newspaper. We can do it in a more subtle and secure manner.

**爱兹拉**：我不会为你制定任务，也不会逼迫你使用不同的药剂，我的研究只需要安静地进行观测，而后记录，确保你的安全与健康就足够了。\
**Ezra**: I will not design any tasks for you to perform, nor will I force you to take any potions. My job is to observe, record, and ensure your health and safety.

**爱兹拉**：就像是记录菌类的变化一样……\
**Ezra**: Like what we do with the mushrooms.

**可燃点**：可我是一个大活人，又不是一颗蘑菇！我已经受够了被人盯着看了……！\
**Spathodea**: But I'm a living arcanist, not a mushroom! I have had enough of everyone watching!

审视着面前的爱兹拉，她有些犹豫，几步退回床铺，用被子包起了自己。\
Looking up and down at Ezra, she hesitates and returns to her bed, wrapping herself up with the quilt like a burrito.

**可燃点**：……我可不想被利用，也不想成为谁学术名声上的装饰品，更不会成为你转变研究专业的论文道具。\
**Spathodea**: I don't wanna be the embellishment added to someone's academic achievement or a subject of the paper that will help you switch fields.

**爱兹拉**：啊，看来是我的说法带来了误会。\
**Ezra**: Ah, I didn't explain it right.

**爱兹拉**：可燃点小姐，请听我说，我作为研究者的心从未偏移，我喜欢神秘学家，也一样喜欢我亲爱的蘑菇们，改变研究方向并非我的目的。\
**Ezra**: Ms. Spathodea, please listen to me. I have never changed my heart as a researcher, and I care about arcanists as much as I care about mushrooms. It was never my intention to use you as a career boost.

**爱兹拉**：你是一个难得的机会，我们谁也不知道下一个“轮回者”会在何时被发现，如果错失了这次宝贵的机遇，学界的新发展可能会推迟几十年。\
**Ezra**: You are such a rare opportunity to us, because none of us know when and where the next "reincarnator" will be found. If we miss this opportunity, the academic circle may have to wait for another decade to further their research.

**爱兹拉**：而你和我可能带来的新发现——也许它会震惊许多人，也许它会让我们的名字写进书籍，但更重要的是，它可以帮助许多人！\
**Ezra**: The discovery you and I made may shock many, our names might go down in history, but most importantly, it's going to help a lot of people!

**爱兹拉**：就像是佩罗蒂女爵士的长腿牧者【Tchangues】一般，它来源于一位拥有神秘学血统的法国长腿牧羊人，而它现在已经帮助无数残疾人重拾了奔跑与步行的可能！\
**Ezra**: Have you heard of Tchangues invented by Dame Perotti? It was inspired by a long-legged shepherd in France, and it has helped many athletes with disabilities to walk and run again!

多漂亮的一击。\
What a nice shot.

**可燃点**：……呜。\
**Spathodea**: Ughhhh.

小拳击手发出漫长而又痛苦的呜咽。\
A long, painful moan escapes the little boxer's mouth.

**爱兹拉**：可燃点小姐？你怎么这样缩在被子里……\
**Ezra**: Ms. Spathodea? You look miserable in the blanket.

**维尔汀**：继续说下去，爱兹拉。你距离成功已经不远了。\
**Vertin**: Keep going, Ezra. You're very close …

**爱兹拉**：我……？成功？嗯？\
**Ezra**: Me? Close to what? I don't follow.

**沙丝绒**：成功——对！说到成功——猜猜谁会成为赚到睡觉都在笑的“成功人士”呀！\
**Desert Flannel**: Close ... Well, speaking of close, guess who is close to becoming the most successful business person here?

**维尔汀**：……沙丝绒？你回来了？\
**Vertin**: Desert Flannel? Where have you been?

**沙丝绒**：嘿！别把眼睛瞪得那么大，我又不是什么地下水道里爬出来的怪物。\
**Desert Flannel**: Hi! What're the wide eyes for? I'm not some monster crawling out of the sewage.

甩掉鞋底的泥巴，沙丝绒手中捧着三只木盒快步走进房间。\
She scrapes the mud from under her shoes and trots into the room, carrying three wooden boxes.

**可燃点**：你看起来好狼狈……你怎么了？\
**Spathodea**: You look a mess. What happened?

**沙丝绒**：呃，我也没问你像个鸵鸟一样跪在被子里是为什么，你也别问我这些背后有什么原因，好吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Err, I didn't ask you why you are crouching in bed like an ostrich, did I? So maybe you can return the favor and keep your nose out of my business, yes?

**沙丝绒**：而且真正重要的是这些——这些好宝贝！\
**Desert Flannel**: And what really matters is the good stuff here!

沙丝绒亲昵地拍动木盒的顶部，发出轻巧的叩叩声。\
Desert Flannel knocks on the cover of a box and is satisfied with the crisp sound.

**沙丝绒**：你们绝对想不到，我们遇上了什么样天大的好运，我亲爱的商——啊不，朋友们。\
**Desert Flannel**: You wouldn't know how unbelievably lucky we are, my dear business part- ... errr, friends.

**可燃点**：我猜不出来。\
**Spathodea**: Yeah, no. I don't.

**可燃点**：我的脑子光是应付爱兹拉一个人就已经精疲力尽了。\
**Spathodea**: *sighs* Ezra alone is already too much information for my brain.

**沙丝绒**：好吧，没耐心又没情趣的家伙。\
**Desert Flannel**: Fine, you restless and humorless people.

握住把手，拉足期待，将橡皮筋理论拴在小木盒的顶板。\
Now hold tight and get ready. The rubber band is being stretched further and further above the box.

**沙丝绒**：我们得重办一场乌卢鲁运动会！\
**Desert Flannel**: We will bring back the Uluru Games!

**可燃点**：……唔。\
**Spathodea**: Hmph.

**爱兹拉**：嗯……\
**Ezra**: Emm.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**沙丝绒**：喂，这是在干什么呢？一片恼人的沉默？\
**Desert Flannel**: Hey! What kind of reaction is this? Why are you quiet as stones?

**沙丝绒**：这可是天大的好事，你们怎么一点反应都没有！\
**Desert Flannel**: This is a great idea, and you're giving me this?!

在充满疑惑与沉默的房间内，隆起的被窝中孤零零伸出一只手，悬停在她面前。\
In the room brimmed with wordless doubt and silence, a hand reaches up from beneath the quilt.

**可燃点**：来吧，加入我的复兴小队……握个手吗？握个手吧！\
**Spathodea**: Alright, join my Revival Squad. Handshake? Handshake.

**爱兹拉**：那我……\
**Ezra**: Then I ...

**可燃点**：不，你不行！\
**Spathodea**: No, not you!

可燃点快速地缩回了被窝中，拖出一小段残影。\
Spathodea retracts her hand away from the burrito, in a movement so fast it blurs.

摇曳的水面之上，被推散的漂浮球们相互挂连在一起，你与我，我与你，簇拥着漂向泳池的更深处去了。\
On the choppy water, several buoy balls are connected together. They are floating towards the depths of the pool hand in hand.

## RUG-06 涅槃日 / Day of Rebirth

**可燃点**：唔——啊！我看到了！就在前面！\
**Spathodea**: Mmm. Hey! I see it! Over there!

**可燃点**：它真漂亮，比我梦里看见的还要漂亮——\
**Spathodea**: It's beautiful, even more beautiful than the one I saw in my dream.

灰狗巴士衔着烟尘嘟嘟响着远去，将年轻姑娘留在公路边。\
A Grayhound bus closes its doors and drives away, honking and leaving the girls standing by the road in a puff of dust and smoke.

**沙丝绒**：那可是与大堡礁齐名的最佳景观，当然赏心悦目。\
**Desert Flannel**: This is a miracle of nature like the Great Barrier Reef. Of course, it's pleasing to the eye.

**沙丝绒**：无数人为了它，顶着一股热风，从爱丽丝泉专门乘着巴士来这儿遭罪。\
**Desert Flannel**: Many would wrestle with the heatwave and travel all the way here from Alice Spring by bus.

沙丝绒放下墨镜，撩开拂过面颊的长发。\
Desert Flannel puts down her sunglasses on her head and flips her hair over her face.

**沙丝绒**：哈……但我不能否认，它确实值得人们来这儿受点苦。\
**Desert Flannel**: Hah. I have to admit, it is worth the effort.

**维尔汀**：到了中午，这里会变得更热。\
**Vertin**: The temperature here will get even higher at noon.

**维尔汀**：爱兹拉准备的医药包中有足量的降温口服片和饮用水，如果不幸中暑，我们还有虎皮鹦鹉羽套作应急手段。\
**Vertin**: Ezra has prepared plenty of Cooling Tablets and water in the medical kit for us. If anyone still suffers sunstroke, we also have the Budgerigar Coat as an emergency measure.

**可燃点**：爱兹拉出发之前叫你去那个房间，就是为了交代这些？\
**Spathodea**: So that's why Ezra took you to the room before we left? To tell you all these?

**维尔汀**：爱兹拉很担心你，还有我们。\
**Vertin**: Ezra is worried about you, and so are we.

**可燃点**：……唔。\
**Spathodea**: Hmph.

**沙丝绒**：哈……这下有人开始为自己说的话后悔了～\
**Desert Flannel**: Ooh. Someone is feeling bad about what she said earlier.

**沙丝绒**：实话说，那个人类小姑娘绝非坏心，只是说话做事过于直白，但那份饱满的付出心理，说是天使也不算过分——\
**Desert Flannel**: If you ask me, that human girl has a good heart. Maybe she can work on her ways of communicating with people, but that altruism in her is almost angel-like.

**沙丝绒**：而且她也的确长得就像个小天使，如果带上她一起去拍亲子广告或许会赚得不少，没错，我回去就问问她愿不愿意挣外快……\
**Desert Flannel**: And she has the face of a little angel. Wouldn't be such a bad idea to put her in some baby care commercials. I heard those things pay you generously. I might as well ask what she thinks.

**维尔汀**：嗯？\
**Vertin**: Huh?

**火苗**：向前走。\
**Flame**: Go forward.

**可燃点**：……啊！它又说话了！\
**Spathodea**: Wow! It's talking again!

**沙丝绒**：什么？什么东西说话了？\
**Desert Flannel**: What? Who's talking again?

**可燃点**：是火苗啊！火苗说话了——你没听到吗？\
**Spathodea**: The flame! It's talking! Didn't you hear it?!

**沙丝绒**：在我听来，这团火和昨天没什么差别……它只是燃烧，然后像我死去的老爸活着时那样打鼾。\
**Desert Flannel**: Nah, it sounds the same to me. This is just the sound of fire burning, snoring, like my late old man.

**沙丝绒**：当然，如果你关掉它的电视，它就会立刻跳起来说“我还在看呢”也说不定。\
**Desert Flannel**: Well, maybe you can also try turning off this little thingy's TV. Maybe it will jump up and shout "I'm still watching."

**可燃点**：我没和你开玩笑！它真的说话了，你听——\
**Spathodea**: I'm not joking! It's really talking! Listen!

可燃点双手托着火团，用力将其送往沙丝绒耳边。\
Lifting the flame with both of her hands, Spathodea puts it as close to Desert Flannel's ear as possible.

**火苗**：……\
**Flame**: ...

诡异的沉默中，沙丝绒的脸愈加拧在一起。\
Desert Flannel looks more and more alarmed in the silence.

**沙丝绒**：等等……这东西好像真的越来越烫了，它在变……形？变得像是一个火箭似……\
**Desert Flannel**: Wait. Its temperature has gone up, and ... it's transforming? What is this, a rocket?

**火苗**：急切不等人。\
**Flame**: No more waiting.

**可燃点**：呜哇——！\
**Spathodea**: Whoa!

红色的火光一闪，热浪拍打着额头与鼻尖，滚烫的火团如同离弦之箭般冲往沙漠的另一端。\
As swift as an arrow, the burning fireball radiating heat waves flies towards the other side of the desert.

**可燃点**：别动，等等！你要去哪儿啊——？！\
**Spathodea**: Hey, hang on! Where are you going?!

**可燃点**：我还以为我们是好朋友呢，你这就不要我了吗！！\
**Spathodea**: I thought we were good friends! Are you ditching me already?!

敏捷灵巧的可燃点第一个跟上了火的步伐。\
The agile Spathodea is the first to catch up with the flame.

向后看去，远处的公路边灰狗巴士正第二次启动前行。\
Behind them, the Grayhound bus in the distance is starting again.

**维尔汀**：……留心些，跟上！\
**Vertin**: Everyone, mind your steps and keep up!

**沙丝绒**：在沙漠里搞赛跑比赛，没人比你们更富有创造性了。\
**Desert Flannel**: A race in the desert. Great. I wonder why I'm not as clever and creative as you are.

吵闹的人群远去，重返宁静的沙地上，纤细的身影从树木后探出头来。\
The noisy crowd has gone. Where they once were, a slim figure pops out of a tree.

**爱兹拉**：维尔汀小姐……是在和我说话吗？她似乎总是看着我的方向，难道是已经发现了我正在跟踪……\
**Ezra**: Ms. Vertin ... Was she talking to me? She always looks over, perhaps she knows that I'm following them.

**爱兹拉**：不……不应该。我隐藏得很好。她们不可能发现我的。\
**Ezra**: But ... no. I'm hiding well. They shouldn't know.

喃喃自语着，爱兹拉在手中的笔记本上画下一个火焰图案。\
Mumbling, Ezra sketches a fire pattern into his notebook.

**爱兹拉**：情绪动荡、冲动，对新复苏的记忆具有皈依狂热心理……还有迫切的、难以阻挡的想要“返回故土”的情绪特征。\
**Ezra**: Having emotional turmoil, acting impulsively, feeling fanatical about the retrieved memories ... and the unstoppable urge to return to the "homeland."

**爱兹拉**：这些都与研究笔记中的内容一一对应。\
**Ezra**: These all match the description in the research notes.

**爱兹拉**：而现在，至关重要的火团显现出强烈的活性……\
**Ezra**: And now, the fire, which is also the key in this case, is burning vigorously.

**爱兹拉**：……没有了。关于“轮回者”的研究止步于此，这之后对我们来说的只有未知。\
**Ezra**: The notes end here. That's all we know about "reincarnators."

抬起头，望向更远处，爱兹拉由一片树荫游走至另一丛灌木中。\
Looking up into the distance, Ezra walks from one bush to another.

**爱兹拉**：没有数据支撑我无法做出更多推断，但未知是最危险也最新奇的东西，它可能诞生大灾难，也可能孕育奇迹……\
**Ezra**: I can't deduce more based on the current data, but at the same time, the unknown can be dangerous yet exciting. It might bring about catastrophes or miracles.

**爱兹拉**：正如……正如神秘学家一样，富有魅力，而且充满生命力。\
**Ezra**: Just like arcanists, so charming and lively.

**爱兹拉**：而我要做的事就是帮助他们，保护他们，好不让这些灼手的火焰熄灭……正如妈妈说的一样，这就是我们人类的使命。\
**Ezra**: My job is to help and protect them, so their burning enthusiasm will not be dampened. Like what Mom said, this is our mission as mankind.

年轻的人类孩子又一次翻开自己检查了无数次的背包。\
The human child once again opens the backpack and checks it for the 1,001st time.

**爱兹拉**：环形跳蛙菌、仙女环粉末、蝶状大啡菇……很好，都很齐全。这一次，我已经做好了应对危险的准备。\
**Ezra**: The Annular Jumper Frog Mushroom, the Fairy Ring Powders, and the Butterfly-shaped Portobello Mushroom ... Very well, I have them all. This time, I'm prepared for any danger.

**可燃点**：嘿！我抓住你了，这下你跑不动了吧——\
**Spathodea**: Hah! Gotcha! You are not running away from ...

**火苗**：旅途的，起点……正是此处。\
**Flame**: This is ... the beginning ... of the journey.

**可燃点**：旅途的起点？不，我们的起点是墨尔本，我们是从那儿出发的！\
**Spathodea**: Beginning of the journey? No, we set off from Melbourne!

**可燃点**：这儿是乌卢鲁的脚下，这几乎是我们的终……\
**Spathodea**: We're close to Uluru now, so it's almost our destin- ...

**可燃点**：……天啊，这都是什么啊？\
**Spathodea**: Gosh, what are these?

**维尔汀**：这些是壁画……不，这些是壁雕，所有痕迹都是镌刻而成的。\
**Vertin**: These are murals. No, they are reliefs. All the marks are carved out of the wall.

**维尔汀**：它们比壁画的历史更为古老，也更为粗糙……\
**Vertin**: These carvings existed long before any murals, and they are rougher.

**沙丝绒**：那是当然的了，我们捉起画笔鼓捣颜料是什么时候，用石头在墙壁上涂涂画画——又是什么时候？\
**Desert Flannel**: Of course, they are. Just think, when did our ancestors learn to draw with paints? And when did they start carving with sharp stones?

**可燃点**：它们真漂亮，就像是星星一样，一个接一个的圆圈套在一起……\
**Spathodea**: They are beautiful, like star trails, one circle in another.

**可燃点**：我想我见过这些东西，它们让我感觉很……熟悉，还让我感到口渴。你们看，这个圈就像是一个泉眼……\
**Spathodea**: I think I've seen them before. They feel familiar and make me thirsty at the same time. Look, this circle is just like a spring.

**沙丝绒**：我们不需要找泉眼，我们有水，你可以尽管去喝——\
**Desert Flannel**: We don't need a spring. We brought water ourselves. Drink as much as you want.

**沙丝绒**：嗯……你们瞧，这些八成是远古的遗迹，这里刻着动物，这里又刻着植物！\
**Desert Flannel**: Hmm. Look here. These are most probably some ancient relics. This one looks like an animal, and this, a plant!

**沙丝绒**：嗯？这是什么，这是一只小鸟儿吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Emm? And what is this, a birdy?

**维尔汀**：这和他们的生活有关，这些标记一定代表着什么……\
**Vertin**: They have something to do with people's lives. These marks have to mean something.

**维尔汀**：也许我们能通过它们找到乌卢鲁运动场的入口。\
**Vertin**: Maybe they will lead us to the entrance to the Stadium.

**沙丝绒**：这时候，可燃点的意见可比我们重要多了，来吧，我的钥匙姑娘，来看看这个——\
**Desert Flannel**: This is the time when Spathodea's opinion matters more than ours. Come, key girl, take a look at this.

说着口渴的可燃点无影无踪，水杯跌落在地上，不知滚了几圈，沾满沙土。热砂无声地吞吸着淌出的冷水。\
But they can't find the girl who was talking about her thirst anywhere. The water leaking from the fallen dusty-covered cup is absorbed into the hot sand.

**沙丝绒**：可燃点？她……去哪儿了？\
**Desert Flannel**: Spathodea? Where, where did she go?

**沙丝绒**：还有那团火，那团火——他们都不见了！\
**Desert Flannel**: And that fire, they are all gone!

**沙丝绒**：该死！这又是耍什么花样，她最好只是在恶作剧……我刚刚还在我背后听见她的脚步声——\
**Desert Flannel**: What the hell is going on again? She'd better be pulling a prank on me. I heard her footsteps behind me just now.

**维尔汀**：别紧张，沙丝绒。我们还有一个帮手。\
**Vertin**: Relax, Desert Flannel. We've got help.

树影后，一个人影迈步走出。\
A slim figure emerges from behind the tree.

**沙丝绒**：爱兹拉？你——你是什么时候来，不……你是从什么时候开始跟着我们的？\
**Desert Flannel**: Ezra? How, how did you get here? Wait, how long have you been following us?

**爱兹拉**：很早，我从医院就跟着你们了……抱歉，沙丝绒小姐，请让我先看看这个——\
**Ezra**: From the beginning, when you were at the hospital. Sorry, Ms. Desert Flannel, please let me check this first.

快走几步，爱兹拉拧着眉毛，靠近了充满印记的墙壁。\
Ezra frowns, quickening his pace when nearing the wall of reliefs.

手指碾压沙土，小朵蘑菇在挤压下碎成几块，散发出辛辣的菌菇气味。\
Some mushrooms break into pieces under the pressure and release a pungent scent of spores.

**爱兹拉**：这个味道……不会有错，这就是恶魔刺角菌。\
**Ezra**: This smell ... I can't be wrong—This is Devil's Thorn.

**沙丝绒**：那是什么？和可燃点的失踪有关系吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: What's that? Does it have anything to do with her missing?

**爱兹拉**：一种生长在沙漠中的罕见菌种，据说与蜥蜴有着血缘关系。我过去只在书本里见过它的照片。\
**Ezra**: A rare kind of mushroom that grows in the desert. Allegedly, it's genetically connected to lizards. I've only seen its pictures in books.

**爱兹拉**：菌伞宽阔，带有尖刺，而根部如同海绵，能够保存与吸取地下水分，这种蘑菇往往只出现在水源附近，加上这个螺旋形态的图案……\
**Ezra**: It has wide, open pileus with sharp spikes, and its roots are as absorbent as sponge, which allows it to absorb and preserve underground water. They only appear around water sources, and with this spiral pattern on the wall, I think ...

**爱兹拉**：我想，我或许有办法找到可燃点小姐。\
**Ezra**: I think I might have a way to find her.

**爱兹拉**：爱兹拉站起身体，从口袋中抽出那只金属制的寻水杖。\
**Ezra**: Ezra stands up and takes out a metal dowsing rod from his pocket.

**爱兹拉**：请跟我来。\
**Ezra**: Please come with me.

干渴，由内而外的干渴。如同此生从未饮用过泉水，也如同疲于奔命的荒野兽群。\
Thirst. She felt the dry thirst throughout her body. As if she had never taken even a single sip of water, or she was a beast that must keep running and running for its survival.

视线内的漆黑中，一丛火光呼地燃起。\
A gout of flame pierces through the formless dark.

**可燃点**：火……苗？\
**Spathodea**: Little flame?

**可燃点**：咳——咳咳，我的嗓子……好疼，好渴……\
**Spathodea**: *coughs* My throat ... It hurts ... Water ...

**火苗**：你还记得我吗？\
**Flame**: Do you remember me?

火焰澎湃跳动，逐渐逼近。如同一颗鲜活的心。\
The fire pulses and comes closer to her, like a beating heart.

**火苗**：我穿越漫长的河水、干涸、雨季与如瀑的水滴，这才来到你身边。\
**Flame**: I traveled through the endless flood, drought, rain, and waterfalls to finally reach you.

**火苗**：你还记得我吗？\
**Flame**: Do you remember me?

**可燃点**：我……\
**Spathodea**: I ...

干涸的喉咙深处如同卧着青蛙一般咕咕打颤。\
Her dry throat keeps twitching as if a toad was resting there.

**可燃点**：我记得，但不……我不记得——\
**Spathodea**: I do, but ... not really ...

**可燃点**：我不记得你的名字，不记得你的脸……但我记得……\
**Spathodea**: I can't recall your name or your face, but I do remember ...

手脚一起发热，如同化身为火中的柴芯一般蜷缩起身体。\
She curls up in a tight ball. Her palms and feet getting hotter and hotter.

**火苗**：你还记得你如何与我争吵吗？\
**Flame**: Do you remember our fight?

滚烫的火焰与雨水一同浇灌在年轻姑娘的脊梁之上。\
The boiling raindrops mixed with fire are splashed on her spine.

它们混杂在一起，滚入她干涸的喉管。\
Together, they pour into her dry throat.

**可燃点**：……呜！\
**Spathodea**: Ugh!

她无法确定自己是站立或是爬行在地面上，只能大口喘息。\
She is not sure if she is standing or crawling on the ground. The only thing she can do is breathe like a fish.

火焰顺着耳后流淌到她的眼前，带来一个温暖的拥抱。\
The fire flows from the back of her ears to her eyes, like a warm hug from behind.

**可燃点**：“以此刻的感受作为锚点，于漫长的网罗中探寻。”\
**Spathodea**: "Weigh the anchor of the current feelings and seek in the boundless net."

她听见与她不同的声音从自己的喉咙中滚出。\
She hears a different voice coming from her own throat.

**可燃点**：“寻着我，寻着往日，寻着我们需要寻着的灵智与精神。”\
**Spathodea**: "Seek me, seek the past, seek the intelligence and spirit we are bound to find."

**可燃点**：我不愿再与你和好了！你是一团愚笨的火焰！\
**Spathodea**: I don't wanna make up with you! You dumb ball of fire!

**可燃点**：“我也不想再和你说话，你只是一个傻乎乎的姑娘！”\
**Spathodea**: "Neither do I, you stupid girl!"

**可燃点**：我感到双手滚烫，如同探入炉火。\
**Spathodea**: My hands are burning, like they are soaked in fire.

**可燃点**：“那是你探入我，你与我争吵，我们互相抓挠对方，像是两只猫儿。”\
**Spathodea**: "That's because you reached into me. We had a fight, attacking each other with nails like two cats."

**可燃点**：啊啊——这正如同，我第一次见到你那天！\
**Spathodea**: Ah! This is just like the day we first met!

心中的画面更加明朗，记忆中的线头落在眼前。\
The scene in her mind becomes clear. She can see the clue of this ancient memory within her reach.

**可燃点**：我又感到我的双膝战战，咯咯作响。\
**Spathodea**: I can feel my knees trembling again.

**可燃点**：我知道那是什么。那是一种小把戏，一种无法登入商业比赛，也不能作为职业运动的项目。\
**Spathodea**: I know this game, a sport which is not popular enough to be included in any commercial or professional games.

**可燃点**：那是我每天午后挤出时间偷偷练习的、灯泡堆中的光点，马林吉的收获——不，不对。\
**Spathodea**: It's also the sport for which I've been secretly training myself every day after lunch—the light-bulbs-picking game, Malingee's Harvest ... No, no.

**可燃点**：在我的家里，从没有那样滚烫的篝火，而是……在这里。\
**Spathodea**: But these are not light bulbs for the athletes to pick up from the ground, but fire ... And I don't have such a burning campfire at home. It can only be found here.

**可燃点**：在泉水旁，在星空下，在炙热的沙地之上，我看见滚烫的火堆，与四射的星点……\
**Spathodea**: Beside the flowing spring, under the starry sky, on the scorching sand, I saw the burning campfire and the sparks scattering in all directions.

**可燃点**：我双手都是滚烫的火焰，一次次抚摸内焰，与无数欢声笑语一起，我从空中俯冲而下——\
**Spathodea**: My hands surrounded by blazing flames, I touched the inner cone again and again as I flew by. Immersed in great joy, I dove down from the air.

**可燃点**：“那时候，我们的手曾在火中交握。”\
**Spathodea**: "At that time, our hands held each other in the flames."

**可燃点**：“我们的行迹，曾从一枚火种蔓延到另一枚火种……”\
**Spathodea**: "Our traces went on from one torch to another."

**可燃点**：是的，我明白，我想起来了——\
**Spathodea**: Yes, I know. I remember it now.

**可燃点**：我也曾在那里饮用泉中的冷水，将七彩色的布条缠满四肢，我歌唱与舞蹈，直至满是皱纹的双手抚上我的额头……\
**Spathodea**: I once drank the cold water in the spring and covered my limbs with colorful strips. I sang and danced until a pair of wrinkled hands touched my forehead.

漆黑的洞窟深处，一名老者步履蹒跚地走出。\
An elderly man staggers to his feet and rises from the depths of the dark cave.

**老祭司**：好孩子，我的好孩子……\
**Priest**: Good girl, my good girl ...

**老祭司**：你赢得了比赛，你的双手沾满尘土，你的灵魂却闪闪发亮。是你为我们寻得了最灼热的火，与它交好，与它相接。\
**Priest**: Your hands are dusted, but you win the game, and your soul is sparkling. It's you who find the hottest fire for us! It's you who connect to it and make friends with it!

**老祭司**：我将授予你权柄，给予你高台。\
**Priest**: I shall grant you the scepter and lead you to the highest platform.

**可燃点**：我将成为乌卢鲁神殿的祭司。\
**Spathodea**: I shall become the next Priestess of the Uluru Temple.

**可燃点**：我为红土上的每一滴汗水尽责，我颂赞所有伟大而公正的竞技。\
**Spathodea**: I shall take responsibility for every drop of sweat on the red soil, and I shall eulogize all the significant, fair competitions.

**可燃点**：我会将这火种保存于我的口中，胃中，心中与肋骨之中。\
**Spathodea**: I shall store the flame in my mouth, my stomach, my heart, and my ribs.

**可燃点**：我会守护它。不叫它熄灭。不叫它遗失。不叫它离去。\
**Spathodea**: I shall protect her, not to let her extinguish, nor to let her go astray or away.

**可燃点**：我在此起誓……\
**Spathodea**: I hereby swear ...

**可燃点**：我将与乌卢鲁运动会同在。直至……永永远远。\
**Spathodea**: I shall be with the Uluru Games, until ... forever.

**可燃点**：我……我妈妈……\
**Spathodea**: M-Mom ...

**可燃点**：可从来都没和我说过……我我我们家有喷火红龙的血统呀……\
**Spathodea**: M-M-Mom never told me ... w-w-we are descendants of the Red Dragon ...

**守卫魔精**：吼吼——！！！\
**Critter**: *roars*

**可燃点**：呜啊——？！我，我醒来了……这儿是，啊，是运动场的入口！\
**Spathodea**: Ah?! I-I'm awake now. This is the entrance to the Stadium!

**可燃点**：那这个声音，应该就是——\
**Spathodea**: Then that howl must be ...

瘫软在地的姑娘猛地弯身，就地翻滚一圈，躲开了袭来的利爪。\
The girl bends and rolls on the ground in a circle to avoid the sharp claws' attack.

**可燃点**：是运动场的守卫者……！咳，咳咳……\
**Spathodea**: The guardians of the Stadium, I knew it! *coughs*

**可燃点**：身体……还在发软！这下糟糕了，我总不能就这么滚着打败它们啊……！\
**Spathodea**: I'm too weary to stand up! Shoot, there's no way I can beat them just rolling around!

**爱兹拉**：可燃点小姐！\
**Ezra**: Ms. Spathodea!

**可燃点**：爱——爱兹拉？！还有沙丝绒，维尔汀！\
**Spathodea**: E-Ezra?! And Desert Flannel, Vertin!

**可燃点**：太好了！你们找到我了……！\
**Spathodea**: Thank goodness you found me!

**爱兹拉**：这些魔精——和我所知的任何魔精都不一样，它们到底……\
**Ezra**: These critters—they don't look like any kind that I know of. What are they ...

**守卫魔精**：嘶哈——\
**Critter**: *hiss*

硕大的石块抛向可燃点，她顺势向前滚翻一圈，稳稳当当地趴在了掩体后。\
Facing the boulders thrown by the critters, Spathodea does a forward roll and hides behind a shelter.

**可燃点**：它们是乌卢鲁运动场的守卫魔精！情况复杂，现在没时间和你们解释了，我们得先对付这些家伙！\
**Spathodea**: These critters are the guardians of the Stadium! They are ... Ugh, I can explain it later. We have to deal with them first!

**可燃点**：嗯？火苗？！火苗——你上去做什么呀！\
**Spathodea**: Hmm? Little flame?! Hey! What are you doing?!

小小的火苗飘飘荡荡地迎向怪物。\
The little flame floats leisurely toward the monsters.

**维尔汀**：来不及了，保护可燃点，进入作战。\
**Vertin**: No time to hesitate. Protect Spathodea and engage!

**爱兹拉**：很好！它们倒下了！\
**Ezra**: Great, they are down!

**爱兹拉**：为确保安全，请大家暂时后退，确认危险排除后再做靠近……\
**Ezra**: Everyone, for the sake of prudence, please stay back and do not approach before confirming the danger has been eliminated.

**可燃点**：不，这里已经没有危险了，你看！\
**Spathodea**: No, there's no more danger now. Look!

涌动的热流从乌卢鲁岩石的顶部滚至脚边的泉眼。\
A heated current of air surges from the top of Uluru Rock to the spring by the people's feet.

守卫魔精残破的躯体之中，骨制的长柄正被火焰吞没。\
Among the remains of a guardian critter, a bone torch is engulfed in the flame.

**火苗**：不必忧愁，不必思虑。\
**Flame**: No need to worry or hesitate.

灼人的热度如暴风一般席卷。\
The scorching heat storms around.

**可燃点**：现在——已经是安全的时候啦！\
**Spathodea**: Now, it's all clear!

**可燃点**：我们长话短说吧，朋友们，我已经找回了许多记忆，至少，我想起了我的身份。\
**Spathodea**: Long story short, mates, I've retrieved many memories. At least now I know who I used to be.

**可燃点**：我曾经的名字叫作“小火”，如同现在我亲近之人所称呼的一样。\
**Spathodea**: My name in the last life was Flammy, exactly what my close ones call me now.

**可燃点**：我还是我，未曾被任何人替代。\
**Spathodea**: I am still ME. I'm not replaced by anyone.

**爱兹拉**：你……还是你，未曾被替代……\
**Ezra**: You are still you, the modern version ...

**爱兹拉**：这是到目前为止的“轮回者”身上都没有出现过的症状——！\
**Ezra**: This has never happened to any "reincarnators" as far as we know!

**可燃点**：因为我与“小火”的相似，也因为我肩负的使命。\
**Spathodea**: That's because Flammy and I are very alike, and we both have the same duty on our shoulders.

**可燃点**：……\
**Spathodea**: ...

**可燃点**：我是小火，我用我的双手从火中摘取圣火，我是有史以来第一届乌卢鲁运动会的践行祭司。\
**Spathodea**: I am Flammy. I obtained the Uluru Flame from the fire with my own hands. I was the first Priestess in the history of the Uluru Games.

**火苗**：我是可燃点，我以我的胸腹部驻留自远古而来的火种，我将成为有史以来最新一届乌卢鲁运动会的践行祭司。\
**Flame**: I am Spathodea. I keep the flame that traveled all the way from the ancient times inside me. I will become the next Priestess in the history of the Uluru Games.

火苗早已不是火苗，它如野兽般满溢，成为一幢魁梧的高楼。\
The flame is no longer the small flame as it was. Now, it is roaring like a beast, rearing up into the sky.

**可燃点**：记得我说过的话吗，朋友们？我的火焰会带领我们无往不利。\
**Spathodea**: Remember what I said, mates? My flame is our compass!

**可燃点**：我妈妈说过，好孩子不会说谎……所以——我总是说到做到！\
**Spathodea**: Mom said good kids never lie. So, I always keep my word!

**可燃点**：可燃点回过头，露出一个胜利般的笑容。\
**Spathodea**: Spathodea looks back and gives them a grin.

她快步向前，跃入火中。\
In an instant, she hurries her pace and jumps into the fire.

## RUG-07 老火种 / The Old Flame

**沙丝绒**：可燃点！可燃点——她，她跑哪儿去了呀！\
**Desert Flannel**: Spathodea! Spathodea! Where, where did she go?!

**？？？**：像是一场漫长的沉睡，如同站在隔板之后观赏花园。\
**???**: It was like a long slumber, or a view of the garden behind the wall.

陌生的声音，夹杂着冷风，吹去浓郁的白雾。\
A new voice is heard coming alongside a gust of cold wind, blowing away the thick steam.

**？？？**：如今，我又一次见着日头。外界又是新的天地。\
**???**: But now, I finally get to see the sun again. The world out there has completely changed.

火焰铸成的人形睁开双眼，眼中仍是火焰。\
The person made of fire opens her eyes. They are also filled with flame.

**？？？**：但你却是不变的，小火，我的好朋友。\
**???**: But you remain the same, Flammy, my dear friend.

**？？？**：你找到我，带走漫长而黝黑的梦境……将我再一次点燃，成为火该有的模样。\
**???**: You found me, and put an end to the long, dark dream. You set me on fire again, bringing me back to what a flame should be like.

**可燃点**：……欢迎来到20世纪末，和平乌鲁。\
**Spathodea**: Welcome to the end of the 20th century, Ulu.

**可燃点**：这里很有趣，有许多新东西，我想我们可以慢慢地再去了解一切有趣儿的东西！\
**Spathodea**: For you, this is an interesting era with many many new things. Well, I think we can learn them together later, one by one!

**可燃点**：而另一边——\
**Spathodea**: While for my dear brave friends ...

**可燃点**：欢迎来到乌卢鲁运动会，我其他的亲爱的、勇敢的好朋友们！\
**Spathodea**: Welcome to the Uluru Games, my dear brave friends!

推动沉重而高大的门扉，更多蓬勃的风从其中涌出。\
The giant heavy gate opens with winds blowing out from inside.

人群先后进入其中，只有爱兹拉，落在了队伍末端，一动也不动。\
The team members go through the gate one after another. Ezra, however, remains still like a statue.

**可燃点**：你还在等什么呢？\
**Spathodea**: What are you waiting for?

**爱兹拉**：乌卢鲁运动场大门的显现源自于一种神奇的神秘学仪式，它的过程比起“召唤”更加近似于“献祭”……\
**Ezra**: The conjuring of the entrance to the Uluru Stadium is sourced from a fantastic arcane ritual. Instead of a summon, it's closer to a sacrifice ...

**爱兹拉**：当然，火苗……或者说“和平乌鲁”也是其中重要的一环，直接关系着“轮回者”的反复出现的火图腾……\
**Ezra**: The fire element also plays an important part in this sacrifice. In Spathodea's case, Ulu is her flame.

**爱兹拉**：这和可燃点小姐身上与众不同的融合反应有关吗？她不同于其余“轮回者”，即使年纪尚小，依然保持了清晰的现世记忆……\
**Ezra**: Will it have anything to do with the unique condition Ms. Spathodea has? Unlike other "reincarnators," she still has a clear memory of this life, despite her young age.

**爱兹拉**：或者说，她的光点二者本就相同，从未经历过变革……而这一切则是因为……\
**Ezra**: Or, it's because that two light spots of hers—the older self and the modern self—are not that different, so she's spared going through any drastic changes, and the reason behind it might be ...

**可燃点**：爱兹拉！！！\
**Spathodea**: Ezra!!!

**爱兹拉**：……！是的，我在！\
**Ezra**: ...! Yes, I'm here!

爱兹拉的眼睛连续眨动几下，如同受惊的动物一般，缓慢地从笔记本中抬起眼睛来。\
Ezra blinks several times, like a frightened animal, slowly looking up from the notebook.

**爱兹拉**：请问你有什么事儿吗……可燃点小姐？\
**Ezra**: What can I do for you, Ms. Spathodea?

**可燃点**：我在等你。\
**Spathodea**: I'm waiting for you.

**爱兹拉**：啊……我明白了。抱歉，我太专注于信息记录了。\
**Ezra**: Ah, I see. Sorry, I was too involved in taking notes.

**爱兹拉**：我会尽快收拾好东西返回拉普拉斯。不过在那之前……\
**Ezra**: I will pack and return to Laplace as soon as possible. But before that ...

四下观望几圈，爱兹拉用力拍了拍自己的胸口。\
After looking around a few times, Ezra pats his chest.

**爱兹拉**：我会把战斗痕迹以及各类孢子痕迹清理干净后再离开的，如果放任不管的话，它们可能会对这里的环境造成改变。\
**Ezra**: I have to clean up the spores and the mess we made in the battle first; otherwise, they may change the environment here.

**可燃点**：……哈！真奇怪！\
**Spathodea**: Oh, c'mon, you weirdo!

**可燃点**：你怎么又要走了？我真是从来都搞不明白你这个古怪的家伙！\
**Spathodea**: You're leaving now, after all our effort? I can never understand you!

**爱兹拉**：你不是在等我离开吗？\
**Ezra**: Aren't you waiting for me to leave?

**可燃点**：当然不是了！我在等你过来，和我们一起进入运动场！\
**Spathodea**: Of course not! I'm waiting for you to join us. We'll go into the Stadium together!

**可燃点**：我……\
**Spathodea**: I ...

**可燃点**：我陷入混乱，一会儿口渴，一会儿又无所不能。我陷入幻觉，紧接着，我又消失不见，最后如你所见，我昏倒在了地上……\
**Spathodea**: Come to think about what I have suffered: coma, hallucination, confusion, thirst, misconception that I was almighty, and then, as you can see, I fell into a coma again after my sudden disappearance.

**可燃点**：我想你说得很对，我是需要一个随行医生的！\
**Spathodea**: I think you're right. I do need a doctor by my side!

**爱兹拉**：可是，人类是无法进入乌卢鲁运动场的，我们都知——哇啊！\
**Ezra**: But mankind cannot enter the Stadium. We all know thaaaaaat ...!

一阵忽如其来的拉力将爱兹拉拽入门中。\
An arm suddenly yanks Ezra into the gate.

**可燃点**：哎呀！真啰嗦！它过去还从来都没出现在人类眼前过呢！\
**Spathodea**: Ugh blah blah blah! Please, the Stadium has never shown itself to any humans before!

**可燃点**：如果看到一块给你的蛋糕，就乖乖吃掉那块蛋糕！\
**Spathodea**: When life gives you cake, just dig right in!

最后的小姑娘跃入门中，而后，恢弘的大门咔地一声闭合。\
After the girl hops through it, the magnificent gate closes with a mighty snap.

**爱兹拉**：天啊，这就是……乌卢鲁运动场？\
**Ezra**: Strewth! This is the Uluru Stadium?

**维尔汀**：这儿比我想的更漂亮，也更……令人感到舒适和愉快。\
**Vertin**: It's even more splendid than I thought, and ... more comfortable and pleasing.

**爱兹拉**：舒适和愉快？\
**Ezra**: Comfortable and pleasing?

**爱兹拉**：我并没有这样的感觉——\
**Ezra**: I don't feel the same way as you do.

爱兹拉前进几步，又缓慢而认真地呼吸了几次。\
Ezra takes a few steps ahead and matches them with deep breaths.

**爱兹拉**：并不是说这里不美丽宜人，相反这里充满了魅力，可我的身体并没有任何特殊的感受……\
**Ezra**: But not in the sense that this place doesn't look beautiful to me, on the contrary, it's stunning, but physically I don't feel anything special.

**沙丝绒**：或许是因为你是人类吧，嘿，等一下！\
**Desert Flannel**: Maybe because you're a human. Hey, wait!

**爱兹拉**：唔！小心，别跑得这样快——沙丝绒小姐，你会跌倒的！\
**Ezra**: Mmm! Not so fast, be careful! Ms. Desert Flannel, you will fall!

**沙丝绒**：不会的，不会的～\
**Desert Flannel**: I won't, I won't!

沙丝绒拉开身体，猛地发力，如同离弦之箭般冲向早已跑到运动场另一端的可燃点。\
Desert Flannel stretches herself and suddenly steps firmly on the ground, running like an arrow toward Spathodea, who has already reached the other end of the field.

**沙丝绒**：我现在身体轻盈，比刚刚吃了牛排和生日蛋糕还精力充沛！\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm feeling as light as the wind and even more energetic than when I finished a big meal of steak and cakes!

**沙丝绒**：我什么时候跌倒，都不会现在跌倒！\
**Desert Flannel**: I may fall anytime anywhere, but not now, not here!

**和平乌鲁**：这正是神秘学家该有的感受。\
**Ulu**: This is exactly what arcanists should feel.

**爱兹拉**：和平乌鲁小姐！啊……抱歉，我可以这样称呼你吗？\
**Ezra**: Ms. Ulu! Ah, pardon me. May I call you that?

**和平乌鲁**：如果你愿意的话，孩子。\
**Ulu**: Go ahead if you want, child.

**和平乌鲁**：但是最好可以称呼我为女士。因为我比你们都长几岁。而另一方面，我是这场运动会最为神圣的火种……唔？！\
**Ulu**: But of course, I would appreciate it if you call me Madam, since I'm a few hundred years older than all of you. Besides, I am the most sacred flame of the Games ... Hmm?!

**可燃点**：哈！是我先跑回来啦！好久没跑得这么畅快了——！\
**Spathodea**: Hah! I won! Been a long time since I had so much fun running!

打断了谈话，可燃点脸上毫无歉意，探头探脑地询问起来。\
Despite interrupting the conversation, Spathodea seems unfazed and keeps asking questions endlessly.

**可燃点**：和平乌鲁！那边的草地是怎么回事呀？过去是没有的！还有那些椅子！\
**Spathodea**: Ulu! Is that a lawn? We didn't have anything like that before! And those benches!

**和平乌鲁**：事事都会改变，小火。\
**Ulu**: Things change, Flammy.

**和平乌鲁**：在你离去后的千百年中，乌卢鲁运动会发生了无数改变。\
**Ulu**: In the past hundreds of years when you were absent, countless changes happened to the Uluru Games.

**和平乌鲁**：它为自己长出绿茵，不知不觉地添置了椅子，但这都不是人所为的。\
**Ulu**: New lawns and benches had somehow appeared in the Stadium, but none of these changes was made by arcanists.

**和平乌鲁**：人所带来的是新比赛项目，新的规则，政府与官方加入的管理。那些才是乌卢鲁运动会真正的改变。\
**Ulu**: Those actually made by arcanists were new events, new rules, and new management. These are the changes that really made the Uluru Games different.

**可燃点**：原来如此，怪不得我在回忆中从没有见过冰上平衡竞走的画面！嗯，也没有投石占卜和新型铁人十三项……\
**Spathodea**: I see. No wonder I've never seen Ice Racewalking in my memories! Let me see, so there was no Stone Throw Divination or New Tridecathlon either ...

**爱兹拉**：冰上平衡竞走并不是澳大利亚的传统运动项目，它来自于北欧，在多数气候寒冷的国家流行。\
**Ezra**: Ice Racewalking is not a traditional sport in Australia. It originated from Northern Europe and became popular in cold countries.

**和平乌鲁**：没错，冰上平衡竞走于1926年被引入乌卢鲁运动会。\
**Ulu**: That's right. Ice Racewalking was introduced to the Games in 1926.

**和平乌鲁**：如果我没记错的话，那是圣洛夫基金会做出的提议。他们希望以此展示运动会的世界性与包容性，另一方面……\
**Ulu**: If my memory serves me well, it was introduced by the St. Pavlov Foundation. On one hand, they hoped to show the internationality and inclusiveness of the Games; on the other ...

**爱兹拉**：另一方面？\
**Ezra**: On the other?

**和平乌鲁**：另一方面……它替代了火中竞速赛。\
**Ulu**: Well ... it took the place of Fire Racewalking.

**爱兹拉**：原来如此，我看过一些资料……在20世纪初，圣洛夫基金会接管乌卢鲁运动会后，取消了许多难度较高、危险性较大的项目。\
**Ezra**: I see, I read it somewhere before. At the beginning of the 20th century, after St. Pavlov Foundation took over the Uluru Games, some challenging and relatively dangerous sports were canceled.

**爱兹拉**：也是在那之后，乌卢鲁运动会的关注度逐渐走低，各项目的参赛选手也连年减少……\
**Ezra**: This was also the turning point of the Uluru Games. From then on, the Games declined in popularity, and fewer and fewer athletes came each year.

**可燃点**：哼，他们那些人……不……是那些笨家伙！他们根本就不懂神秘学家运动会的真谛！\
**Spathodea**: Humph, these people ... No, these idiots! They know nothing about the essence of arcanists' sporting event!

**可燃点**：哪有神秘学家会在火中竞速中烫伤自己的双脚呢，人人都知道，只要你相信你不会被灼伤，那些火焰就不会灼伤你！\
**Spathodea**: Where on earth can you find an arcanist who would burn their own legs in Fire Racewalking?! Everyone knows you'll be fine as long as you believe the fire is harmless!

**爱兹拉**：但……从理性逻辑来说，火焰的确是危险的。\
**Ezra**: But, in point of fact, fire is dangerous.

爱兹拉小声回复，并昂起头，左转右转地打量起透天的屋顶。\
Ezra replies in a whisper and looks up, checking the roof from left to right.

**可燃点**：可是……让现在的我想来，也真不可思议！和平乌鲁你的脾气这么火爆，居然允许他们取消你最喜欢的项目——\
**Spathodea**: But think about it. It's unbelievable! Given your short fuse, I can't believe you just let them cancel your favorite event, Ulu.

**爱兹拉**：脾气……火爆？\
**Ezra**: Short ... fuse?

**可燃点**：嗯！没错！她的脾气最大啦，就像是她的身体一样！熊熊燃烧呢！\
**Spathodea**: Yeah, you heard it right! She's got the hottest temper! Burns like herself!

**和平乌鲁**：咳——咳咳咳！！！\
**Ulu**: Ahem! AHEM!!!

**和平乌鲁**：事事都会改变的！小火！我——已经度过了千年有余的岁月，我早不是过去与你一样年轻的我了！\
**Ulu**: Things change, Flammy! I ... have already spent over a thousand years in this world. I'm no longer the young, hotheaded flame of your age!

**和平乌鲁**：哪怕大家的祖母恐怕也得称呼我为奶奶了！\
**Ulu**: Even your grandmother should call me Grandma now!

**可燃点**：……奶奶？因为变成了奶奶，连自己最喜欢的项目都要让别人抢走了吗？我不明白！\
**Spathodea**: Grandma? So they can just take away your favorite event just because you're old now? I don't understand!

走开几步，可燃点气愤地握紧了拳头。\
Walking a few steps away, Spathodea clenches her fists in anger.

**可燃点**：但现在我回来了！乌卢鲁运动会是时候回到神秘学家手中了！让我们重新制定一套属于神秘学家的比赛条目吧！\
**Spathodea**: Anyway, Flammy is back! It's time arcanists took back the Uluru Games from the Foundation! Let's design a new list of events that fit real arcanists!

**可燃点**：就从火中竞速赛开始，这里还有木头，和平乌鲁可以把它们变成火堆……\
**Spathodea**: We'll start from Fire Racewalking. There are woods here. Ulu can start some bonfires with them ...

**沙丝绒**：圣洛夫基金会会同意你这么做吗？他们看起来可没那么好说话。\
**Desert Flannel**: Will the Foundation agree to this? They seem difficult to deal with.

**爱兹拉**：想从基金会手中拿走运动会很难，但如果准备好充足的安全设施，再通过拉普拉斯科算中心的窗口进行申请承办……\
**Ezra**: It's hard to take it over from the Foundation, but if we have all the security-related facilities prepared, and apply to host the event through Laplace Scientific Computing Center ...

**维尔汀**：配合可燃点的身份，我们并非全无机会。\
**Vertin**: Considering Spathodea's identity, we do stand a chance.

**维尔汀**：但我们将要应对的文书工作……\
**Vertin**: But the paperwork we are going to deal with ...

**可燃点**：哎呀！哎——呀！你们可不能在神圣的乌卢鲁运动场里谈论工作！\
**Spathodea**: Oh, c'mon! COME ON! You are not supposed to talk about paperwork in the sacred Uluru Stadium!

**可燃点**：比起一群身体羸弱，爬不上几层台阶就气喘吁吁的精英纸片人，我们现在更需要的是一群杰出的运动健将来帮助我实验火中竞速赛！\
**Spathodea**: Instead of a bunch of weak office workers who would pant from climbing a few stairs, what I need is some real athletes who can help me complete the Fire Racewalking!

**可燃点**：他们活跃，充满能量，性格可爱或是古怪，而且各个都得是神秘学家！这样才能玩好这个项目——\
**Spathodea**: I don't mind whether they are cute or weird, I only need them to be energetic! This is the only thing we ask of athletes in this sport ...

**沙丝绒**：不错的想法。唯一不足的就是我们正处于沙漠中央，人迹罕至之地。\
**Desert Flannel**: Great idea. But the only inconvenience is that we are in the middle of the desert, a place where only flies visit.

**沙丝绒**：而我的电话簿中——只有客户、客户、客户，还有被我放了鸽子的客户，我们上哪儿去找这么多人呢？\
**Desert Flannel**: And as I checked my contact list, I saw only ... client, client, and client ... the ordinary ones and the ones I once stood up. Where are we going to find the athletes?

**维尔汀**：有意思。我恰好认识许多符合你需求的人。\
**Vertin**: Well, I happen to know many arcanists who meet your need.

**维尔汀**：他们现在也在这里。\
**Vertin**: And they happen to be here right now.

**可燃点**：嗯？那我怎么瞧不见他们呢？\
**Spathodea**: What? How come I can't see them anywhere?

**可燃点**：咦……你放下箱子做什么？你要在这儿整理行李吗？\
**Spathodea**: Hmm? Why are you opening the suitcase? Are you gonna organize your stuff here?

手提箱展开，平铺在地面上，沿着边沿敲击两下，里头的回声清晰可闻。\
Open the suitcase, place it on the ground, and knock on the edge. A knocking sound echoes in the black space.

**维尔汀**：有谁想要出来感受一下新鲜空气吗？\
**Vertin**: Anyone care to have some fresh air?

大家围着箱子，神情愈发地困惑。可燃点张了张嘴，数次欲言又止。\
The other three standing around the suitcase look more puzzled. Spathodea tentatively opens her mouth but shuts it once again.

但是很快，人们就听到了一阵明快而清脆的蹄声——从深不见底的箱内传来。\
Soon a clear clip-clop comes from the bottomless suitcase.

**哒哒达利**：咴呜——！\
**Darley Clatter**: *neigh*

率先冒出的是一袭美丽鬃毛。\
The first thing they see is a silky, shining horse with a mane fluttering in the wind.

**哒哒达利**：多么丰润动人的青草香气呀，带着烟熏的焦香气息！我相信它的味道会比镀金小胡萝卜更好～\
**Darley Clatter**: The fresh smell of grass with smoked fragrance! There is no doubt that it tastes better than gilded carrots!

**哒哒达利**：还有……还有这样一群健壮的皇家护卫！\
**Darley Clatter**: And, look at this army of royal guards!

**哒哒达利**：喁喁～它们一定是来迎接伟大的达利阿拉伯的——呜咴！\
**Darley Clatter**: They must be here to greet the Great Darley Clatter!

**沙丝绒**：皇家护卫？它在说什么玩意儿？啊——等一下，那边浑身是刺的大家伙就是它说的皇家护卫吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Royal guards? What is he saying? Aaah ... no kidding, is that giant creature covered with spikes his "Royal Guard"?

**魔鬼蜥蜴**：吼吼——！！\
**Thorny Lizard**: *roaring*

运动场深处传来低声怒吼。\
A deep, angry roar comes from the depths of the Stadium.

**和平乌鲁**：那是魔鬼蜥蜴，它们从热土中化生，获得了巨大的身姿，为运动员们所骑乘……看来它们沉睡了太久，已不记得主人家的面目。\
**Ulu**: That's the thorny devils, the enormous creatures born in the burning sand of the Stadium. They used to be mounts for the players, but looks like they have forgotten their master after all these years of slumber.

**和平乌鲁**：多说无益，让它们归为尘与土。\
**Ulu**: Enough talk. Let's put them back to dust and ashes.

**沙丝绒**：好，又一次伟大的胜利！献给可燃点小姐！\
**Desert Flannel**: Yes! Another great victory! And I dedicate this win to Ms. Spathodea!

**可燃点**：也献给沙丝绒小姐！\
**Spathodea**: And to Ms. Desert Flannel!

气氛活跃，年轻姑娘们的手在空中碰了一下虚拟的酒杯。\
Surrounded by the fiery atmosphere, the girls raise an invisible glass to each other.

而后，沙丝绒拉着可燃点的手臂高高抬起，对着源源不断冒出新面孔的箱子大声呼唤。\
Desert Flannel grabs Spathodea's wrist and lifts it up like a referee, calling out to the suitcase, out of which more arcanists pour out.

**沙丝绒**：现在——有谁不畏怕火焰，且愿意行走于火中的，请来此报道！\
**Desert Flannel**: Now, people ... those of you who are not afraid of fire and wish to walk among the flames, please register here!

## RUG-08 火警热线 / Triple Zero

**和平乌鲁**：好！做得好！再跑快些，再跳高些！\
**Ulu**: Good! You're doing great! Faster, higher!

奶奶也有疯狂的时候，给她一些时间，她将熊熊燃烧，如同另一枚太阳。\
A grandma can be crazy about sports too. Give her time, and she will burn like the sun.

**可燃点**：太好了！和平乌鲁——你看起来就像是从前我认识的和平乌鲁！\
**Spathodea**: Yes! Ulu, you are exactly the Ulu I knew in my memory!

**可燃点**：火中行走竞速、闪现400米短跑、飞跃树梢与马林吉的收获……我们已经实践了这样多的项目了！\
**Spathodea**: Fire Racewalking, Apparate 400 Meters, Branch Vault, and Malingee's Harvest ... We have brought back so many old games!

**可燃点**：哦——和芭妮芭妮小姐掰手腕比赛就要开始了，我得快点儿过去参加！\
**Spathodea**: Oh, I have to go! The Bunny Bunny Arm Wrestling is about to start!

一场场奇妙的比赛，一个个伶俐的巧思。\
Games after games, ideas after ideas.

喜动与好静的神秘学家都在这场地中找到了属于他们自己的快乐。\
Both active and inactive arcanists find their own happiness on this field.

**爱兹拉**：每个人都过得如此开心，脸上挂满汗珠，我在拉普拉斯从未见过这样的场面……\
**Ezra**: The people are having a good time here. They are sweaty but also delighted. I've never seen anything like this in Laplace.

爱兹拉又一次抬起头，望向斑驳的吊顶。\
Once again, Ezra looks up at the shabby rooftop.

**爱兹拉**：根据和平乌鲁女士所说，这股振奋的根源来自于乌卢鲁运动场……这是一种针对于神秘学家起效的康益神秘术吗？或是振奋药剂？\
**Ezra**: As Ms. Ulu said, this excitement comes from the Stadium itself. Is this a recovery arcane skill that works on arcanists? Or, a kind of cheering potion?

**维尔汀**：不，不像是。但是这里的……味道，闻起来很熟悉。\
**Vertin**: No, I don't think so. It just smells ... familiar here.

**星锑**：没错！说得对！我也这么觉得！\
**Regulus**: Yes! Right! Totally agree with you!

**星锑**：它闻起来就像是，之前海岛上那个奇怪的洞穴……嗝！嗯……？\
**Regulus**: It smells like the, uh, the weird cave on that island ... burp! Hmm?

**星锑**：哦——我闻到一股番茄、混合烧烤调料和牛肉的气味……哦！我想那是我的番茄牛排口味船长薯片……嘿哈！这太好玩儿了！\
**Regulus**: Oh, I smell beef, with tomato and mixed grilling sauce ... Oh! It must be my tomato steak flavor potato crisp. Haha! This is great fun!

**星锑**：我一点儿酒都没喝，但总感觉脑袋晕乎乎的！\
**Regulus**: I didn't touch a drop, but, ah, feeling dizzy!

**维尔汀**：星锑，小心。你要摔倒了。\
**Vertin**: Watch out, Regulus. You are falling down.

摇滚海盗被搀扶住，如同一条长果冻那样摇晃弹跳。\
Supported by a pair of friendly arms, the Rockin' Pirate softly jumps like a long, thin jelly.

**星锑**：哦……？难道运动比赛也有神经麻醉功效吗？嗯……我想，APPLe先生比我更懂这个，让我看看他在哪儿……\
**Regulus**: Oh? Are you saying that a sports game can narcotize people, too? Hmm. I think Mr. APPLe knows it better than me. Let me check where he is.

她兴致斐然，果冻有果冻探查四周的方式。\
Despite her weakness, the pirate's excitement is not dampened. She's in a "jelly" mood to explore.

**维尔汀**：唔！\
**Vertin**: Mmm?!

**星锑**：我看到了！那是一团红色，那一定是APPLe先生！但……但APPLe先生他好像变圆了，也变得更大了……\
**Regulus**: I see him! I see a red ball. Oh! That must be Mr. APPLe! But, but he seems rounder and bigger.

拉扯着挣扎的星锑，广场另一侧新的比赛落下帷幕。可燃点擦去脸上的汗水，脸颊通红，眼中闪烁。\
While Vertin is trying to keep a drunk Regulus balanced, the game on the other side of the Stadium has come to an end. Spathodea wipes the sweat off her forehead with rosy cheeks and eyes sparkling.

**芭妮芭妮**：比赛结束！沙丝绒小姐——胜出！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Time's up! And the victory goes to—Ms. Desert Flannel!

**沙丝绒**：哈……！我明明白白地和你说过，比掰手腕是没人赢得过我的～！\
**Desert Flannel**: Ha ...! I told ya, no one beats me at arm-wrestling!

**可燃点**：呼——哈，我比不过你……你的力气太大了！\
**Spathodea**: *pants* Ugh, I lost ... You are so strong!

**可燃点**：你太厉害了，我从来都……呃，呜……\
**Spathodea**: The strongest I have ever ... Ugh ...

可燃点直起身体，敏捷而轻快。\
Spathodea bounces up like a spring.

——又如同滑入汤碗的勺子一般瞬间瘫软下去。\
And immediately slumps down.

**沙丝绒**：可燃点！\
**Desert Flannel**: Spathodea!

**沙丝绒**：你怎么了，喂——醒醒！快，快把湿毛巾拿来！\
**Desert Flannel**: You alright? Hey ... wake up! Go, get me the wet towel!

沙丝绒熟练地折叠毛巾，盖上脸颊通红的姑娘额头，又用自己的夹克为她扇风。\
Folding the towel and putting it on that rosy girl's forehead has become a routine to Desert Flannel. After finishing this, she fans her with her own jacket.

**维尔汀**：她的体温……比刚刚要低一些，状态也稳定，这次应该不是因为神秘学反应，而是其他的原因。\
**Vertin**: Her temperature ... is a bit lower than just now, but her condition is quite stable. I guess it's not a "reincarnator" reaction, but something else.

**哒哒达利**：嗅——嗅嗅——\
**Darley Clatter**: *sniff*

**哒哒达利**：她还好吗？她接触起来很热，但还热不过纯金打造的马蹄铁。\
**Darley Clatter**: Is she alright? She feels hot, but not as hot as the horseshoe made of pure gold.

**沙丝绒**：她绝对有比你的小蹄子更烫的时候。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm positive that she was once a lot hotter than your little hooves are right now.

**沙丝绒**：这姑娘曾经浑身都燃着火，又猛又烈，是一瞬间就能让木头付之一炬的那种火！\
**Desert Flannel**: She was a walking fire that burned fiercely, the forest-destroying kind.

**哒哒达利**：吁吁——？！\
**Darley Clatter**: Neigh?!

小马儿惊叫着仓皇地后退，金属轮子吱吱作响。\
The wooden horse whinnies in panic and rolls backward on its squeaky metal wheels.

**爱兹拉**：请不要太过惊慌。可燃点小姐的眼中与口腔内并未见到火焰，她不会再次燃烧起来的。\
**Ezra**: Please don't panic. I have not observed any signs of flame in her eyes or mouth. She's not ablaze again.

**爱兹拉**：沙丝绒小姐，在忽然昏厥之前，她身上有任何异常表现吗？\
**Ezra**: Ms. Desert Flannel, did she have any abnormalities before she passed out?

**沙丝绒**：异常？好像有一些，她看起来就像是醉了一样，情绪高涨，意识模糊，走路也有些摇摇晃晃的……\
**Desert Flannel**: Abnormalities? Some, I think. She waddled as if she was pissed, and talked so loudly that anyone could tell she wasn't in a clear mind ...

**维尔汀**：醉酒，意识游离……糟了，星锑！\
**Vertin**: Drunk, clouding of consciousness ... No, Regulus!

**星锑**：你现在简直就像是一块儿苹果红色的巨石，APPLe先生！我们的……嗯……我们的小船会载不下你的……\
**Regulus**: You look like an apple-color giant rock, Mr. APPLe! You are so big, and our ship is so small.

**和平乌鲁**：我感觉如此愉快……与振奋！呼——啊！\
**Ulu**: I'm feeling so good ... and inspired! *deep breath*

一团巨大的火，将摇滚骑师衬得娇小依人。\
Standing next to a tremendous ball of fire, the Rockin' Pirate has never felt this small before.

**星锑**：呼——啊？哈？看起来体型也改变了你的声音……\
**Regulus**: *exhales* Ah? Huh? Seems your change of size changes your voice as well.

**星锑**：但没关系，如果你变得这样大，我们可以直接去撞翻伦敦那些老顽固，将摇滚的旗帜插在最高处——！\
**Regulus**: But! Since you get this huge, we can strike those old fogeys in London like a meteor! On top of the world, there will be our flag of Rock 'n' Roll!

**星锑**：来！来吧——让我们拥抱一个——\
**Regulus**: Come! Come to me—I require the biggest huuuuug!

拥抱火焰不是一个好主意。\
But it's not a good idea to have any hugs with fire.

**维尔汀**：星锑！\
**Vertin**: Regulus!

**星锑**：哇啊啊！好烫！好烫啊！我的手——！\
**Regulus**: Whoaa!! It's hot! It's burning!! It's burning my hands!

它们是灼热的，不稳定的，充满激情的。\
Because they are scorching, unstable, and fiery.

**和平乌鲁**：超越自己的极限，汗水就是对这片红土最高的赞誉！\
**Ulu**: Go beyond your limits! Your sweat is the best eulogy for the red land!

**爱兹拉**：是和平乌鲁女士，她失控了！这难道也是……也是运动场所导致的吗？！\
**Ezra**: That's Ms. Ulu! She's out of control! Is this ... Also a result of the Stadium's power?!

**芭妮芭妮**：天啊！星锑小姐！小心呀！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Oh, my! Ms. Regulus! Be careful!

火团愈演愈烈，快步赶往营救的芭妮芭妮拉起了星锑的衣袖。\
The fireball grows bigger and bigger. Bunny Bunny runs to Regulus and grabs her sleeve.

**星锑**：啊……好困，我先……睡一会儿……\
**Regulus**: Ah, I'm so tired. Let me take a nap.

**芭妮芭妮**：星锑！星锑！哎呀呀……你怎么也晕过去了呀！我现在就抱着你离开这儿，再等几秒钟！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Regulus? Regulus! Oh, dear ... Don't pass out now! I'm getting you outta here, just a sec!

**星锑**：哈呼呼……Zzzz……\
**Regulus**: Zzzz ...

**爱兹拉**：又一个晕厥反应，如果再等下去，恐怕所有神秘学家都要……维尔汀小姐，我们必须立刻离开这里！\
**Ezra**: Another one has passed out. If we let it go on like this, every arcanist here would ... Ms. Vertin, we have to leave at once!

**芭妮芭妮**：但是可燃点小姐已经昏过去了，谁能打开那扇门呢——\
**Bunny Bunny**: But Ms. Spathodea has passed out, too! Who can open that door?

**维尔汀**：芭妮芭妮，带上所有人返回箱子里！\
**Vertin**: Bunny Bunny, take everyone back to the suitcase!

**维尔汀**：在我重新打开箱子之前，不要让任何人出来。\
**Vertin**: Don't let anyone out before I open it again!

**芭妮芭妮**：好的，我明白了——哎呀，是什么绊了我一跤——啊？！APPLe先生！你怎么睡在草丛里呀！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Alright, got it ... Oops! I got tripped by ... Huh?! Mr. APPLe! Why are you sleeping in the grass?

**哒哒达利**：交给达利！\
**Darley Clatter**: Darley is on it!

背后驮着喀嚓喀嚓，口中叼着APPLe，哒哒达利拱着掉队的泉水精灵一起跳入手提箱。箱盖砰地一声合上，神秘学家们隔绝在那一头。\
With Click on his back and APPLe in his mouth, Darley Clatter pushes La Source into the suitcase and jumps inside after her. Clang. The suitcase closes, blocking the fire from a full room of arcanists.

**和平乌鲁**：运动，运动的快乐！我如同千年前一样燃烧！\
**Ulu**: All the fun, the fun of sports! I am burning like I did a thousand years ago!

**和平乌鲁**：哈哈……让我们手挽着手，为崇高的日头与……雨季起舞吧！\
**Ulu**: Haha ... Let's dance hand in hand, for the respectable sunshine ... and rain!

火焰炽热，千百年中持之以恒燃烧着的圣火更甚。\
Fire is always scorching, not to mention the Uluru Flame which has been burning for a thousand years.

她如新生时一般挥洒着自己的热能，泥土中的兽骨也冒出烟雾，几近燃烧。\
She emits her heat like she did as a newborn baby. Smoke coming billowing from the soil, even the beast bones inside eventually burn.

**爱兹拉**：唔——这样太危险了，可能会引发火灾的！\
**Ezra**: Mmm. This is too dangerous. She may start a fire!

**维尔汀**：我们得让她暂时熄灭。\
**Vertin**: We have to put her out for now.

爱兹拉的目光投射而来，公园一夜的画面似乎再度重演。\
Ezra turns to Vertin. They both remember what happened that night at the park.

**维尔汀**：……好在，我们是一对熟练的灭火拍档。\
**Vertin**: ... The good news is, we are already a skilled fire brigade.

## RUG-09 万事救星 / The Superman

**维尔汀**：沙丝绒的头晕症状已有缓解，她的精神很好，正在传真室忙着自己的事务……这会对她的身体产生有害的影响么？\
**Vertin**: Desert Flannel's dizziness is in remission. She's already well enough to deal with her business on the fax machine. Will it do harm to her physical condition?

**爱兹拉**：沙丝绒小姐的不良反应很轻微，她可以自由行动。四处走动对她的身体也会有好处，而可燃点小姐则正相反……\
**Ezra**: Ms. Desert Flannel is only experiencing a very mild reaction. She can move around freely, and it is recommended for her to do so. Ms. Spathodea, on the contrary ...

**维尔汀**：她还没有醒。\
**Vertin**: She's not even awake.

**爱兹拉**：是的。不过她的体温和神秘术波动已经开始趋于稳定，应该很快就会醒来。\
**Ezra**: No. But her body temperature and her arcanum level are getting stable now. She should wake up in any minute.

**维尔汀**：是因为她在运动场中参与了过多的比赛所导致的？\
**Vertin**: Is it because she took part in too many events in the Stadium?

**爱兹拉**：没有错，在接下来至少三天内，她都需要卧床休息。\
**Ezra**: That's right. She has to stay in bed for the next three days.

**爱兹拉**：星锑小姐和APPLe先生也一样，我已经拜托兔子小姐为他们送去了药物。如果顺利的话，他们应该已经醒来了……\
**Ezra**: As well as Ms. Regulus and Mr. APPLe. I have asked Ms. Bunny to send them the medicine. If everything went well, they should have woken up by now ...

**芭妮芭妮**：爱兹拉医生！我回来了！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Dr. Ezra, I'm back!

开着缝隙的门中探出兔女郎的身影。\
The bunny girl pops out from between the crack in the door.

**芭妮芭妮**：APPLe先生和星锑都醒过来了，我给他们喝了药！但……和平乌鲁女士还在沉睡……\
**Bunny Bunny**: Both Mr. APPLe and Ms. Regulus are awake now, so I gave them some medicine! But ... Ms. Ulu is still in a coma ...

**爱兹拉**：别担心，和平乌鲁女士与其他昏厥的神秘学家不同。她的消耗来源于自身内部和长久沉睡带来的虚弱。而非其他人那样，源于外部影响。\
**Ezra**: Don't worry, Ms. Ulu is different to the other unconscious arcanists. She was weakened by the long sleep, while the other arcanists lost consciousness because of external factors.

**爱兹拉**：瞧，这是昏厥者们三个小时内的身体情况检查记录——\
**Ezra**: Look, this is their physiological data in the last three hours.

**爱兹拉**：许多神秘学家都表示，在进入运动场后感到了身体状态的提高，体感接近于“睡了一个好觉”或是“得到了足够的休息”。\
**Ezra**: Many arcanists have told us that their physical abilities were improved as they entered the Stadium. They felt they were in a refreshed state like they had a good sleep or rested properly.

**爱兹拉**：参与四至六个运动项目，平均运动时长超过三个半小时后，开始感到接近于醉酒的晕眩感——\
**Ezra**: But after they competed in 4 to 6 different games, or the average sporting time exceeded 3.5 hours, they would feel dizzy, as if they had consumed too much alcohol.

**维尔汀**：而在离开乌卢鲁运动会后，这些症状很快获得了减轻。\
**Vertin**: And these symptoms were relieved soon after they left the Stadium.

**芭妮芭妮**：哎呀，你们的意思是……大家东倒西歪的，都是因为那个运动场？\
**Bunny Bunny**: Ah, you mean ... people are in oblivion because of that ... Stadium?

**芭妮芭妮**：那儿这样危险，还能继续举办运动会吗？\
**Bunny Bunny**: If that place is so dangerous, is it possible to hold the Games again?

**爱兹拉**：过去的乌卢鲁运动会，一位选手只允许参加三个项目，我想也是因为这方面的顾虑。只要我们维持这个限制……就不成问题。\
**Ezra**: I think this is why in the past, athletes were only allowed to compete in three different sports. As long as we stick with the same rule, the safety of our athletes shouldn't be problematic.

**芭妮芭妮**：啊——我明白了！这个运动场很安全，就像我工作的俱乐部一样安全！只要不犯规，就不会出事儿！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Oh! I got it! So this place is just as safe as the club I work in! As long as we ain't breaking the rules, nothing will happen!

**芭妮芭妮**：我们的俱乐部里有保镖，有我，而乌卢鲁运动场既有次数保护，又有爱兹拉小姐特制的药物保护！\
**Bunny Bunny**: Like how the bodyguards and I take care of our club, the rule and special medicine made by Ms. Ezra will protect the Uluru Stadium!

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**爱兹拉**：……小姐？\
**Ezra**: Ms.?

**芭妮芭妮**：哎呀？怎么了吗？爱兹拉小姐？\
**Bunny Bunny**: Oh? What's wrong, Ms. Ezra?

**爱兹拉**：兔子小姐，但其实……我并不是女性。\
**Ezra**: Ms. Bunny, but you see ... I'm not a Ms.

**芭妮芭妮**：嗯？\
**Bunny Bunny**: Huh?

芭妮芭妮缓慢地歪过了脑袋。\
Bunny Bunny slowly tilts her head.

**芭妮芭妮**：您真会开玩笑，您不是女性，还能是男性吗？请别捉弄我了，爱兹拉小姐。\
**Bunny Bunny**: You are funny, Ms. Ezra. Please stop teasing me. What else can you be except a lady? A gentleman?

**维尔汀**：爱兹拉他的确是一位男性。\
**Vertin**: Ezra is indeed a he.

**芭妮芭妮**：……嗯？\
**Bunny Bunny**: ... Huh?

兔女郎的回应中逐渐充满了不确认。\
The bunny girl's voice starts to sound hesitant.

**可燃点**：男——男性？！\
**Spathodea**: A-A HE?!

**爱兹拉**：啊！可燃点小姐，你醒了！来，这是水和营养补充胶囊……\
**Ezra**: Aah! Ms. Spathodea, you're awake! Here, take this water and the nutrition supplement capsule.

**可燃点**：不，不不不不不不不……\
**Spathodea**: No no no no, NOOOO ...

可燃点双手颤抖地推开药丸和水杯。\
Spathodea, hands trembling, pushes away the pills and water.

**可燃点**：你，你是男的？你什么时候……变成男的的？\
**Spathodea**: You-You're a boy? When did you ... turn into a boy?

**爱兹拉**：是的。我是男性。我从出生，到现在，都是男性。\
**Ezra**: Yes, I'm a boy. I was a boy when I was born, and I have been that way since.

**可燃点**：什么？不是……你，你说什么？那你为什么骗我呀！你怎么能说你是——唔？不对，你好像也从来没有说过你就是个女孩儿……\
**Spathodea**: What? Wait ... Wh-What? Why did you lie to me?! Why did you say you were a ... Wait, you never said you were a girl ...

**爱兹拉**：等等——可燃点小姐，请不要抓得这么紧……\
**Ezra**: Wait, Ms. Spathodea, please don't grab me so tightly.

**沙丝绒**：嘿——我回……嗯？你们这是怎么了？\
**Desert Flannel**: Hey ya, I'm back ... Emm? What happened?

**沙丝绒**：可燃点小姑娘抱着膝盖发呆，而爱兹拉妹妹抱着脑袋……发，发晕？\
**Desert Flannel**: Our little Spathodea looks completely absent-minded, arms around her knees, and Missy Ezra here is holding her forehead and looks ... overwhelmed?

**可燃点**：她……啊不，他！他才不是什么“爱兹拉妹妹”！他是爱兹拉弟弟！\
**Spathodea**: She ... Um, he! He is not a "missy"! He's a buddy!

**沙丝绒**：什么……爱兹拉弟弟？爱兹拉是弟弟还是妹妹很重要吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: Aah ... Buddy Ezra? So what, boy or girl, is that such a big deal?

沙丝绒晃晃手里的纸页，将其放在可燃点面前。\
Desert Flannel waves the papers around and puts them on the table in front of Spathodea.

**沙丝绒**：反正——没有这个重要！\
**Desert Flannel**: Nothing is more important than this!

**可燃点**：“亲爱的维尔汀小姐，很高兴收到你的回信……”\
**Spathodea**: "Dear Ms. Vertin, I am glad to hear from you ..."

**沙丝绒**：不，不是这张。这张是维尔汀的——发件人是一个叫作宽檐帽的家伙。\
**Desert Flannel**: No no, not that one. That's for Vertin ... from some guy called Slouch Hat.

纸片迅速被抽离，重新丢到了另一个人面前。\
She fishes out a page out of the pile in Spathodea's hand and throws it to Vertin.

**维尔汀**：哦。谢谢。他是我的本地向导，我们最近一直有书信往来。\
**Vertin**: Oh, thank you. He's my contact in Australia. We've been writing letters these days.

**可燃点**：那我真正要看的是什么？是这张吗？\
**Spathodea**: So what am I supposed to look at then? This one?

**可燃点**：大型活动申请表……爱丽丝泉政府部门……啊！这是！这是！\
**Spathodea**: Large-scale Event Application Form ... Alice Springs Government ... Oh! This is! This is that thing!

**沙丝绒**：哈哈！没错啦！只要我们到了市政厅，写完这个，再交上去！我们就可以立刻开始筹划乌卢鲁运动会啦！\
**Desert Flannel**: Haha! Yeees! We just need to go to the City Hall, fill in the form, and submit it! Then we're ready to have our Uluru Games!

**可燃点**：那还等什么呀，我们立刻就动身吧！\
**Spathodea**: What are we waiting for then? Let's hit the road!

一把掀开被子，可燃点几乎是蹦跳着离开了床铺。\
She throws back the covers and leaps out of the bed.

**爱兹拉**：不行！可燃点小姐！你的身体还十分虚弱，需要静卧休息！\
**Ezra**: No! Ms. Spathodea! You haven't fully recovered. You need to rest!

**可燃点**：我感觉没那么糟——我甚至感觉，很好！对——就是很好！\
**Spathodea**: I'm not feeling that bad ... Actually I'm feeling really good! That's right—reeeally good!

小姑娘举起双手，抓着随行医生的手臂左右使劲摇晃。\
The little girl grips the arm of her doctor and gives him a rough shake.

**可燃点**：市政厅也并不是什么雨林山涧，我们只是去填一些表格，他们不会伤害我的，好吗？好吗～？\
**Spathodea**: The City Hall is not like a no man's land. We're just going there to fill in some forms. They won't hurt me, okay? O-kay?

**爱兹拉**：不——不行。这次和过去的情况不同……\
**Ezra**: No ... NO. This time is different.

小医生则是努力地，努力地在狂风骤雨般的甩动下稳定住了自己的身体。\
The doctor tries to stay solid as a rock amidst the storm of shaking.

**爱兹拉**：这次和过去不同，可燃点小姐！\
**Ezra**: This is not like what happened before, Ms. Spathodea!

**爱兹拉**：我是你的随行医生，我得对你的健康情况负责，我不能让你离开我的视线——\
**Ezra**: I'm your doctor, and I'm responsible for your health. I can't let you leave my sight.

**可燃点**：视线——视线……啊！我明白了！\
**Spathodea**: Your sight ... Your sight ... Oh! Got it!

可燃点停下左右摇晃的动作，很快那股强烈的力道变成了拉扯。\
Spathodea stopped shaking but began pulling hard instead.

**可燃点**：你也和我一起来就好了吧！走吧，走吧！\
**Spathodea**: You can come with me! C'mon, c'mon!

**可燃点**：时间不等人，我们的夏季运动会就要开始啦！\
**Spathodea**: Time waits for no man. Our Summer Games are about to start!

**爱兹拉**：等，等一下——哇啊！\
**Ezra**: Wa-Wait ... Whaaah!

声音还未散去，孩子们就一同消失在走廊的那头。\
The kids disappear at the end of the hallway, their yells and shouts lingering a little longer.

**芭妮芭妮**：哇……可燃点小姐跑得可真快，比喝了魔药后的苏芙比小姐还快……\
**Bunny Bunny**: Whoa ... Ms. Spathodea is surely a good runner, even faster than the potion-drunk Ms. Sotheby ...

**沙丝绒**：好了，既然现在医患矛盾解决了，我这个大型活动策划助理也要一起上路啦！\
**Desert Flannel**: OK, since the doctor and the patient are both happy, I, the event assistance producer, am also hitting the road!

**沙丝绒**：等着我们的好消息吧～\
**Desert Flannel**: Wait for our good news!

**沙丝绒**：这些都是什么呀？！每个单词我都认识——但是拼起来，拼起来我就一个都读不懂啦！\
**Desert Flannel**: What are these? And this?! Look, I know English, but I don't understand any of the things written here.

**沙丝绒**：什么是“北领地活动安全法”？什么又是“Ⅲ型场地安全核验证书”？\
**Desert Flannel**: What is "Northern Territory Event Security Law"? And what is "Type III Field Safety Certification"?

**沙丝绒**：活动类型这里，我们选C就好了吧，它看起来最靠近乌卢鲁运动会，至少它们都是六个字……\
**Desert Flannel**: I think I will just go with C here for Event Types. That's what looks closest to the Uluru Games, since they're both two-word phrases ...

**可燃点**：也许可以，选着试试。\
**Spathodea**: Maybe, let's just go with that one.

**可燃点**：遇到看不懂的东西时，我总是喜欢选C……\
**Spathodea**: I always go with C when I have no idea what I'm reading ...

沙丝绒双手抱头哀叹连连，可燃点嘴里叼着铅笔头啃个不停。\
Desert Flannel buries her head in her hands, wailing, while Spathodea keeps biting her pencil.

**芭妮芭妮**：大型活动申报，火灾预警逃离路线图……可燃点小姐，乌卢鲁运动场中有逃生通道吗？\
**Bunny Bunny**: Mass Event Application, Fire Escape Plan ... Ms. Spathodea, does the Stadium have a fire escape?

**可燃点**：……我过去的记忆中没有。我现在的记忆中——好吧，我一点儿都不知道，我只在意运动来着……\
**Spathodea**: ... Not in Flammy's memory. Let me check Spathodea's ... Alright, I have no idea at all. The sports are all that I care about ...

**芭妮芭妮**：好吧……那我就在这行写上“不知道”好了……\
**Bunny Bunny**: Well ... I'm just gonna write down an "unknown" here ...

**爱兹拉**：……\
**Ezra**: ...

**爱兹拉**：你们……\
**Ezra**: You ...

**沙丝绒**：怎么了，我赌气的朋友，你终于愿意来帮忙了吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: How are ya, my grumpy little friend? Finally made up your mind to help?

爱兹拉将欲言又止的嘴巴死死地压在一起，用力摇头。\
Ezra opens and shuts his mouth, shaking his head roughly.

故作轻松，实际上则焦灼得像是热锅上的蚂蚁。\
At ease as he seems, deep down he is like a cat on hot bricks.

**爱兹拉**：不……我不想帮助对自己身体不负责的病患。请你们自己努力。\
**Ezra**: No ... I have no desire to help a patient who doesn't care about her own health. You are on your own.

**市政员工**：B区13号表格收纳窗口，感谢您的等待。接下来我将审核您的表格是否合乎规……则……\
**Government Staff**: City Government Service Center, District B, Window 13 at your service. Thanks for your waiting. Your form will be exami- ...

**市政员工**：……\
**Government Staff**: ...

**沙丝绒**：很好，她顿住了。这是为什么？\
**Desert Flannel**: Oh, great, she stopped. What happened?

**可燃点**：她的表情看起来不大好，像极了朱迪尔小姐——也就是我的数学老师，往常……她对我露出这个表情的时候……\
**Spathodea**: That's not a good look. I've seen that look on Ms. Judy's face. She's my maths teacher ... Whenever she puts on that face ...

**沙丝绒**：的时候？\
**Desert Flannel**: Yes?

**可燃点**：就代表着“你的整张试卷里，没有一道题写对了！”。\
**Spathodea**: It means "none of your answers are correct!"

**沙丝绒**：啊哈……\
**Desert Flannel**: A-ha ...

一次失败。\
Failure.

满是墨渍的表格从柜台深处被退回，一高一矮两个人对话着走远。\
A sheet of paper stained with ink is returned, and its owners talk to each other, walking away from the service window.

**可燃点**：我就说，我们不能在表格里写“鬼才知道”这样的话的——\
**Spathodea**: Told you we can't fill "Who knows" in the form ...

**沙丝绒**：鬼才知道这个不能写！\
**Desert Flannel**: Who knows you can't write that!

**可燃点**：请看看这个——\
**Spathodea**: Please check this one.

**市政员工**：好的，沙丝……抱歉，您是？\
**Government Staff**: Yes, Ms. Desert ... I'm sorry, and you are ...

**可燃点**：嘿——我是可燃点！这个活动的主要负责人！\
**Spathodea**: Hellooo! I am Spathodea, the director of the event!

**可燃点**：但是这个柜台太——高了，她用起来——更方便！\
**Spathodea**: This counter is wayyy too high! Should've let Desert Flannellll talk to you!

**可燃点**：至于沙丝绒——她看书看得头晕！\
**Spathodea**: But she'ssss feeling sick after reading the form!

**可燃点**：所以——现在就只能我来了——！\
**Spathodea**: Sooooo, I have to do it insteaaaad!

**市政员工**：……我会为您准备一个脚凳的。请不要再跳了。\
**Government Staff**: ... I will prepare a stool for you. Please stop jumping.

又一次不利。\
Another failure.

她的表格失败了。但她至少得到了一架脚凳。\
Her form failed, that is true, but at least she gets a stool to step onto.

**可燃点**：嘿……！太好了，有了这个脚凳我就不用一个劲儿地跳啦！\
**Spathodea**: Ugh! Yes, with this stool, I don't have to jump up again and again!

**可燃点**：这是我们新写的表格，请您看看！\
**Spathodea**: Here's the form we revised. Please check it!

**市政员工**：……好的。\
**Government Staff**: ... Alright.

**市政员工**：《神秘学家集会信息报备表》、《大型活动举办许可申请表》与《沙漠地区集会申请表》三项已经完成。\
**Government Staff**: You've submitted the Arcanist Gathering Registration Form, the Mass Events Application Form, and the Desert Areas Gathering Application Form.

**市政员工**：我将为您投递至管理部门审批。\
**Government Staff**: Your application will be in the approval process very soon.

**可燃点**：天啊——真是太好了！我们真的受不了再写一遍这些表格了！\
**Spathodea**: Gosh, YESSS! I'd go crazy if I had to fill in them again!

**可燃点**：我几乎从来没这么痛苦过，我们两个抱头痛哭了好几次呢！\
**Spathodea**: I've never experienced such pain. We cried on each other's shoulder several times!

**市政员工**：……我也很想哭。\
**Government Staff**: Same for me.

**可燃点**：您说什么？\
**Spathodea**: I'm sorry?

**市政员工**：不，没什么。但请看《运动比赛流程与项目申报表》后半页此处，您所罗列的大部分项目经查验并不在许可运动之列。\
**Government Staff**: It's nothing. But please take a look here at the second half of the Sports Game Process & Events Application Form. Most of the events of your application have been confirmed not approved.

**市政员工**：如果您希望将其加入乌卢鲁运动会，则需要单独申请安全许可。\
**Government Staff**: If you want to add them to the Uluru Games, an independent application for each event's security permissions is required.

**可燃点**：我要怎么得到这些安全许可？\
**Spathodea**: How can I get the permissions then?

表格，更多的表格。难以理解的表格。\
Forms. More forms. Indigestible forms.

**市政员工**：您需要填写这些表格，并为需要申请的运动项目拍摄动态相片进行备案。\
**Government Staff**: You need to fill in these forms and take live photos for the events you want to apply for.

多大的噩耗啊。\
What a miserable piece of news.

**可燃点**：……呜。\
**Spathodea**: Ughhhh.

**爱兹拉**：请把——那些表格，给我——吧！\
**Ezra**: Excuse meeee, please, give me the foooorms!

另一个跳跃的脑袋由柜台下钻出来。\
Another tiny figure jumps up from under the counter.

**爱兹拉**：我会负责它们的——\
**Ezra**: I'll take caaaaare of them.

**爱兹拉**：让这些女孩儿……离开这儿去休息——吧。\
**Ezra**: Let the giiiirls ... leave and rest ...!

**可燃点**：爱兹拉——\
**Spathodea**: Ezra ...

痛苦的泪水变成了欣喜的泪水，感恩化为巨大的拥抱。\
All the miserable tears suddenly change into tears of joy. She gives him a bear hug.

**爱兹拉**：嗯——？！\
**Ezra**: Mmm?!

**可燃点**：天啊，你太好了，你简直就是我认识的最好、最好、最好的人！\
**Spathodea**: Gosh, that's so kind of you! You are the kindest person of all the kind people I know! Thank you, Ezra!

**可燃点**：虽然我不能保证这之后的三天里，乖乖躺在床上，可——可我一定会好好吃药的，一秒也不犹豫！\
**Spathodea**: I can't promise I'll stay in bed for the next three days, but-but I'll take the medicines in time! No hesitation!

**爱兹拉**：别客气，可燃点，我今天也学到了一个道理……\
**Ezra**: No worries, Spathodea. I've also learned something today.

小研究员无力地笑了笑，脸色苍白。\
The little researcher helplessly smiles, his face pale.

**爱兹拉**：……看所有人痛苦，比我自己痛苦更让我难受百倍。我想，还是帮助人的感觉更好。\
**Ezra**: That is, it pains me more to see people suffer than to endure my own suffering. I prefer to give them a hand.

**爱兹拉**：接下来的所有文书工作就请交给我吧。虽然柜台有些高，但我会努力跳高点儿的。\
**Ezra**: Please leave the paperwork to me. I can jump to reach the counter.

**市政员工**：脚凳。那里还有一架脚凳。\
**Government Staff**: Stool. Take another stool over there.

**爱兹拉**：啊——是的，长时间跳跃会使半月板受到不可回溯的损伤，感谢您的提醒，我会好好使用它的。\
**Ezra**: Ah. Yes. Jumping for too long would cause irreversible damage to my meniscus. Thank you so much!

玻璃窗后，市政员工疲惫的脸上终于露出了一丝宽慰的笑容。\
Behind the glass, the exhausted receptionist finally shows a smile of relief.

**和平乌鲁**：运动会与小火将千年前还是个小火苗的我唤醒了，他们让我狂热，让我疯狂。\
**Ulu**: The Games and Flammy woke me up when I was still a small flame a millennia ago. They made me fanatic and crazy.

**和平乌鲁**：但多神奇呀，我年轻的朋友。和你对话时，我就像是现在的我。\
**Ulu**: How amazing, my young friend. I'm just like the present me when I talk to you.

**维尔汀**：什么是“现在的我”？\
**Vertin**: What do you mean "the present me"?

**和平乌鲁**：一个持续燃烧千年的老人。\
**Ulu**: An old flame that has been burning for over a thousand years.

**和平乌鲁**：你很聪明，也有很多有趣的点子，在我还是那团火苗的时候我就在留心你了，你对乌卢鲁运动会的期许很多。\
**Ulu**: You are smart, and your ideas are fun. I've been paying attention to you when I was still a small flame. Looks like you have a lot of expectations for the Uluru Games.

**和平乌鲁**：甚至……有些时候，你比小火更关注这场比赛。\
**Ulu**: Sometimes it feels like ... you care about the Games even more than Flammy does.

**维尔汀**：我对它有所希望，比可燃点期望得更多，也比爱兹拉有更强的意愿。\
**Vertin**: I do have hopes for it. My wish to revive the Games is stronger than Ezra's, and my expectations for it are higher than Spathodea's.

**维尔汀**：时代不同，一场运动比赛能做到的事就不同了。\
**Vertin**: After all, we're in a different age now, which means we can achieve much more than a sports game.

**维尔汀**：但我的热情远不如可燃点小姐，她……嗯？她带着的那些人是……\
**Vertin**: But to be honest, I'm impressed by Ms. Spathodea's energy and passion for all these. She's ... Huh? Who are those people by her side?

小姑娘带着大部队走在沙地上，她兴致勃勃地划分着眼前的空间。\
The little girl excitedly walks on the sand, her hands waving in the air and pointing each part of the space for their usages. Behind her, an engineering team follows.

**可燃点**：这里——这里——然后到这里！\
**Spathodea**: From here, toooo, here!

**可燃点**：我想在这儿修建一个漂亮的入口，我需要凉亭，也要一个冰饮存取点！\
**Spathodea**: I wanna build a neat entrance here. I also need a kiosk and a fridge with drinks!

**维修队员**：好的。我们的工程师明天下午五点之前为您带来合适的建材小样以供参考。您可以届时再进行选择。\
**Repairman**: Okay. Our engineer will bring you the suitable sample materials before tomorrow 5 p.m. You can make a choice then.

**维修队员**：而建筑设计图，我们会在明天早上提交给您。\
**Repairman**: And you will see the architectural drawing tomorrow morning.

**维尔汀**：可燃点，这些是？\
**Vertin**: Spathodea, who are they?

**可燃点**：这些是拉普拉斯特派来的维修队员！\
**Spathodea**: They are engineers from Laplace!

**可燃点**：因为我们的建筑不符合场馆规范，为了申请乌卢鲁运动会的所有许可证书，我们必须对它进行修缮。\
**Spathodea**: Our buildings don't meet the government's requirements, so we have to repair them.

**可燃点**：爱兹拉从爱丽丝泉打电话联系了他们，拉普拉斯似乎很支持这次活动。他们坐着特别快的车，不到一小时就赶到了这儿！\
**Spathodea**: Ezra called them from Alice Springs, and Laplace seems very supportive. They took the fastest ride and got here in less than an hour!

**和平乌鲁**：修缮？这会改变运动场的内部构造吗？\
**Ulu**: Repair? Will they change the internal structure of the Stadium?

**可燃点**：当然不会了！我当然不会允许那种事情发生啦！\
**Spathodea**: Of course not! There's no way I'd let them do that!

**可燃点**：乌卢鲁运动场并非神秘学家的造物，而是来自于自然伟大神力与崇高精神的馈赠，我们要做的只有在其中尽情燃烧而已。\
**Spathodea**: The Uluru Stadium is not a creation of arcanists', but a gift from great nature and its noble spirit. All we will do inside is sweat and let our spirits burn!

**维尔汀**：等等。\
**Vertin**: Wait.

“——吱吱。”\
Squeak.

**可燃点**：嗯？我好像听到了什么声音……\
**Spathodea**: Hmm? I think I just heard something ...

“呼哧呼哧。”\
Huff, huff.

**和平乌鲁**：我也听到了……它在……\
**Ulu**: I heard it too ... It's ...

**本耶普**：呜哈——！\
**Bunyip**: *roars*

**可燃点**：是本耶普！还有那些从乌卢鲁运动场里溜出来的魔鬼蜥蜴——！\
**Spathodea**: The Bunyips! And those Thorny Devils! They must have snuck out from the Stadium!

**可燃点**：都怪那些八卦报纸！我们成了流言蜚语的中心！这些东西一个劲儿地跟着我们跑——就像是忘了盖盖子的果酱总能吸引蟑螂一样……！\
**Spathodea**: Ugh, darn those tabloids! We're at the center of the storm now! These things just won't let us go, like some cockroaches attracted to an open jar of jam!

**和平乌鲁**：它们的嘴里还沾着一些纸片，这是……报纸？\
**Ulu**: There are scraps of paper sticking to the corner of their mouths. Is that newspaper?

**和平乌鲁**：“乌卢鲁运动会复兴小队携兔女郎……大闹市政厅？强压下精神崩溃的市政员工！《叮咚快报》……独家访谈……？”\
**Ulu**: "MAYHEM! REVIVAL SQUAD OF ULURU GAMES IN CITY HALL WITH BUNNY GIRL?! MENTAL BREAKDOWN OF RECEPTIONIST! Exclusive on Australian Nagger ..."

**和平乌鲁**：天啊，孩子——你们在外面到底都做了什么呀？！\
**Ulu**: Gosh, children ... What have you done out there?!

## RUG-10 过家家 / Let's Play House

一切都比想象中进展得更加好。\
Everything is going smoother than expected.

**维尔汀**：过去的两周之中，经由拉普拉斯转递，向基金会申请活动举办资格的进程顺利。宽檐帽先生今早与我通过电话。\
**Vertin**: Laplace has forwarded the Uluru Games application to the Foundation, and it has been moving smoothly in the system in the last two weeks. I heard that from Mr. Slouch Hat on the phone this morning.

**维尔汀**：他们认为，这是一个树立神秘学家正面形象的好机会，更可以推进人类与神秘学家的交流、关联。基金会总乐于看到这一幕。\
**Vertin**: They believe it will be a good opportunity to build a positive image for arcanists, and it will strengthen the communication between them and humans. The Foundation is happy to see that happen.

**爱兹拉**：审批文件的下放时间呢？\
**Ezra**: Then when will we have the result of the application?

**维尔汀**：因为流程复杂，以及近日才完成的比赛项目安全性申报，审批至少需要20天。\
**Vertin**: The procedure is long and complicated. Besides, the safety reports were only submitted a few days ago, so it will take at least 20 days.

**可燃点**：20天？如果20天后才能确认开工，我们就赶不上预定的举办日期了——之前，施工队说至少需要一个半月来完成入口。\
**Spathodea**: Twenty days? If we start the construction after that, we'll never make it on the opening day. The engineers said the construction will take at least a month and a half.

**维尔汀**：这已经是很快的速度了，我们的时间还能再推迟吗？\
**Vertin**: That's almost the fastest they can do. Can we postpone it a bit more?

**可燃点**：嗯……恐怕不行。我已经为修缮推迟了半个月，如果继续推迟，夏天就要结束了。\
**Spathodea**: Hmm ... I'm afraid not. I already postponed it until half a month later for the construction. Summer will be over if we wait any longer.

**爱兹拉**：没关系，我与他们规划过施工顺序。\
**Ezra**: It's okay. We have talked about the construction arrangement.

一张标记着许多文字的地图在桌面上铺开。爱兹拉手持红笔，划出一道新的弧线。\
A map marked with writings is rolled out on the table. Ezra draws a new line.

**爱兹拉**：我们可以优先开始修缮工作，而后调派人手，同时进行多类工作。如同图示，优化分工和时间安排，赶在一个月内完成修缮。\
**Ezra**: We may start the renovation ourselves, and move on to other things when we have more people to help. As I demonstrated here, if we plan it properly, we may be able to finish the construction in a month.

**爱兹拉**：届时，刚好可以赶上可燃点小姐最初安排的日期。\
**Ezra**: By then, we can start the event as Ms. Spathodea first planned.

**可燃点**：天啊——我明明都看了好多次日程安排了！\
**Spathodea**: Gosh! I already checked the schedule a hundred times!

**可燃点**：你是怎么做到挤出半个月时间来的！真是不可思议——\
**Spathodea**: How did you manage to cut down 15 days from nowhere?! This is unbelievable!

可燃点拿起纸页，举到面前认真观看起来。\
Spathodea holds the paper level to her nose and has a read.

**可燃点**：你可真是个天才，爱兹拉！没有你，我们的比赛或许就办不成了！\
**Spathodea**: You're a genius, Ezra! I guess the Games would have died on the vine without you!

**爱兹拉**：这在人类之中并没有什么了不起的，神秘学家才该是这场比赛的主心骨。\
**Ezra**: It's nothing extraordinary, compared to what a real human genius can do. Don't forget arcanists are the pillar of the Games.

**可燃点**：让我看看——将工人小队分为三组，分别开始修缮运动场内部吊顶、墙壁与外部入口……\
**Spathodea**: Let me see ... Divide the construction team into three groups, one building the entrance, and the other two repairing the internal ceiling and walls ...

**可燃点**：……运动场内部的吊顶与墙壁？\
**Spathodea**: ... The internal ceiling and walls?

**可燃点**：爱兹拉，我没有与拉普拉斯维修队提出过这样的需求，你们一定是搞错了什么，我们不需要对运动场内部进行更迭！\
**Spathodea**: Ezra, I have never made that request to the construction team. You must be mistaken. We need not repair what's inside the Stadium!

**爱兹拉**：这是我增加的维修项目。\
**Ezra**: I added it to the list.

**爱兹拉**：我已经带着维修队的成员去考察过，那里十分古老，墙壁风化严重，支撑结构薄弱。比起运动场，更像是自然景观。\
**Ezra**: I have investigated the site with some workers from the construction team. The Stadium is ancient. The walls are badly weathered and can barely hold up anything. It has become more of a natural scenic spot than a Stadium for sports.

**爱兹拉**：为了观众和运动员们的安全考量，我们选用合金支架进行支撑……\
**Ezra**: For safety reasons, we might use a support structure made of alloy to ...

**可燃点**：不行！绝对不行！\
**Spathodea**: No! Definitely NO!

椅子向后翻倒，可燃点猛地站起身子。\
Spathodea stands up quickly, overturning the chair.

**可燃点**：那可是乌卢鲁运动场啊，那不是可以随便搭建的办公楼！我是不会让你们进去的！\
**Spathodea**: This is the Uluru Stadium we're talking about, not some office building on the street! I will not let you in!

**可燃点**：如果你早一步告诉我，你会做出这种事情——我就不会让那儿的门开着了！\
**Spathodea**: I wouldn't have left the gate open if you told me your plan earlier!

**爱兹拉**：可是观众们要怎么办？可燃点小姐，观众的安全呢？\
**Ezra**: But what about the audience, Ms. Spathodea? How are we going to look after their safety?

**爱兹拉**：如果遭遇塌方或是落石，那些观众应该如何逃生？\
**Ezra**: If one of the walls or the ceiling collapses, how can they escape?

**可燃点**：过去从没有发生过这样的事，这么多年来都没有！\
**Spathodea**: Nothing like that has happened before, not even one case in the past hundreds of years!

**爱兹拉**：世界上从来都没有万全不变的事物，我们必须预估可能发生的危险，才好避免悲剧。\
**Ezra**: Nothing stays the same forever. We have to foresee the danger before it is too late.

**可燃点**：……人们能躲开的。\
**Spathodea**: They can run away from the danger themselves.

**爱兹拉**：什么……？\
**Ezra**: Excuse me?

**可燃点**：你们不是也研究出来了吗？乌卢鲁运动场会祛除神秘学家身上的疲劳，将其身体与神秘学能力调整到最佳状态。\
**Spathodea**: You already figured it out, right? The Stadium can get rid of fatigue from arcanists and adjust their conditions and arcane abilities to their best.

**可燃点**：当“万一”的危险来临，他们能保护自己，那些预言家与占卜师也能保护他人。\
**Spathodea**: Even if accidents really happened, they can protect themselves. The prophets and diviners will also warn the others.

**可燃点**：我们从来都不需要钢铁架子来保护我们的脑袋！\
**Spathodea**: We never needed metal bars above our heads to protect us!

**爱兹拉**：那人类的观众呢？\
**Ezra**: What about the human audiences?

**爱兹拉**：他们没有神奇能力，也没有超强感知，无法驾驶扫帚，也无法瞬间移动，他们甚至无法从密集的人群中尽可能快地抽身离去。\
**Ezra**: They have no superpower, nor super senses. They can't fly a broom or teleport themselves. They can't even get themselves out of a packed room.

**爱兹拉**：在你预想中，人类观众要如何保证自己的安全呢？\
**Ezra**: In your plan, how are you going to ensure their safety?

**可燃点**：人类？人类为什么会在运动场里？\
**Spathodea**: Humans? What are they doing in the Stadium?

**爱兹拉**：……！\
**Ezra**: ...!

**可燃点**：乌卢鲁运动会从没有人类参加过，没有人类寻着它的大门，无人成功踏入其中——\
**Spathodea**: There has never been a single human in the Uluru Games. None of them managed to find the entrance, not to mention enter it ...

**爱兹拉**：……可我也是一个人类，可燃点小姐。\
**Ezra**: But I am human, Ms. Spathodea.

**爱兹拉**：你邀请过我，你说过“乌卢鲁运动场”出现在了我面前，人类——也就是我，从那一刻开始，就可以踏入这所运动场了！\
**Ezra**: You invited me to the Games. It's also you who told me that humans, like myself, can enter the Uluru Stadium if it shows itself!

爱兹拉手里的水杯落在桌面上。\
The cup in his hand falls to the table.

**可燃点**：你——我，我当时以为你是不一样的人类！\
**Spathodea**: You ... I-I thought you were different!

**可燃点**：你很关心神秘学家，你愿意帮忙，心地也不坏……\
**Spathodea**: You showed concern about arcanists, and you helped us a lot. You're a kind human ...

**爱兹拉**：我并不是人类中特殊的个体。\
**Ezra**: But I'm not special.

**爱兹拉**：我并不比其他人类更崇高与伟大，我不值得获得殊荣，我与大多数人类一样——我只是一个普通的人类。\
**Ezra**: I am no greater than any other humans. I don't deserve to be treated differently. I'm just one of the majority, an ordinary human.

**爱兹拉**：既然我被乌卢鲁运动场接受，那其他人类自然可以踏足其中！\
**Ezra**: If I can be accepted by the Stadium, so can other humans!

爱兹拉的手掌按在红笔勾勒的计划地图上，巨大的弧线无声地向他划去。\
Ezra presses on the map dotted with red marks, dragging that arc he drew towards himself.

**沙丝绒**：可燃点，爱兹拉，你们先冷静一下——！现在不是吵架的时候！\
**Desert Flannel**: Spathodea, Ezra ... Guys, calm down! This is not the time for a fight!

**可燃点**：现在不是吵架的时候，什么时候是吵架的时候？\
**Spathodea**: This is not the time?! When shall we have it then?!

**可燃点**：世界上尽是人类的运动会，一个又一个、一个又一个的人类运动会！\
**Spathodea**: The world is full of sports games for humans! One after another and another!

**可燃点**：但世界上只有这么一个神秘学家的运动会呀！你们去管理自己的运动会还不够吗？\
**Spathodea**: But THIS, this is the only sports game for arcanists! Why don't you go mind your own games?

**可燃点**：人类把神秘术抢走了，加上科学，加上那些我听不懂的东西，那些我知道的戏法就变成了新东西——属于人类的新东西！\
**Spathodea**: And haven't humans stolen enough from us? They even made our arcane skills accessible to them. They modified arcane gadgets and added some science stuff and ... Bang! The arcane tricks I know suddenly became something new—some invention exclusive for humans' use!

**可燃点**：现在他们又要用合成金属架子来抢夺乌卢鲁运动场了——那是我找到的运动场，我是不会把它让给你们的！\
**Spathodea**: And now, they're even taking away the Uluru Stadium with metal bars?! It was me who found this Stadium, and I'm not giving it to anyone!

不甘示弱的姑娘一样伸手，将桌面上的地图拉向自己。\
Not to be outdone, the girl pulls the map to her side.

**爱兹拉**：抢夺……？\
**Ezra**: Taking away?

**爱兹拉**：我们，不……我，我从没有想过要抢夺任何东西，可燃点小姐。\
**Ezra**: We, no ... I-I have never thought of taking anything away from you, Ms. Spathodea.

**爱兹拉**：我只是想为你提供帮助，拉普拉斯的大多数研究员也一样，我们生活在实验室中，我们读书，我们彻夜不眠——\
**Ezra**: I was just trying to help, like most of the Laplace researchers. We spend most our time in the lab, we read, we study day and night ...

**爱兹拉**：我们从来都不是为了人类的崇高，也不是为了神秘学家的名誉！\
**Ezra**: We weren't doing it to make humans noble, nor for arcanists!

**爱兹拉**：那些结果——那些，神秘学与科学的结晶，它们的诞生是为了创造便利，为所有人创造便利。\
**Ezra**: Those products and achievements ... They are the fruit of the combination of arcanum and science. They were made to make everyone's life better.

一股力道，充满着憋闷和不解。\
One side is full of sullen resentment.

**可燃点**：便利？什么便利！别以为我没看过拉普拉斯科算中心的广告！\
**Spathodea**: Make life better? Get out! You think I never saw the ad of Laplace?

**可燃点**：以科学引导神秘学，以理智驾驭无序的力量——这不都是你们对外说的话吗？！\
**Spathodea**: "Guide arcanum with science, tame the orderless power with sense." That's what you tell the people!

另一股力道，满是不甘和委屈。\
The other side seems unwilling and filled with grievance.

可燃点将身体越过桌面，愤怒让她的脸颊发红、滚烫。\
Spathodea cranes out to Ezra, her face flushed with anger.

**爱兹拉**：……理智将引导感情，好让它不至于覆灭于自身燃起的烈火。\
**Ezra**: Sense will guide sentiments, so as to prevent the latter from destroying itself in the flames.

**爱兹拉**：你需要悉心地对待火焰，了解它们，保护它们远离危险……这是我所受到的教育，也是我一直以来践行的原则。\
**Ezra**: You have to attend to the flames carefully, to understand them, protect them from danger ... This is what I've been taught, and this is also the principle I've always acted upon.

**爱兹拉**：现在，我们所处的手提箱也正放置于人类与人类用手掌搭建出的入口！你正立于其上，你不该如此揣测他们！\
**Ezra**: And this very suitcase that we are staying in is also placed at the entrance made by humans! You shouldn't think so ill of them when you're standing on it!

理智的漂亮孩子眉间紧皱，握着钢笔的手指用力得发白。\
The rational, delicate boy frowns and grips the pen until his finger whitens.

**爱兹拉**：我们想提供帮助，仅此而已！\
**Ezra**: We were only trying to help, that's all!

平整的桌面上，修缮计划图纸被扯成了两半，如同一条难以弥合的裂谷。\
Rip! The drawing is torn into two pieces, underneath which the table in between seems like the King's Canyon.

**可燃点**：我回去了！我和这种无礼的家伙没有任何好谈的！\
**Spathodea**: I'm out! It's pointless arguing with a rude human who has no respect for arcanists!

可燃点快步离去，她的脚步越来越快，越来越快，直至几近奔跑，最终砰地一声，将自己关入了走廊尽头的房间。\
First trotting, then scooting and running, Spathodea storms toward the room at the end of the hallway. "Bang!" She slams the door and shuts the world out.

**爱兹拉**：……\
**Ezra**: ...

**爱兹拉**：对不起，我也先回去了。\
**Ezra**: Sorry, I will go back to my room now.

深深地低下头，另一个孩子逃也似的离开了桌面。\
Head lowered and murmuring, Ezra runs away from the table as if chased.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：这是一张很好的地图。\
**Vertin**: It's a nice map.

伸出双手，左右拼合，纸张上巨大的裂痕依旧难以忽视。\
She puts the two pieces together, but the crack on the paper still can't be ignored.

**维尔汀**：它不应该就这样碎掉……不是吗？\
**Vertin**: It shouldn't be left in halves. What do you think?

**沙丝绒**：我不喜欢半途而废，也没有搞砸过任何工作——\
**Desert Flannel**: I don't like the idea of giving up, and I have never messed up a job once I took it.

沙丝绒按住地图左侧的一半，将右侧推往燃烧的火焰面前。\
Desert Flannel pushes the left half of the map towards the burning flame.

**沙丝绒**：我负责这个，你……负责这个？怎么样？\
**Desert Flannel**: I'll take care of this, and you look after that. What do ya say?

**和平乌鲁**：……\
**Ulu**: ...

**维尔汀**：和平乌鲁？你还好吗？\
**Vertin**: Ulu? Are you alright?

**和平乌鲁**：没关系，我只是……感觉有些恍惚……\
**Ulu**: I'm fine. I just ... feel a bit dizzy ...

**和平乌鲁**：从上次和那些本耶普战斗后，我总觉得脑子有些昏沉，有时还会感到身体痒痒的……我想这可能是因为我还没有完全恢复。\
**Ulu**: My head has been feeling heavy since the battle against the Bunyips, and sometimes even my body feels itchy. I think I'll be fine after I fully recover.
