和平乌鲁摇着头，拾起残破的纸张。\
Ulu shakes her head and picks up the broken map.

**和平乌鲁**：这半张地图就交给我吧，我会和她好好谈谈的。\
**Ulu**: Leave this half to me. I'll talk to her.

**维尔汀**：辛苦你了，和平乌鲁。我会再和拉普拉斯询问是否可以增加你的助燃剂剂量的。\
**Vertin**: Thanks, Ulu. I'll request another raise of your accelerants from Laplace.

**维尔汀**：沙丝绒负责那一侧，我也会继续推动基金会方面的许可证书事宜。\
**Vertin**: Desert Flannel, you take care of Ezra. I'll follow the progress of the Foundation's examination.

**维尔汀**：行动起来吧，朋友们。\
**Vertin**: Let's move, friends.

桌边的人一个接一个离去，最终只剩下几只零落的座椅。\
The people set out for their targets one after another, leaving only empty chairs in the room.

**本耶普**：……嘶嘶。\
**Bunyip**: Ssss ...

一抹煤渣般的小小的黑色由一处阴影中走出。\
A small figure as black as cinder walks out of one pool of shadow.

紧接着跃入另一处阴影，消失无踪了。\
And then vanishes into the other.

**报社主编**：你说的是什么话！什么叫没有新消息了？！\
**Chief Editor**: What the heck did you say?! What do you mean "no other progress"?!

**报社主编**：乌卢鲁运动场修缮进度——谁会为了这个买你们的报纸？！\
**Chief Editor**: Progress of the Uluru Stadium Renovation. Who the heck will buy our newspaper for this piece of s**t?!

两撇八字胡在愤怒的鼻息下瑟瑟发抖。\
His mustache quivers with every angered breath.

**马科尔**：……对不起，主编。\
**Makower**: Sorry, Sir.

**马科尔**：我们已经很久没有得到复兴小队的信息。在上次报道风波后，他们已经有两周左右没有离开过那个箱子了。\
**Makower**: We haven't been able to find anything new about the Revival Squad for a long time. They didn't even step out of that suitcase in the last two weeks after we got their names in the papers.

**马科尔**：我们放出的信子也还没有音讯……呃！\
**Makower**: Neither did we hear anything from the sources … Ugh!

成沓稿纸摔打在马科尔阴沉的脸上。\
A file filled with papers is thrown into Makower's face.

**报社主编**：我接收你这种声名狼藉的家伙在新闻界，可不是为了拿到这么无聊的消息的！\
**Chief Editor**: I'm not hiring a notorious journalist like you for this boring news!

**报社主编**：去！再给我去找——找到像是“乌卢鲁运动会复兴小队与兔女郎大闹市政厅”一样，有趣儿、有味道又爆炸的东西来！\
**Chief Editor**: Get out and find more! Some big and breaking news like that REVIVAL SQUAD OF ULURU GAMES IN CITY HALL WITH BUNNY GIRL!

一阵河马般的咆哮后，主编摔门而去。\
The chief editor storms off, leaving his lion roar lingering in the room.

**马科尔**：……\
**Makower**: ...

**本耶普**：嘶嘶——嘶……！\
**Bunyip**: Sss ... SSS!

**马科尔**：……呵，真巧，是你回来了。\
**Makower**: ... Heh, it's you. Good timing.

身形小巧的本耶普蛇一般地爬上马科尔的身体，盘踞在他的手指上。几秒之后，便化作了一团墨渍。\
The tiny Bunyip swiftly crawls up Makower's leg and winds around his finger. Seconds later, it turns into a spot of ink.

**马科尔**：乌卢鲁运动会濒临破裂，复兴小队……内讧，不和！我就知道，你们如此愚笨，一定会自取灭亡——！\
**Makower**: The Uluru Games on the edge of total disruption, the Revival Squad ... turn against each other! I knew it, a group of monkeys ...!

**马科尔**：多有趣的消息啊……主编和她都一定会满意的。\
**Makower**: This is fun. The chief editor and that chick will both enjoy this.

**马科尔**：呵呵，呵呵呵呵呵……咳咳……\
**Makower**: Heh-heheheheheh ... *coughs* ...

马科尔的身影在阴影中抖动，抖动，抖动，直到剧烈地摆动起来。\
His body keeps trembling, trembling, and trembling, until he can't help but let out uncontrollable laughter.

## RUG-11 玻璃鞋 / Glass Slippers

房间的门紧闭着。\
The door is closed.

**维尔汀**：你好，我是维尔汀。\
**Vertin**: Hi, it's Vertin.

**维尔汀**：沙丝绒小姐，爱兹拉还和你在一起吗？\
**Vertin**: Ms. Desert Flannel, is Ezra still with you?

等待之后，房间的门仍是紧闭的。\
After a while, the door is still closed.

**维尔汀**：……沙丝绒小姐？\
**Vertin**: Ms. Desert Flannel?

门的那一侧充满了沉默。\
Silence is the only answer.

**维尔汀**：可燃点决定独自承担维修队的调度工作，和平乌鲁陪伴她一同前往施工场地，我想来看看你们的情况。\
**Vertin**: Spathodea has decided to supervise the construction herself, and Ulu is now with her at the site. I'm wondering how you are doing with Ezra.

**维尔汀**：仍旧没有回应，难道是……\
**Vertin**: No response. Are they ...

**维尔汀**：果然，他们不在房间里。\
**Vertin**: Not in the room, I knew it.

床边的木桌上留着一张纸条。\
A note has been left on the desk beside the bed.

**维尔汀**：……？\
**Vertin**: ...?

**维尔汀**：“我带爱兹拉出去见见世面，很快……就回来。”\
**Vertin**: "Showing Ezra what the world is like. Be right back."

**维尔汀**：“沙丝绒留。”\
**Vertin**: "Desert Flannel."

**沙丝绒**：小心脚下，也小心头上。\
**Desert Flannel**: Watch your feet and your head.

**沙丝绒**：这儿的人从不往下看，你的鞋子很快就会变得漆黑又破烂。\
**Desert Flannel**: The people here never look down. That's how you get muddy shoes when you're out of here.

**沙丝绒**：——来，拉住我的手。\
**Desert Flannel**: Here, take my hand.

**爱兹拉**：沙丝绒小姐，这到底是哪儿？我们来这儿做什么？\
**Ezra**: Ms. Desert Flannel, what is this place? What are we doing here?

**沙丝绒**：……做要做的事，说些要说的话。\
**Desert Flannel**: Something that needs to be done, and something that needs to be said.

人群欢呼的声音越来越大，队伍也愈加拥挤。\
The deeper they go, the louder the cheering they hear from the crowd.

**沙丝绒**：嘿！大个子，别挡路，让开！\
**Desert Flannel**: Hey! Big bloke, don't get in my way!

高大的身影侧开，直射灯掠过爱兹拉的眼睛，将其视线打成一片惶惶然的白。\
The big guy steps aside. A ray of light penetrates the air and pierces Ezra's eyes, and the only thing he can see is boundless white.

**爱兹拉**：唔——这是……\
**Ezra**: Emm ... this is ...

**沙丝绒**：澳大利亚式橄榄球锦标赛的预热场。这可不是正式比赛，但所有人都热心得发狂，总的来说……一票难求。\
**Desert Flannel**: The warm-up of the rugby game. It's not a formal game, but the audience enthusiasm is burning. I mean ... it's hard to get the ticket.

**沙丝绒**：但我是沙丝绒，我在街道上有些名气，这不仅仅局限于墨尔本。\
**Desert Flannel**: But I'm Desert Flannel, and I know people on the streets. Even when we're outside Melbourne.

**爱兹拉**：抱歉，我过去从没有看过体育比赛，我也不明白橄榄球的规则。\
**Ezra**: Sorry, I've never watched any games, and I don't know the rules of rugby.

**爱兹拉**：我……可能会看不懂这场比赛，这会让你感到失落吗？\
**Ezra**: I ... I don't think I will understand any of this. Do you mind?

**沙丝绒**：不，不会。因为我们的重点不是那个。\
**Desert Flannel**: No, I'm cool with that, because the game is not what we are after.

**沙丝绒**：你瞧，那是汤姆，一个不可忽视的澳式橄榄球新星，有史以来最好的拦截手。他来自墨尔本帆车俱乐部。\
**Desert Flannel**: You see that guy over there? That's Tom, a shining new star in the NRL, the best fullback they've ever had. He's from the Melbourne Sail Car Club.

**沙丝绒**：他们的吉祥物是一只海鸥，嘴里叼着一条鱼和一根薯条。\
**Desert Flannel**: They have a seagull as their club's mascot, with a fish and a chip in its mouth.

**爱兹拉**：是的……？我明白了？\
**Ezra**: Yes ...? Okay ...?

**沙丝绒**：而那一位——那是基普卡尔，他来自霍巴特蓝湖俱乐部，擅长拳击球，外号是“猛击卡尔”。\
**Desert Flannel**: And that bloke over there. That's Kip-Karl of the Hobart Blue Lake. He's the kind of player who knows how to really tackle. They call him the Unbreakable K.

**沙丝绒**：最后，个子小一些的那个是拉塞尔，他看起来不够勇猛，但他却被称为“黄油跳鼠”，因为他总是在抢夺截球时敏捷得无人能敌。\
**Desert Flannel**: And lastly, I want you to look at that smaller guy. That's Russel. Doesn't look tough, does he? But he is the Slippery Jerboa, because, man, he is fast when he gets the ball.

**爱兹拉**：可这和我们有什么关系呢？我还是不明白……\
**Ezra**: But what is this to do with us? I still don't understand ...

**沙丝绒**：爱兹拉。\
**Desert Flannel**: Ezra.

**沙丝绒**：我要你猜猜看，他们之中有几个神秘学家。\
**Desert Flannel**: Guess how many of them are arcanists?

**主持人**：好球！好球！拉塞尔又得一球，漂亮的拦截！\
**Commentator**: Nice one! Nice one! Russel made it again! Excellent interception!

**主持人**：最重要的一分！跳鼠掉进黄油桶——跑吧，跑吧！拉塞尔！胜利是属于牧羊人队的！\
**Commentator**: The key score! Now the Jerboa is as slippery as butter! Run, run for it, Russel! Victory is going to the Shepherds of Melbourne!

绿茵场上，抢得一球的拉塞尔振奋呼嚎，在沾满泥土与草屑的运动服上划出胜利的十字。\
On the green field, Russel is roaring excitedly after his goal. He draws a cross symbolizing victory on his uniform stained with dirt and grass.

**观众**：拉塞尔！拉塞尔！拉塞尔！\
**Audience**: Russel! Russel! Russel!

**观众**：拉塞尔！拉塞尔！拉塞尔！拉塞尔！\
**Audience**: Russel! Russel! Russel! Russel!

人群的呼唤一浪更高过一浪。\
Wave after wave, the cheer of the audience swells through the field.

爱兹拉却被手臂处的一股拉力牵走，愈加远离了光辉闪烁的竞技场。\
Ezra, however, is pulled by a sudden force at his arm and heads out of the Stadium.

那是一条漆黑的地下通道。沙丝绒前进的脚步毫不迟疑。\
Inside a dark and long tunnel, Desert Flannel marches without hesitation.

**爱兹拉**：人类以身体坚韧与耐性出名，以此考虑……\
**Ezra**: Mankind is known for their physical resilience and endurance, that is to say ...

**爱兹拉**：汤姆与基普卡尔是人类，而灵巧富有技术和神秘特性的拉塞尔是神秘学家。\
**Ezra**: Tom and Kip-Karl are humans, while Russel, whose skills and unpredictability are his strength, is an arcanist.

**沙丝绒**：嗯～符合逻辑的猜想～\
**Desert Flannel**: Hmm. A reasonable deduction!

**沙丝绒**：强韧的身体，丰富的技术，这些的确应该是分属于人类与神秘学家的标签。\
**Desert Flannel**: Physical resilience and varied skills are indeed the respective features of mankind and arcanists.

**沙丝绒**：……但是，事情总是不如标签上写的那么简单。\
**Desert Flannel**: However, things are not as simple as they appear.

沙丝绒停在一扇门前，握住把手，向前推开。\
She stops at a door, turns the doorknob, and pushes it open.

汗水、尘土、青草地与应急药物的苦味混杂着呢喃的粗口扑面而来。\
What welcomes them is a mixed smell of sweat, dust, grass, and medicine, together with occasional curses.

鼻青脸肿的运动员们来了又去，没人顾得上往打开的门看一眼。\
Players, black and blue, are busy coming and going. Nobody has time to take care of these two trespassers.

**沙丝绒**：实际上，他们三个都是神秘学家。\
**Desert Flannel**: In fact, all of them are arcanists.

**跳鼠拉塞尔**：……该死，快把那玩意儿拿给我。嘶——呼……\
**Russel**: ... S**t, gimme that thing. *exhales*

**球队经理**：给你——当心点儿，别用太多了，止疼药会让你成瘾的。\
**Team Manager**: Here ... Be careful, don't overdose. Painkillers are addictive, you know.

**球队经理**：等会儿还有报纸等着采访你们这些冠军们呢！别在镜头前一副恍惚的样子，嘿，听我说——\
**Team Manager**: And the newspaper is gonna interview you champions, so don't get high in front of the camera. Hey, listen ...

**跳鼠拉塞尔**：呼……\
**Russel**: Emm ...

**沙丝绒**：运动是畅快的，但运动也是十分危险的。\
尤其是橄榄球、搏击、拳击一类肢体对抗为主的运动。\
**Desert Flannel**: Sporting is great fun, but it can also be dangerous, especially for sports like rugby, MMA, or boxing, which involve a lot of intense physical contact.

**沙丝绒**：而那些擅长于“康复”的神秘学家，理所当然地成为了其中最好的种子选手。\
**Desert Flannel**: And the arcanists, who are good at healing, will naturally become the best athletes of all.

**沙丝绒**：十五分钟，只需要十五分钟。大多数“康复”类神秘术的起效时间是十五分钟。在这十五分钟之前，他们使用止痛药帮助自己。\
**Desert Flannel**: … 15 minutes, that's all they take. Most of the arcane treatments take only 15 minutes to heal the patient. And before that happens, the athletes would just take painkillers to help themselves get through the game.

**沙丝绒**：在这十五分钟之后——他们光洁如新，如同崭新出厂的运动员娃娃。\
**Desert Flannel**: And after that 15 minutes, they are refreshed and healthy, like those athlete dolls you'd find in the souvenir store.

**沙丝绒**：他们可以豁出去滑铲，不管不顾地撞击，即使受了重伤，也不会因此缺席重要的赛季。\
**Desert Flannel**: They can slide, impact like a maniac, and don't have to worry about missing any important sporting sessions if injured.

**爱兹拉**：这是一种……优势？\
**Ezra**: This is an advantage?

**沙丝绒**：没错，一种不可思议的优势。但……但他们真的“没事”了吗？\
**Desert Flannel**: That's right, an unbelievable advantage. But ... are they really as good as they look?

**沙丝绒**：想吃饱饭，就要付出汗水。世界上从来没有这样轻松愉快的事儿。那些韧带损伤，不可逆的撕裂，它们都轻易而重复地不断出现……\
**Desert Flannel**: Their glory comes with a price. Ligament damage and the irreversible tears keep recurring ...

**沙丝绒**：那头房间里的大象一直都在。它左右踱步，发出声响，就像现在的我们一样。\
**Desert Flannel**: But there is still an elephant in the room. It paces around, making noises which are unfit for the place, like this conversation we're having in the locker room.

**沙丝绒**：但热血沸腾，但运动与孔武至上。没有人有空停下来，看一眼这怪声响的源头。\
**Desert Flannel**: But on the sports field, where the blood boils, power and strength are the only things that matter. Nobody has the time to stop and ask what we are doing here, just like they don't have the time to notice the elephant.

**爱兹拉**：……\
**Ezra**: ...

**沙丝绒**：十年前，来自布罗肯希尔的玛格丽特在球场上所向披靡。\
**Desert Flannel**: Ten years ago, Margret of Broken Hill was invincible on the court.

**沙丝绒**：去年8月，她死在冬日的最后一个夜晚。\
**Desert Flannel**: In August last year, she died on the last day of winter.

**爱兹拉**：是……习惯性损伤吗？常常重复受伤而后自愈的神秘学家，很大几率会患上习惯性损伤，他们的身体会变得过度敏感，仅仅行走都有可能造成扭伤或……骨折……\
**Ezra**: Did she die of recurrent injuries? It's very likely that arcanist athletes who repeatedly get injured and heal themselves would get hurt on the same body part in the future. Their body will become fragile. They might even twist their ankle from walking. Sometimes even break a bone or two.

**沙丝绒**：不。她死于药物过量。\
**Desert Flannel**: No. She died from an overdose.

**爱兹拉**：……！\
**Ezra**: ...!

**沙丝绒**：她需要的止痛药太多了……多到她的身体无法承受。\
**Desert Flannel**: She needed a horrific amount of painkillers to ease her pain, so much that her body was overwhelmed.

**爱兹拉**：这——这太不人道了……！\
**Ezra**: This, this is cruel!

**爱兹拉**：我们可以向上报告这种乱象，解决与肃清它们，给这些人提供帮助，让他们更好地运动——\
**Ezra**: We have to report this to the Foundation and solve it once and for all. The athletes could have played in a safer way if given help.

少年人的声音中少有如此的不自信，漂亮姑娘一样的脸上写满错愕。\
It's rare to see the boy being so unsure and nervous. An astonished look takes over his pretty girlish face.

沙丝绒沉吟片刻，转向他。\
Desert Flannel ponders and looks at him.

**沙丝绒**：但如果我说，神秘学家也是“无可选择”呢？\
**Desert Flannel**: But what if I tell you the arcanists also don't have a choice?

**沙丝绒**：天生体力更好的人类，可以利用自己的体力去成为第一名。\
**Desert Flannel**: For humans who have the talent for sports, they can win the medals with their physical strengths.

**爱兹拉**：而……神秘学家，也只是利用了自己的天赋……？\
**Ezra**: So, arcanists have to make the most of their advantages to keep abreast with their competitors?

沙丝绒沉默着点了点头。\
She silently nods.

**爱兹拉**：……\
**Ezra**: ...

**爱兹拉**：我……我从来都不知道……\
**Ezra**: I, I had no idea.

**沙丝绒**：对不起，真的。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm sorry, truly.

耸起肩膀，沙丝绒的手臂再一次搭在年轻孩子肩头，如同家中长姐一般将其拉入怀中。\
Desert Flannel once again puts her hand on his shoulder and pulls the boy into her arms in a sisterly embrace.

**沙丝绒**：我无意引起你的愧疚，也不想借此让你感到痛苦，但是爱兹拉，我也曾参加这些商业比赛，靠着奖金混饭吃。\
**Desert Flannel**: I didn't mean to make you feel guilty, nor did I deliberately put you in pain. But Ezra, I was once one of them. I used to live on the prize money.

**沙丝绒**：这一切都是真的，这一切……每分每秒都在发生。药物成瘾、早衰、不可逆的身体损伤……这就是每一个神秘学家运动员几乎必然的结局。\
**Desert Flannel**: I'm only telling the truth. It is happening every day, every moment, and every second. Drug addiction, premature senility, and irreversible physical damage ... This is almost a destined end for every arcanist athlete.

**沙丝绒**：而没有人会为此负责，俱乐部老板不会，比赛主办方也不会，滥用药物——纯粹的个人作风问题，仅此而已。\
**Desert Flannel**: And nobody is held accountable for this, not the clubs, or the hosts of the games. Drug abuse is a personal behavior, that's it.

**沙丝绒**：我不明白那些热爱运动的人，除了运动员之外不想从事任何职业的人将如何生活，如何面对，但他们的选择并不多。\
**Desert Flannel**: Those people who are passionate about sports and don't wanna lead a life without them ... I have no idea how they would make a living or handle a quiet life, so I know they don't have much of a choice.

**沙丝绒**：人类的运动界是慷慨的，他们从不拒绝神秘学家的加入，但它也是可悲的，就像是灰姑娘的姐姐与那双水晶鞋。\
**Desert Flannel**: The sport industry of humans is generous. They offer equal chances to human and arcanist athletes. But it's also cruel, and the athletes are like the girls in Cinderella story who wish their feet would fit the glass slippers.

**沙丝绒**：——总得有人削去脚跟，才能跻身其中。\
**Desert Flannel**: They have no choice but to cut off part of their heels to earn the glory.

**爱兹拉**：这不公平，这些运动与裁决方式并不合适神秘学家，他们……正在被不公地对待。他们不被允许，真正的加入……\
**Ezra**: This ... this isn't fair. These sports and rules are not appropriate for arcanists. They, they have been treated unjustly. They aren't taken seriously and respected as athletes ...

**爱兹拉**：而这之中，也有……可燃点吗……\
**Ezra**: Is ... is Spathodea ... one of them ...?

**爱兹拉**：所以她……才会，像是那样忽然的愤怒……\
**Ezra**: That's why she was ... so furious ...

**？？？**：这么说来，乌卢鲁运动会复兴小队成员不睦的传闻竟然是真的！\
**???**: So the rumor that they are turning against each other is true!

**马科尔**：镜头，看过来，这正是本次事件中的人类代表——\
**Makower**: Camera, this way. This is the human representative of the event ...

**爱兹拉**：……！\
你是，那个时候的……八卦记者？\
**Ezra**: ...! You, you are that paparaz- ...?

**马科尔**：这不是一个礼貌的称呼，爱兹拉先生。\
**Makower**: This is not how a polite kid would address others, Mr. Ezra.

**马科尔**：我只是一个对各位关怀备至的记者，恰巧在采访橄榄球运动员的途中，偶遇了两位。\
**Makower**: I'm just a concerned journalist who run into you while reporting a rugby game.

**沙丝绒**：小心你的行为，先生！这可是不折不扣的骚扰！\
**Desert Flannel**: Watch your mouth, mister! This is harassment!

拉扯着怀中的孩子，沙丝绒快步后退，转身之后，仍是镜头。\
She covers Ezra and rapidly moves backward, but behind them are still clicking cameras.

**爱兹拉**：我们已经没有退路了……！\
**Ezra**: We are cornered ...!

**沙丝绒**：那就打碎他们的镜头，让他们知道嚼舌根的下场。\
**Desert Flannel**: Then we will break his camera and let him know the price of being a long-tongued liar!

## RUG-12 千年独行 / Lone Journey

**维尔汀**：……可燃点。这并不全是你的错。\
**Vertin**: Spathodea, it's not all your fault.

修缮工具四散在地面上，工地上却无走动的人，年轻姑娘靠着木材堆坐下，把头埋进双手中。\
The tools are scattered all over the place, but no one is working at the site. The young girl sits on the ground, leaning against the timber and burying her head into her palms.

**可燃点**：不，别安慰我了，我做不好这个工作……\
**Spathodea**: No, you don't have to be nice. I'm not capable of the job.

**可燃点**：就跟我做不好填报表格一样，我管理不来修缮队伍，修缮小队的大家都回去了，我规划的时间安排得一团糟……\
**Spathodea**: I should've known when I couldn't even fill in some forms correctly. I don't know how to supervise the construction team. They all left and my schedule is in a mess now.

**可燃点**：我急躁又粗心……却对帮了我那么多忙的人发脾气……\
**Spathodea**: I'm hasty and careless. I actually lost my temper with the people who tried to help me.

**可燃点**：对……爱兹拉也是……呜……\
**Spathodea**: And, I also did that to Ezra ... *sobs*

低下的头更低，双手一个劲地揉着眼睛。\
Lowering her head even further, Spathodea sobs and rubs her eyes.

**可燃点**：我知道他没有坏心的，也知道他不是个坏人，也许有人类让我委屈，可那和他——和其他人，有什么关系呢……\
**Spathodea**: I know he has no ill intention, and he's not a bad guy. Maybe some humans mistreated us, but that has nothing to do with him ... and all the others ...

**可燃点**：我应该立刻从他眼前消失！我搞砸了乌卢鲁运动会，这一切都是不符合友爱精神的，我根本不是什么圣火祭司，我就是一个差劲的讨厌鬼……\
**Spathodea**: I should've got out of his face right away! I screwed up the Uluru Games. What I did was not out of friendship or sportsmanship at all. I'm just a nuisance not qualified for the Priestess.

**和平乌鲁**：小火，听我说……来，听我说。\
**Ulu**: Flammy, listen. Come here, listen to me.

火焰飘然，拭去小姑娘满脸湿漉漉的鼻涕和泪水。\
The flame flies near her and wipes the tears and snot off her face.

**和平乌鲁**：每个人都会犯错，我还在你心中沉睡时，你母亲这样教导过你，你还记得吗？\
**Ulu**: Everyone makes mistakes. That's what your mom told you when I was still asleep, remember?

**可燃点**：呜，嗯……我记得……\
**Spathodea**: *sobs* Yes ...

**和平乌鲁**：每个人都会犯错，而年轻人更甚。\
**Ulu**: Everyone makes mistakes, especially young people.

**和平乌鲁**：我们曾经一样年轻，在你面前自称长辈让我感到如此不适，可是现在——我的确要称呼你为孩子。\
**Ulu**: We were of the same age in the past. It feels awkward to talk like an elder to you, but now, I have to address you as "child."

**和平乌鲁**：你今年14岁，还记得那时候的我吗？我刚从火堆跃然而出，那样年轻，那样的缺少经历。我的火焰动人，也会灼烧人。我难以控制自己，难以理解他人。\
**Ulu**: You are 14 now. Remember what I was like at your age? I appeared out of the campfire, so young and naive. My flame was beautiful, yet lethal as well. I couldn't control myself, not to mention understand others.

**可燃点**：可是，我……\
**Spathodea**: But my ...

**可燃点**：我和你不一样，我真的说了很糟糕的话，我已经……\
**Spathodea**: My situation is different. I said something really bad, and I already ...

**和平乌鲁**：你不可能不犯任何错误，也不可能变得完美无缺，你需要面对它们，然后成长。要从污浊的河，走向清澈的溪流。\
**Ulu**: It's impossible that you make no mistake or do everything perfectly. You just need to face them and learn from them. You stepped into the muddy river, that's fine, just keep going towards the clean stream.

**和平乌鲁**：重要的是，你要认识到问题，然后对你伤害过的朋友道歉。\
**Ulu**: The point is, you must know your mistake and apologize to the friends you've hurt.

**和平乌鲁**：你……还有机会去成长，用来……避免漫长的悔恨。\
**Ulu**: You still have room for improvement and the opportunity to avoid the lasting regret.

**可燃点**：漫长的……悔恨？有什么比现在更让人悔恨的吗？我想不到更糟的情况了——和平乌鲁，我搞砸了……\
**Spathodea**: Lasting regret? What's worse than what I'm dealing with? I can't think of anything. Ulu, I'm screwed.

**可燃点**：也许过去的我更好，也许现在的我已经不一样了，我的名字改变了，我不再是你最好的搭档……也，也不是维尔汀、爱兹拉和沙丝绒的好搭档……\
**Spathodea**: Maybe Flammy is a better choice for you than Spathodea. My name has changed, and I can no longer be your best partner, neither can I be Vertin's good partner, nor Ezra's, nor Desert Flannel's.

小姑娘疑惑地抽噎着，脸颊上淌过一条小小的河流。\
The little girl asks her question, with uncontainable tears running down her cheeks.

**可燃点**：这是我的第二次人生，我依然像个傻瓜……过去的我是什么样子呢？我如何长大，我是否不再伤害我的朋友？不再和你争吵？\
**Spathodea**: This is my second life, but I still feel like an idiot. What was I like in the previous life? Did I grow up? Did I hurt my friend? Did I have fights with you?

**和平乌鲁**：……\
**Ulu**: ...

**和平乌鲁**：你还记得我们的争吵吗，小火？\
**Ulu**: Remember our fight, Flammy?

**可燃点**：我记得……我们好像是在争执一些小事，有关于谁才是第一场运动会最大的助力……\
**Spathodea**: Yes, we were arguing who contributed the most to the first Games. What a trifle!

**和平乌鲁**：没错。只为了这件小事，我们就吵得不可开交。\
**Ulu**: That's right. We had a huge fight, over this trifle.

**和平乌鲁**：我们从未想过超越对方，我们只是希望得到认同，得到爱，可最终——我们不再和对方说话。这样的时间持续了好几个昼夜。\
**Ulu**: We never meant to win the fight. All we wanted was recognition and love, but in the end, we didn't talk anymore. This lasted for several days.

**和平乌鲁**：我想去找到你，与你和好。\
**Ulu**: Then I tried to find you to make it up.

**可燃点**：和好？我……我完全不记得这件事了——！\
**Spathodea**: Make it up? I-I don't remember that at all!

**和平乌鲁**：因为你没有等到我。\
**Ulu**: Because I didn't make it.

**和平乌鲁**：我找到你时，你正在远处，一只剧毒的红蛇游弋在草丛之中。不到几秒钟，蛇毒便让你失去了意识。\
**Ulu**: You were in the distance when I found you. The next second, you were attacked by a toxic red snake ambushing from the bush. Its venom made you pass out within seconds.

**和平乌鲁**：巫医在你床前徘徊了三日，而后，他们送你前往埋骨之地。我……再也没能对你道歉。\
**Ulu**: The witch doctors stayed by your bed for three days before they sent you to the grave. I didn't even have the chance to apologize.

微弱的火焰摇曳不断。\
The dim flame keeps flickering.

大颗大颗的眼泪从和平乌鲁眼中涌出，落入火焰中，滋滋地化作一阵蒸汽。\
Large tears roll down Ulu's face and drop into the fire, evaporating into steam, sizzling.

**和平乌鲁**：你从未长大过，我的朋友。\
**Ulu**: You never grew up, my friend.

**和平乌鲁**：我在漫长的时间中成为了一个老人，而你现在再一次成为了一个青春期的姑娘。\
**Ulu**: I'm already an old flame after such a long time, while you are still a teenage girl.

**和平乌鲁**：所以——我多愉快能再看见你，又多遗憾，我曾与你起过隔阂。\
**Ulu**: So, I'm really happy to see you again and really sorry that we once grew apart.

**可燃点**：我明白了……和平乌鲁，谢谢你告诉我这一切。\
**Spathodea**: I see. Thank you for telling me, Ulu.

可燃点张开双手，将朋友拥入怀中。\
Spathodea opens her arms and wraps her friend.

她的胸口很快被打湿，那些泪水很快又在火的温热中化作一股暖意。\
She feels tears dripping on her chest, but soon they get warm inside the heat of the flame.

**可燃点**：你曾经住在我的心里，好朋友，我们曾经在一具躯体里燃烧。\
**Spathodea**: You were in my heart, dear friend. We once burned together as a whole.

**可燃点**：没有人会比你更懂，我的心脏如何跳动——我会长大的，如你期望的一样。\
**Spathodea**: No one knows my heartbeat better than you do. I will grow up, as you wish.

**可燃点**：我会找到爱兹拉，和他和好——\
**Spathodea**: I will find Ezra and make it up to him.

**沙丝绒**：哈……那可太——太巧了……刚说到我们，我们这就回来了！\
**Desert Flannel**: Ha ... Isn't that convenient ...? Here we are!

撑着膝盖，沙丝绒拨顺散乱的头发，大口呼吸着。\
Hair messed up, the owner of the voice supports herself with hands on her knees, panting.

**维尔汀**：沙丝绒？还有爱兹拉？你们怎么这样气喘吁吁的？\
**Vertin**: Desert Flannel? Ezra? What's the hurry?

**沙丝绒**：就——就刚刚！该死，那些家伙追得也太紧了吧！\
**Desert Flannel**: That ... That was ... Hell, those guys were chasing us like crazy!

**沙丝绒**：总之，这就是我们气喘吁吁的原因了——我们被记者跟踪了，在沙漠里奔跑的时候，又遇上了一堆魔鬼蜥蜴……！\
**Desert Flannel**: Anyway, that's why we are out of breath. A paparazzi was following us, and as we were running in the desert, we-we ran into a bunch of Thorny Devils!

**维尔汀**：先处理好这些麻烦，然后再慢慢谈吧。\
**Vertin**: I see. We'll deal with this problem before we talk.

**维尔汀**：再等我五分钟，我很快就能让他们再也不能骚扰我们。\
**Vertin**: Give me five minutes. They will no longer be a problem for us.

**可燃点**：嘿——呀！火焰！上勾拳！！\
**Spathodea**: Hah! Fireee uppercuuut!!

**魔鬼蜥蜴**：咔啊——！\
**Thorny Lizard**: GAAAAARH!

强烈的反击下，魔鬼蜥蜴们嘶嘶呜鸣着，退回了渐黑的夜色中。\
The counterattack finally stops the Thorny Devils. Hissing and moaning, the monsters turn tails to hide in the darkness.

**可燃点**：太好了！这些家伙终于走了！\
**Spathodea**: Yes! Finally drove them away!

**记者**：你们几位曾在半月前登上名为《火焰、袋鼠、住房焦虑将刺痛谁的心灵？》的报道专栏。\
**Journalist**: Two weeks ago, you were in the column WHOSE HEART IS HURT BY FIRE, KANGEROOS AND HOUSING STRESS?.

**可燃点**：……？\
**Spathodea**: ...?

但另一种麻烦，则在黑暗中愈加闪光、刺眼。\
Yet another trouble is approaching, accompanied by dazzling flash lights.

**记者**：您们对此有何解释，又有何想法呢？\
**Journalist**: Would you care to make a statement?

**和平乌鲁**：那只是一个意外！绝非真正的失职！\
**Ulu**: That was just an accident! Not a misconduct!

**和平乌鲁**：火，火焰总有失控的时候，毕竟那是火焰，年轻人们——\
**Ulu**: F-Fire goes out of control very easily, as it's fire, after all. Young people ...

**马科尔**：另一方面，前些日子您与您的党羽被目击到骑乘着木质玩具马，在街头追击一枚金属色不明飞行物。\
**Makower**: Besides, you and your fellow team members were seen chasing after a metal UFO on the back of a wooden horse.

**马科尔**：据爆料者称，乌卢鲁运动会的再启动全由外星神秘势力推动，而您已被外星人控制大脑，您是否愿意配合进行身体检查？\
**Makower**: Rumor also has it that an alien power is behind the revival of the Uluru Games, and the very power has also controlled your mind. Would you run a check-up to clarify?

**爱兹拉**：……怎么会呢，星之眼先生无比善良，绝不会有任何坏心思！\
**Ezra**: What do you mean? Mr. aliEn T is good and kind. He has never had any ill thoughts!

**记者**：“星之眼先生”，这是它的名字吗？\
**Journalist**: Huh? Mr. aliEn T? Is that the name?

记者眼中迸发出惊喜的光，无数话筒齐刷刷地伸向爱兹拉。\
Excitement beams from the journalists' eyes. Countless microphones are reached out towards Ezra.

**爱兹拉**：……唔！\
**Ezra**: ... Uh ...

**马科尔**：看来，您与外星人交往甚密，或许您也参与了那些妄图篡夺地球的邪恶勾当？您是一名邪恶的科学家吗？\
**Makower**: So you've known this alien well. Are you involved in the evil plans of taking over Earth? Are you an evil scientist?

**马科尔**：作为一名来自于拉普拉斯的邪恶科学家，您可以谈谈您第一次见到“星之眼”先生的地点和想法吗？\
**Makower**: When and where did you first meet this alien as an evil scientist working for Laplace? What was your first thought of the meeting?

**维尔汀**：问题的答案远比各位想的更简单。\
**Vertin**: The answer is much simpler than you think.

**宽檐帽**：术式的白光闪烁，一道剪影从空气中逐渐成形。\
**Slouch Hat**: An arcane ritual shimmers, silhouetting a figure against the light.

**维尔汀**：我与星之眼先生的相遇并不复杂。\
**Vertin**: Mr. aliEn T and I met in a very simple way.

**维尔汀**：地点在美国，新墨西哥州，圣洛夫基金会分部的办公室内。\
**Vertin**: It was in the office of a Foundation branch, New Mexico, USA.

**维尔汀**：当时的想法……嗯，这里有“一个飞碟”。\
**Vertin**: My first thought ... Well, "There's a 'UFO' here."

**可燃点**：维尔汀，你终于回来了！嗯？你身边的那个东西是什么……？\
**Spathodea**: Vertin, you're back! Hmm? What's that thing beside you?

**宽檐帽**：你好，可燃点小姐，我听说过你的伟大故事——\
**Slouch Hat**: Greetings, Ms. Spathodea. I've heard about the legendary story of yours.

**宽檐帽**：一只澳洲宽檐帽，装点着鹦鹉羽毛，独自飘在空中。\
**Slouch Hat**: An Australia slouch hat decorated with a parrot feather is floating in the air beside Vertin.

**维尔汀**：是一只帽子。\
**Vertin**: He's a hat ...

**维尔汀**：也是我们的帮手。\
**Vertin**: As well as a helping hand.

**宽檐帽**：各位好，我是宽檐帽。\
**Slouch Hat**: And greetings to everyone. I'm Slouch Hat.

**马科尔**：该死，赶快撤退……！\
**Makower**: D**n it, go, go!

**宽檐帽**：相信各位媒体行业的朋友们与他们不同，大多数都认识、听闻过我的名字。\
**Slouch Hat**: Unlike them, I'm sure most of you in the media industry know or at least have heard of me.

**宽檐帽**：宽檐帽轻轻飞起，在空中浮动，如同有人将其按在胸口，向人群行礼。\
**Slouch Hat**: Slouch Hat flies in the air elegantly, as if its invisible owner took it off from their head, put it before his chest, and bowed to the people.

**宽檐帽**：我来自北澳大利亚游骑护卫队，是一名快乐的骑手。与此同时，也在圣洛夫基金会澳大利亚分部担任新闻发言负责人。\
**Slouch Hat**: I'm a member of the Northern Australia Rangers, also the spokesman of the St. Pavlov Foundation Australia Branch.

**宽檐帽**：我部近日批准再度开启的乌卢鲁运动会一直聚集着各界目光，与此同时，也有一些虚假消息借此机会甚嚣尘上。\
**Slouch Hat**: These days, the re-opening of the Uluru Games has attracted much focus, and speculations have reached such a pitch that we have to respond.

**宽檐帽**：在此，我将代为回答有关于各位对乌卢鲁运动会的问题……\
**Slouch Hat**: Here I will answer your questions about the Uluru Games ...

**宽檐帽**：——就从你开始吧，热心的马科尔先生。\
**Slouch Hat**: Starting from you, the ardent Mr. Makower.

已经走出一些距离的人群尴尬地定住身形，其中领头者缓慢地转回身体。\
Called by their name, the leader of the crowd slowly turns around.

**马科尔**：……当然，不胜荣幸。\
**Makower**: Of course, it's my pleasure.

**沙丝绒**：啊哈！你们看到马科尔那个表情了吗——！\
**Desert Flannel**: Haha! Did you see Makower's face?

**沙丝绒**：看起来真是太爽了，畅快！开心！愉快！有了基金会分部的人撑腰——现在，他也只有收拾行李滚开的份儿了！\
**Desert Flannel**: Aah, it made my day. I feel happy! Contented! Overjoyed! Now that we have the Foundation's people on our side, he can b****r off for good!

**维尔汀**：你和他很熟吗？\
**Vertin**: You know him well?

**可燃点**：应该是仇人才对，维尔汀。\
**Spathodea**: He's her enemy, Vertin.

**维尔汀**：……你和他是仇人吗？\
**Vertin**: He's your enemy?

**沙丝绒**：啊——啊啊，话可不能那么说，他和我不是仇人，我和他几乎就是陌生人——\
**Desert Flannel**: Ah ... Ah-ah, mind what you're saying! We are not enemies. I don't even know him.

**可燃点**：陌生人？仇人？我不太能理解这其中的关系……\
**Spathodea**: You don't even know him? And he's not your enemy? I don't quite get your relationship.

**和平乌鲁**：普世的男女之间总会有些复杂的故事，你们还年轻，如果活到了我这样的岁数，自然就可以理解了。\
**Ulu**: Things can be complicated between men and women nowadays. You're still too young to understand it. Don't worry. You will get it at my age.

**维尔汀**：原来这是一种需要年岁才能增长的见识。\
**Vertin**: So it's a kind of experience one must grow old enough to learn.

**维尔汀**：当前人类的平均年龄是50～75岁，我想，我应该没有机会追上您的年纪……\
**Vertin**: The current life expectancy is 50-75 years. I don't think I will ever reach your age ...

**沙丝绒**：不！才不是呢！别胡乱教这些小毛头！\
**Desert Flannel**: No no no! Don't put it like that! You're confusing the kids!

沙丝绒从沙发中弹起身子，双手在和平乌鲁与可燃点间摇晃，将她们分开到两侧。\
Desert Flannel bounces up from the sofa, waving her arms between Ulu and Ezra to separate them.

**沙丝绒**：现在就让我，我本人，故事主角，亲自和你们讲清楚！咳咳——\
**Desert Flannel**: Alright! Now, I, as one of the parties involved in this story, will explain it to you very clearly. Ahem …

**可燃点**：等一下！\
**Spathodea**: Wait!

**沙丝绒**：咳噗——咳咳，你等什么？！\
**Desert Flannel**: A-ah ... *coughs* What?!

**可燃点**：爱兹拉呢？爱兹拉怎么不在这里？\
**Spathodea**: Where's Ezra? He's not here!

**沙丝绒**：他好像刚刚就回房间去了，没和我们一起过来。\
**Desert Flannel**: He just went back to his room. He didn't come out when we left.

捂着呼吸不顺的喉咙，沙丝绒抬头示意爱兹拉房间的方向。\
Rubbing her neck to clear her throat, Desert Flannel nods in the direction of Ezra's room.

**沙丝绒**：你是要先去和爱兹拉谈心，还是听我这儿的小道消息？这么丢人的事儿，我可不打算说第二次。\
**Desert Flannel**: Are you going to talk to him first, or will you stay for my little anecdote? I won't tell the story again, it's way too embarrassing to tell it twice.

**可燃点**：我……嗯，我……\
**Spathodea**: I, emm ... I ...

犹豫几番。\
The girl hesitates.

孩子总归还是难敌一个故事。\
But kids can never say no to a story.

**可燃点**：我先听你的故事，然后马上就去找他——！\
**Spathodea**: I'll listen to your story first, and I'll go talk to him right away!

## RUG-13 “永不沉没” / "Unsinkable"

**可燃点**：嗯——灯光设备……没问题。\
**Spathodea**: Hmm ... Lights ... checked.

**可燃点**：入口处的宽度……没问题。\
**Spathodea**: Width of the entrance ... checked.

**可燃点**：顶部支撑结构……没问题。\
**Spathodea**: Support structure for the ceiling ... checked.

**可燃点**：用于转播比赛的摄影鹦鹉，嗯，毛茸茸的——没问题！\
**Spathodea**: Camera parrot for broadcasting the Games, hmm, very fluffy, so ... checked!

修缮完毕后的运动场亮堂而宽阔，可燃点缓步行走在红土跑道上。\
Spathodea walks slowly along the clay runway, under the wide and bright rooftop of the renovated Stadium.

**可燃点**：预备的圣火火炬、障碍赛道的布置、树枝坚韧度与红土块的温度……很好！这些都没问题！今天凌晨的开幕点火仪式只剩下一项需要检查了！\
**Spathodea**: Spare torch for the Uluru Flame, obstacles for Steeplechase, tenacity of the branches and temperature of the red clod ... Alright, checked! Only one more item to go before the flame lighting ceremony this midnight!

**和平乌鲁**：……呜呜。\
**Ulu**: *sobs*

**可燃点**：我们的圣火……和平乌鲁？你还好吗？\
**Spathodea**: The Uluru Flame ... Ulu? You alright?

**可燃点**：你——你怎么又哭啦？是我做什么事儿让你感觉难过了吗？\
**Spathodea**: Wh-What's with the tears?! Did I make you sad again?

**和平乌鲁**：哦，不……没什么，我只是眼睛里进了一些沙子——\
**Ulu**: No ... nothing. I just have sand in my eyes ...

**沙丝绒**：很正常，无论什么地方都可能有沙子。\
**Desert Flannel**: Oh, sand is common here. It gets into your eyes very easily.

**沙丝绒**：我奶奶第一次瞧见我走路时，很凑巧，也有那么一粒沙子。\
**Desert Flannel**: Just like when my granny saw me walking for the first time.

**和平乌鲁**：年轻人，你应该对老人的尊严放尊重一些！\
**Ulu**: Young lady, you should've preserved the dignity of this old flame!

**沙丝绒**：哇啊——好烫！\
**Desert Flannel**: Waah-ah! You burned me!

**可燃点**：……和平乌鲁，精神活跃，火焰灼热。没有问题。\
**Spathodea**: ... Ulu, burning hot and energetic, checked.

笔记本上画下一个新勾，可燃点向上抬起头。\
Ticking off another check in the notebook, Spathodea looks upwards.

**可燃点**：场地安全系数——也没问题。\
**Spathodea**: Safety factor of the field ... checked.

**可燃点**：拉普拉斯……真是帮了我们一个大忙呀……\
**Spathodea**: Laplace ... really did us a huge favor ...

**可燃点**：只可惜自从那天之后，我再也没有找到机会和爱兹拉好好说话，大家都很忙，而少有的几次……我们面对面时，也……\
**Spathodea**: Shame I haven't had the time to talk to Ezra since we had that fight. We were both busy, and when we met, it was ...

**沙丝绒**：什么？你们还没把话说开？可你们看起来和以前没什么差别啊——\
**Desert Flannel**: What? You haven't talked about it? But I didn't feel anything wrong between you two ...

**可燃点**：我们是和好了。这没有错。\
**Spathodea**: We did make up, that's for sure.

**可燃点**：但我们从来没好好聊过那场矛盾呀，那就像是摔伤了腿，却把裤子放下来，就当看不见伤口一样——\
**Spathodea**: But we never really talked about the fight. It's like you break your knee and just cover the wound up with trousers, as if it had never been there …

**可燃点**：跑跑跳跳时都没问题，可一安静下来呢，膝盖就发疼……\
**Spathodea**: You may feel fine when you jump and run, but it hurts whenever you sit down for a break ...

挠了挠头发，紧接着，可燃点又愁眉苦脸地去抠手指。\
She scratches her hair and then starts to play with her fingers, a glum look on her face.

**可燃点**：哎……也不知道爱兹拉和维尔汀的巡查确认得顺不顺利。\
**Spathodea**: *sighs* I wonder if Ezra and Vertin are going well with the patrol.

**和平乌鲁**：放轻松点，小火。\
**Ulu**: Relax, Flammy.

**和平乌鲁**：开幕仪式就在明天，我们检查这张表单上的内容比检查松针织成的长衫更细密。躲在阴影中的本耶普已许久未曾露面……\
**Ulu**: It will be the opening ceremony tomorrow. Our checklist is even more intricately designed than a robe made with pine needles. Besides, the Bunyips haven't turned up in quite a while ...

**和平乌鲁**：一切都像是最稳定的船一样行驶在海面之上，缺少沉没的契机。\
**Ulu**: Everything is working like an unsinkable ship at sea. There isn't anything that may cause it to sink.

**可燃点**：好吧……可是，上一艘自称为“永不沉没”的船，好像是那个——那个什么来着……\
**Spathodea**: Alright ... but the last ship that claimed to be "unsinkable," um, what was it called ... um …

苦思冥想的姑娘身后，紧闭着的石门猛地被推开。\
The stone door is opened without warning from behind the thinking girl.

**可燃点**：啊！对了——！\
**Spathodea**: Oh! I got it!

**爱兹拉**：不好了，出事了！\
**Ezra**: We have an emergency!

**可燃点**：那艘船是——泰坦尼克号！\
**Spathodea**: It's called the Titanic!

**观众**：我是买了票的！让我进去！\
**Audience**: I've bought tickets! Let me in!

**观众**：我大老远跑过来都是为了乌卢鲁运动会——你们告诉我这是第一届允许所有人进入的乌卢鲁运动会！\
**Audience**: I came all the way here just for the Uluru Games, because you said that it is open to all for the first time!

**马科尔**：稍安勿躁，各位观众。\
**Makower**: Everyone, please be patient.

手持一支麦克风，马科尔站在一处略高于地面的石群上。\
Holding a microphone, Makower stands on a pile of rocks, making him stand out from the group.

空中的飞艇卷起旋风，让疲劳的旅人们步履更显蹒跚。\
The whirlwind brought up by the airship only makes the travelers' steps more staggered.

**马科尔**：我们已经到达了乌卢鲁运动场的门口——正是在这里，传闻中的“轮回者”将会携带着炙热的火焰，降下雨水！\
**Makower**: We are now standing at the entrance to the Uluru Stadium, and this is where the rumored "reincarnator" will come with flames and bring about the rain!

**马科尔**：抚慰所有虔诚而干渴的嘴唇，沁润所有龟裂而破损的足底！\
**Makower**: The rain will comfort the thirsty travelers and soothe their dry heels!

**马科尔**：我以乌卢鲁运动会使者的身份对你们保证，无论人类或是神秘学家，每一位手持门票的观众都可以进入运动场！你们需要的只是诚心等待！\
**Makower**: I guarantee you, as the ambassador of the Games, that no matter what your lineage is, you are welcome here as long as you have a ticket! All you need to do is wait patiently and with sincerity!

**观众**：诚心？我们已经跟着引导人在沙漠打转了一整天了！\
**Audience**: Sincerity? We've followed the guide and circled around the desert for a whole day!

**观众**：我们需要水，也需要食物！有些年轻的孩子已经开始脱水了！\
**Audience**: We need water and food! Some kids have become dehydrated!

**观众**：没错！我们需要水！我们需要乌卢鲁运动场！你们得兑现你们的承诺！\
**Audience**: Yes! We need water! We need to get into the Uluru Stadium! You've promised us!

**观众**：我们需要水！我们需要乌卢鲁运动场！\
**Audience**: We need water! We need to get into the Uluru Stadium!

**马科尔**：没错，就是这样。就是这样。\
**Makower**: That's right, yes, that's right.

**马科尔**：复兴小队，我相信你们会喜欢我的这份大礼，我相信。\
**Makower**: Revival Squad, I'm sure you will enjoy this gift from me.

**观众**：我们需要水！我们需要乌卢鲁运动场！我们需要水！我们需要乌卢鲁运动场！\
**Audience**: We need water! We need to get into the Uluru Stadium! We need water! We need to get into the Uluru Stadium!

那呼唤声越来越响，像是要震动滚烫沙地的浪潮。\
Getting louder and louder, the rumble shakes the whole desert.

一股接着一股，在巨岩的上方回荡。\
And echoes above the giant rock.

**可燃点**：天啊——！！！他——那是——他啊！！\
**Spathodea**: Gosh!!! It's him, that guy!!

**可燃点**：这太无耻了！我们从来就没有售过票，也没有对外部邀请过这样多的人来参加运动会！他们怎么能这样说谎呢！\
**Spathodea**: How shameless! We never sold a single ticket or invited so many outsiders to the Games! How can they tell such a lie?!

**维尔汀**：他在创造舆论，这一直是他擅长的事情。\
**Vertin**: He's whipping up public opinion—just his greatest strength.

**维尔汀**：……根据刚才的短期观察，场外至少有三千五百名以上的观光客。\
**Vertin**: I took a glance at the crowd. There are at least 3,500 of them out there.

**维尔汀**：这不是马科尔一个人就可以调度的人数，一定还有人是他的帮手，那些人更擅长带队、诈骗或勒索一类的工作……\
**Vertin**: Not a number Makower can incite alone. Some of them must be his accomplices. I'm sure they are good at mobilizing, swindling, blackmailing and stuff ...

**沙丝绒**：是桉树兄弟会！那个带头闹事的男青年就是他们的人——我认识他们！\
**Desert Flannel**: It's the Eucalyptus Brotherhood! The leader is one of them. I know his face!

**沙丝绒**：该死，我拿了他们的票，他们八成也打算找我的麻烦，对上马科尔就这么一拍即合了！\
**Desert Flannel**: D**n it! Seems like they're not going to make this easy for me, since I took their tickets. And there's Makower—how convenient for them!

**可燃点**：我们不能让这些人继续留在这里了，没有运动场的帮助，他们没有水也没有食物，很快就会中暑的！\
**Spathodea**: We can't just leave them here. Outside the Stadium, they have no food or shelter. They will suffer sunstroke in no time!

**沙丝绒**：你想怎么处理这件事？\
**Desert Flannel**: How are you going to handle this?

**可燃点**：沙丝绒，你手上还有那些假票吗？\
**Spathodea**: Desert Flannel, do you still have those fake tickets?

**沙丝绒**：有，怎么了？\
**Desert Flannel**: Yeah, why?

**可燃点**：卖掉它们。\
**Spathodea**: Sell them.

**沙丝绒**：你在说什么胡话呢？！我现在为你做这些事早就不是为了钱了，我只是想——\
**Desert Flannel**: Excuse me?! I thought you knew that I'm not doing this for money. I'm doing it for ...

**可燃点**：我知道你需要钱的原因。\
**Spathodea**: I know why you need money.

**可燃点**：你要买下你祖母住了一辈子、养育你长大的房子。这对你很重要，就像是乌卢鲁运动会对我与和平乌鲁很重要一样。\
**Spathodea**: You have always wanted to buy the house where your grandmother spent her life and raised you. It's important to you, just like the Uluru Games to me and Ulu.

年轻的姑娘站起身体。\
The young girl stands up.

**可燃点**：爱兹拉、维尔汀，请你们分别联系官方进行求援，而沙丝绒，我需要你帮忙做好初步疏散与管理人群秩序的准备！\
**Spathodea**: Ezra, Vertin, please contact the Foundation for help. Desert Flannel, I need you to prepare to guide the crowd and maintain order!

**爱兹拉**：可燃点，难道你想——\
**Ezra**: Spathodea, you're not planning to ...

**可燃点**：放手去做吧，朋友们。\
**Spathodea**: Let's go all out, mates.

**可燃点**：我出发了。\
**Spathodea**: I am going.

揽起因泪水泛潮的和平乌鲁，甩开沙丝绒带着汗水的双手。\
Holding the Ulu soaked in tears in her arms, Spathodea shakes off Desert Flannel's sweaty hands.

干爽的热风从她身后吹拂而过，带起尘沙，也带出那扇缥缈的门扉。\
A dry breeze follows after her, kicking up the dust and forming that shadowy gate.

**可燃点**：……\
**Spathodea**: ...

**可燃点**：请大家都看向我——！\
**Spathodea**: Everyone, your attention, please!

人群骚动起来，细碎的声音如潮水般涌向她们。\
The crowd's attention turns, murmurs surround the girls like a vortex.

**观众**：那是……那是乌卢鲁的大门！就在她背后！是那个报纸上的女孩！\
**Audience**: Ah! That is the door of the Uluru Stadium! Behind her! She is the girl in the newspaper!

**观众**：什么？谁？那就是传说中的“轮回者”吗？！\
**Audience**: What? That girl is the "reincarnator"?

**观众**：天啊！是她！瞧啊——瞧那团火！那不就是报道中说的圣火吗？！\
**Audience**: Oh, dear, there she is! And look! That flame! Isn't that the Uluru Flame in the newspaper?

**观众**：为我们开门啊！圣火祭司！让我们见识见识乌卢鲁运动场吧！\
**Audience**: Open the gate for us, Priestess! Show us the Uluru Stadium!

**马科尔**：为我们打开门吧！我有票！我带着门票！\
**Makower**: Open the gate for us! We have tickets! We have tickets!

站在高处的马科尔高高抬起手臂，一张长条形的纸张夹在他的手中。\
Standing above the crowd, Makower raises his hands, showing everyone the ticket.

**观众**：为我们打开门吧！我们有票！我们有门票！\
**Audience**: Open the gate for us! We have tickets! We have tickets!

一呼百应。\
Like a summoning.

振奋的呼声裹挟着马科尔得意的质问扑面而来。\
A tumultuous clamor goes up from the crowd, punctuated by Makower's questioning.

**马科尔**：看看这些姑娘们吧！我亲爱的朋友们！可燃点小姐与和平乌鲁女士！\
**Makower**: Look at those girls, my friends! That is Ms. Spathodea and Ms. Ulu!

**马科尔**：报纸与电视上写满了她们的好话：促进人类与神秘学家的融合，为和平出一份力的新锐分子，与所有商业赛不同的体育精神赛事——\
**Makower**: The newspapers have been praising them for facilitating the union of mankind and arcanists, bringing back the true spirit of sporting events, and calling them the pioneer peacemakers ...

**和平乌鲁**：我以圣火的姿态起誓，那并非谎言！\
**Ulu**: In the name of the Uluru Flame, I swear it's not a lie!

**马科尔**：当然，当然，你们从来都是句句属实的。\
**Makower**: Of course, of course, you are not lying. You never lie.

**马科尔**：每一句话都来自你的真心，每一句也都来自你的真意！\
**Makower**: No lies have been spoken. Every word was true!

**马科尔**：一个来自墨尔本的中学生，一个古老的灵魂，一位“轮回者”，她会站在何处，她会想什么，她会做什么，请各位与我一起见证吧！\
**Makower**: A junior student from Melbourne, an old soul, a "reincarnator." What's her attitude, and what will she do? Please find out with me!

闪烁着银光的麦克风指向夜空，飞艇射灯打向年轻姑娘。\
The microphone in his hand points up at the sky, reflecting the airship's spotlight glaring down at Spathodea.

**可燃点**：……唔！\
**Spathodea**: ... Uh ...

雪片一般的录音相纸由空中落下。\
Scattering audio photos fall from the sky.

**“照片”**：“人类？人类为什么会在运动场里？”\
**"Photos"**: "Humans? What are they doing in the Stadium?"

可燃点的声音从中清晰地传出。\
People hear Spathodea's voice crystal clear.

**“照片”**：“世界上尽是人类的运动会，一个又一个、一个又一个的人类运动会！”\
**"Photos"**: "The world is full of sports games for humans! One after another and another!"

**“照片”**：“以科学引导神秘学，以理智驾驭无序的力量——现在他们又要用合成金属架子来抢夺乌卢鲁运动场了！”\
**"Photos"**: "Guide arcanum with science, tame the orderless power with sense" ... "And now they're even taking away the Uluru Stadium with metal bars!"

**和平乌鲁**：这，这些是——！\
**Ulu**: Th-That's ...!

**马科尔**：多可笑啊！她象征着和平，而她却将人类的安危、科技、帮助与权利置于不顾！\
**Makower**: How ridiculous! She said she stands for peace, yet she has never considered mankind's safety, technology, assistance, or rights!

**马科尔**：神秘学家——神秘学家！口口声声，只有神秘学家！\
**Makower**: Arcanists, arcanists ... that's all she's talking about!

**观众**：这是……圣火祭司？！她……她怎么会这样说——\
**Audience**: It's the voice of the Priestess? H-How could she say that ...

**观众**：怎么可能？这是一届有拉普拉斯人类科技参与的乌卢鲁运动会，他们在报纸上大谈平等融合，和平友爱——\
**Audience**: Nonsense! It is the first Uluru Games with the help of Laplace human technology. They've been talking about equality, peace and love all the time.

**观众**：该死，你们怎么能这样卑劣！\
**Audience**: D**n you! How could you be so despicable!

**观众**：这些建筑支架都来自于拉普拉斯！这可是货真价实的人类力量！\
**Audience**: All the constructions are built by Laplace! These are all human contributions!

**观众**：我要离开这儿！这不是乌卢鲁运动会——这根本就不是我在祖母故事里听到的乌卢鲁运动会！\
**Audience**: I'm out of here! It's not the Uluru Games, not the one I heard from my grandma at all!

**马科尔**：我们应该相信她是个诚恳的女孩，她的口中没有谎话！\
**Makower**: We should believe that she's an honest girl. She would never have lied!

**马科尔**：可燃点小姐，这是否曾是你的所为？\
**Makower**: Ms. Spathodea, did you really say that?

马科尔递交出自己的话筒，如同确认了自己的胜利。\
Makower passes the microphone to Spathodea, with a celebratory flair.

一只本耶普从他的外套内钻出来，贪婪地舔舐着空气，充气般地鼓胀起来。\
A Bunyip appears out of his coat. Its body starts swelling as it devours the air.

扭曲、挣扎，人们动荡的骚乱之中，谎言与不信任编织成就它的身体。\
From the turmoil of lies and distrust, it gains additional power.

**和平乌鲁**：小火，去面对它。\
**Ulu**: Flammy, confront it.

**和平乌鲁**：点燃它，征服它，使其燃烧……\
**Ulu**: Light it up, conquer it, and make it burn ...

**可燃点**：我明白，我完全明白你的意思。\
**Spathodea**: I will. I know what my duty is.

**可燃点**：你说得没有错，马科尔先生……\
**Spathodea**: You are right, Mr. Makower.

**可燃点**：这些都是我曾说过的话，我对此供认不讳！\
**Spathodea**: I did say that. I take responsibility for every word heard in that photo!

**可燃点**：所有人！请听我说——\
**Spathodea**: But people! Listen to me!

**可燃点**：那些话是错的，我是错的，我是个笨蛋、傻瓜，是树上头最苦最酸的坏果子！\
**Spathodea**: Those words are wrong, so am I. I am a fool, an idiot, the stinkiest rotten egg in the kitchen!

**可燃点**：我从墨尔本来到爱丽丝泉，来到乌卢鲁岩，我见过无数人类。\
**Spathodea**: I've seen countless humans on my way here, from Melbourne to Alice Springs, and then Uluru.

**可燃点**：我见过拉普拉斯的维修队，见过政府的文员小姐，见过体贴的医生，也见过——见过我的第一个人类好朋友！\
**Spathodea**: I've met the construction team from Laplace, the receptionist at the City Hall, the considerate doctors, and ... and my first human friend, my good friend!

**可燃点**：过去我想到人类，我总想到“另一种人”，想到难以理解的冷血家伙，想到一些人们常说的坏话和官方说辞——\
**Spathodea**: In the past, I saw humans as "the other kind." I thought they were unreasonable, cruel people who deceive others with bureaucratic jargon …

**可燃点**：可现在，我想到人类，我将会……\
**Spathodea**: But now, when I think of humans, I'm reminded of …

**可燃点**：将会……\
**Spathodea**: Of ...

**可燃点**：……我将会想到我的朋友。我温和的、勇敢的、聪明的、无私的、笨拙的人类朋友。\
**Spathodea**: Of my friend, my gentle, brave, smart, selfless, clumsy human friend.

**马科尔**：什、什么——你们该不会是要！\
**Makower**: Wh-What? Are you going to ...?!

**和平乌鲁**：面对它。点燃它。征服它。使其为你而燃烧。\
**Ulu**: Confront it, light it up, conquer it, and make it burn for you.

和平乌鲁引燃的火光灼烧向匍匐的本耶普。\
The flame lit by Ulu burns all the way to a crawling Bunyip.

不出片刻，甚至听不见响声，只一眨眼，红土上便只剩下了焦黑的痕迹。\
In an instant, the only thing left on the red soil is burned ashes. The Bunyip didn't even make a sound.

**本耶普**：呜——呜哈——！\
**Bunyip**: Ahh ... AHHH!!

余下的本耶普四散奔逃，钻入人群，钻入角落，引起阵阵尖叫。\
The rest of the Bunyips scatter. Fleeing into the crowd and corners, causing a chorus of screams.

**可燃点**：我也愿意相信，这里的每一个人都和我一样，热爱运动。\
**Spathodea**: And I'm willing to believe, everyone here loves sports as much as I do.

**可燃点**：我很抱歉我曾经是一个狭隘的笨蛋——\
**Spathodea**: I must apologize for being an idiot with such a narrow view. I'm sorry.

**可燃点**：可如今，我希望每个人都能体会到纯粹的运动与汗水流淌的快乐！\
**Spathodea**: Now, I hope everyone can enjoy pure sports and have fun sweating!

**可燃点**：有门票的朋友们！全都可以入场！\
**Spathodea**: Those of you who have tickets, please enter the Stadium in order!

**可燃点**：没有门票的朋友们——仅用一澳币便可在沙丝绒小姐处购得门票！\
**Spathodea**: Those of you with no tickets, you can buy one from Ms. Desert Flannel for just one dollar!

**可燃点**：乌卢鲁运动会，在此开启——！\
**Spathodea**: I hereby declare the opening of the Uluru Games!

门扉已然开启，人群的欢呼声中，小火高举手臂。\
The gate is already open. Flammy puts her arms in the air as the crowd cheers.

**可燃点**：而它会欢迎每一个人！\
**Spathodea**: Everyone is welcome!

**马科尔**：该死，怎么会……我得到的信息里，他们明明就十分不和！\
**Makower**: D**n it! How come ... The source has confirmed the rift between them!

**马科尔**：只要我溜得够快，我一定还有机会……\
**Makower**: Run, if I'm fast enough, there is still a chance.

挤出人群，抱紧怀中的相机，马科尔带着他的残党们仓皇而逃。\
Grabbing the camera tightly, Makower and his team hurry out of the crowd in a panic.

**沙丝绒**：但很有可能，你没有这个机会了。\
**Desert Flannel**: Or maybe, you don't deserve that chance at all.

站定身体。数十人堵住了小径的出口。\
A wall of people stand at the exit.

**维尔汀**：我们有帮手。\
**Vertin**: We've got a helping hand.

**爱兹拉**：还有另外一群帮手。\
**Ezra**: More than one hand.

**沙丝绒**：啊哈——\
**Desert Flannel**: Aha ...!

**沙丝绒**：民间通常将这种行为称之为“正义的群殴”。\
**Desert Flannel**: This is what we call "the hammer of justice."

**沙丝绒**：接招吧，讨厌的***烂舌头**，我会把你的舌头从你的眼窝里掏出来，谁叫你惹了不该惹的人呢，你一开始就该知道今天……\
**Desert Flannel**: Take that, you s****y little long-tongue pig. I will pull your tongue out through one of your eye sockets. You should have known better than to mess with me.

## RUG-14 跑者史诗 / The Epic of Runners

**维尔汀**：观众们已经入席就坐，并没有人因为踩踏或推搡受伤。\
**Vertin**: The audience are all seated. No stampede or jostle, not to mention injury.

**爱兹拉**：今晚到来的人类参赛选手已经登记完毕，相对应的人类独有与神秘学家混合运动项目也已草拟完毕——预计三日后开始进入比赛！\
**Ezra**: All the human athletes have registered, and their mixed sporting events with arcanist athletes have been properly planned and are ready to start in three days!

**沙丝绒**：哈啊——我不行了，我真的一根指头也动不了了……\
**Desert Flannel**: Aah! I'm done. I can't even move a finger right now.

这是几近于奇迹的结果。\
This is almost a miracle.

所有人都奔走着，奔走着，奔走着——像是蟒蛇吞食大象那样消化着过剩的工作。直到如今，一切都完成得如此恰好。\
Everyone is running, running, and running for the tremendous workload, like a python trying to digest an elephant. Fortunately, they manage to complete all the work just on time.

**和平乌鲁**：来吧，小火。\
**Ulu**: Come on, Flammy.

**和平乌鲁**：是我们出场的时候了——\
**Ulu**: It's our turn.

**可燃点**：……！\
**Spathodea**: ...!

**可燃点**：哈……哈哈，我们又一次一起走在这样璀璨的道路上了！和平乌鲁！\
**Spathodea**: Hah ... Haha, again we walk on this glorious path together, Ulu!

**和平乌鲁**：跑吧。\
**Ulu**: Run.

**和平乌鲁**：孩子，跑吧。\
**Ulu**: Get yourself running, child.

**和平乌鲁**：如同你曾许诺的一样——点亮那只乌卢鲁的火把！\
**Ulu**: Light up the Uluru torch, as you have promised!

**可燃点**：如同……我曾许诺的一样！\
**Spathodea**: As ... I have promised!

心脏砰砰直跳，肋骨根部颤颤，如同一只鸟儿寄宿在胸膛中，正想振翅而去。\
Her ribs tremble excitedly as Spathodea's heart flutters like a bird, now flapping its wings to fly away.

可燃点的脚步是轻快的，与她愉快的心一样，与她疲惫的身体不同。\
Tired as her body is, the way Spathodea runs is as lively as her heart.

**可燃点**：我在奔跑，而千百年前的奔跑于我而言正如昨日。\
**Spathodea**: I am running. Even though the day I last ran here was a thousand years ago, it feels just like yesterday to me.

**可燃点**：我跑过漫长的跑道，我脚踩着炙热的红土，我正在流汗，如同一枚闪闪发亮的星星！我将要前往赛场的最高处，点亮那只火把——\
**Spathodea**: I run across the long track, stepping on the burning red soil. I am sweating, like a sparkling star! I am going to the top of the Stadium to light up the torch ...

**可燃点**：和平乌鲁！和平乌鲁！\
**Spathodea**: Ulu, Ulu!

**可燃点**：我如你愿望一般长大了吗？我是一个新的我了吗？\
**Spathodea**: Have I grown up like you wished for me? Am I a new and different me now?

欢呼、歌唱、口哨与快门淋满年轻姑娘的背脊。\
Cheers, songs, whistles, and clicks encourage the girl forward.

她尽可能快速地跑着，打开嗓子呼唤。\
She runs as fast as she can, calling out.

**可燃点**：这对我来说的一瞬间，对你来说，却是数以千万计的漫长日夜，我想让你满意，我想让你快乐！\
**Spathodea**: This is just a moment of my life, but I know you've waited a million days and nights for it! I want you to be proud! I want you to be happy!

**和平乌鲁**：我的朋友！我的朋友啊！\
**Ulu**: My friend, my dear friend!

**和平乌鲁**：你已经是我的小火了，但你也不只是我的小火……\
**Ulu**: You're my Flammy, but you're so much more than that ...

**和平乌鲁**：你还是我的可燃点，我的小姑娘……！\
**Ulu**: You're also my Spathodea ... My little girl ...!

**和平乌鲁**：你已经长大了，如我无数次梦到的那样成长了——这儿的毒蛇没有伤你分毫，没有损害你的身体与心灵——\
**Ulu**: You have grown up, as I have dreamed of countless times. The snakes here didn't lay a single tooth on you. Both your body and mind are intact.

**观众**：哎呀？那是什么？圣火中流出了好多水滴——！\
**Audience**: Hey, what's that? The Uluru Flame is dropping water!

**和平乌鲁**：呜……\
**Ulu**: *sobs*

**和平乌鲁**：呜哇哇啊啊啊啊啊啊啊啊啊——！\
**Ulu**: *cries out loudly*

**可燃点**：和，和平乌鲁……？！\
**Spathodea**: U-Ulu?!

火焰在泪水中熄灭，小祭司的脚步猛地停止，左右颠倒着失去了重心。\
The flame is put out by her tears. The little Priestess stops running subconsciously, which makes her lose her balance.

摇摇不定地向前扑倒。\
She falls forward to the ground.

**观众**：火……圣火、圣火它——\
**Audience**: Flame! The Uluru Flame! It's ...!

**观众**：是——是那个拉普拉斯的孩子！\
**Audience**: It's-It's the kid of Laplace!

**爱兹拉**：……！\
**Ezra**: ...!

**观众**：火——圣火！圣火重新被点燃了！\
**Audience**: Flame! The Uluru Flame! It's lit up again!

重燃的火焰凝聚在年轻孩子们相连的手中，温热宜人。\
The flame that revives is burning in their joined hands, feeling warm and comfortable.

爱兹拉惶惶然地四处张望起来，人群的喝彩这才到达他耳中。\
Ezra finally hears the people's cheers as he looks around at a loss.

**爱兹拉**：成……成功了！\
**Ezra**: We ... we did it!

**爱兹拉**：乌卢鲁运动会的开幕式，成功了——！\
**Ezra**: The opening ceremony took place just as we planned!

**可燃点**：太好了，太好了！我们成功了！谢谢你——爱兹拉！\
**Spathodea**: Yes, YES! We made it! Thank you, Ezra!

可燃点呵护着尚且脆弱的和平乌鲁，一把抱住和自己一般纤细的少年。\
Spathodea holds the weak Ulu gently while holding the boy in her arms.

**可燃点**：你的手中着火，你……你也和我有一样的想法，对不对？如果不是真心渴望着乌卢鲁运动会，那些火焰是不会在你身上燃烧的！\
**Spathodea**: The flame is burning in your hand. You ... You share the same thought, don't you? It wouldn't have burned on you if you weren't wishing for the Games sincerely!

**爱兹拉**：我……我的确很希望这个比赛举办成功。\
**Ezra**: Yes, I, I do. I want it to be a successful event.

**爱兹拉**：它对你们很重要，现在……对我们也是。\
**Ezra**: It's important to you, and so to us now.

**爱兹拉**：爱兹拉露出笑容，他离开怀抱，将自己与可燃点的手高高举起。\
**Ezra**: With a smile on his face, Ezra holds Spathodea's hand and lifts it in the air.

**爱兹拉**：所有现场的、广播前的、电视与网络前的人类与神秘学家呀！我请你们与我一同见证这火炬的点燃。\
**Ezra**: Mankind and arcanists who are here with us or following the event through radio, TV, or internet, I invite you to witness the blazing of the Uluru torch.

**爱兹拉**：她的名叫和平乌鲁，象征着和平、拼搏与竞技的崇高精神。\
**Ezra**: She is Ulu, the noble spirit of peace, hard work, and competition.

**爱兹拉**：在过去的数千年中，无数比赛之内这象征着和平与所有美好精神的火种，曾登至最高的山峰，行至幽深的海峡。\
**Ezra**: In the past thousands of years, the holy fire has been to the highest mountain and touched the rocks in the deepest sea, taking the peace and all other noble qualities to every corner of this world.

**爱兹拉**：她高飞直到宇宙，与所有繁星展现，又于船中、飞行器中、双脚之下、双手之上传递。\
**Ezra**: It was also brought out of this world, into space by rockets, and traveled among the stars. From ships, to spaceships, from one hand to another, it has journeyed far.

**可燃点**：而此次，唯一一次，将被点燃的手炬奔火而来。\
**Spathodea**: And now, for the first time, the torch to be lit has come to the flame.

**可燃点**：人类的双手与神秘学家的双手在此一同燃烧。\
**Spathodea**: The flame is burning in the joint hands of human and arcanist.

**可燃点&爱兹拉**：在此处，我们许诺将忘却仇恨、纷争、纠乱与混杂的昨日。\
**Spathodea&Ezra**: We hereby swear we shall forget the hatred, conflict, turbulence, and chaos of the past.

**可燃点&爱兹拉**：我们将奔跑，以竞技的精神，我们将行走，以人最初的姿态。\
**Spathodea&Ezra**: We shall run in the name of sportsmanship. We shall walk in the original form of men.

**可燃点&爱兹拉**：我们彼此比量，参与大过于胜利。\
**Spathodea&Ezra**: We shall compete against each other, not for victory but for participation.

## RUG-15 红岩护卫队 / The Uluru Guardians

**爱兹拉**：所以——比赛结束之后，沙丝绒小姐去医院找了马科尔先生吗？\
**Ezra**: So, did Ms. Desert Flannel go to the hospital to visit Mr. Makower?

**可燃点**：没错！她买了所有杂志，带着去找……啊，对了，你还不知道沙丝绒和马科尔之间的故事吧——\
**Spathodea**: Yeah! She bought all the magazines with that photo and brought them to ... Oh, wait, I guess you don't know the story between Desert Flannel and Makower.

**爱兹拉**：不，我不知道，我当时正在房间里思考白天看到的事情。\
**Ezra**: No idea. I was in my room pondering what happened that day.

**可燃点**：……\
**Spathodea**: ...

**爱兹拉**：……\
**Ezra**: ...

**沙丝绒**：别——别这么看着我呀！我都说了！那么蠢的故事我只会讲一次！\
**Desert Flannel**: Don't, don't look at me like that! I've told you I will never repeat that story again!

**爱兹拉**：好吧，我想我不知道也没什么……那只是一个故事而已。\
**Ezra**: OK, I guess it doesn't matter if I never had the chance of hearing it. It's just a story.

乖孩子总是让人于心不忍。\
It is very hard to disappoint a child like that.

沙丝绒举手投降，调整了一下坐姿，拍了拍身边的座位。\
Throwing her hands in the air, Desert Flannel declares her defeat. She makes some space and pats the seat beside her.

**沙丝绒**：好吧！我讲——我讲就是了！过来吧，小崽子！\
**Desert Flannel**: Fine! I will, I will tell it to you! Come over here, kid.

**爱兹拉**：太感谢你了！\
**Ezra**: You are so kind!

爱兹拉很快坐在了那里，乖巧地等待着。\
Ezra sits beside Desert Flannel and waits like a quiet kitten.

**沙丝绒**：你们都该知道，我有很多工作，我总忙于各种工作，而这工作的后头是一个个主顾，代表着许多许多钱。\
**Desert Flannel**: You must all know that I have many jobs. These part-time jobs eat away most of my time, but the clients who gave me these jobs never let me go home empty-handed.

**沙丝绒**：当一个人为了钱能接受“绝大部分”工作的时候，她总会遇到一些“诡异”的主顾。\
**Desert Flannel**: If you were me, you'd know that … if you are willing enough to take as many jobs as possible, you'd meet some strange clients.

**沙丝绒**：比如扮演别人的母亲参加家长参观日。\
**Desert Flannel**: Like going to a School Day pretending to be someone's mom, or ...

**沙丝绒**：又比如为盲人的视觉系猎犬编满302条辫子。\
**Desert Flannel**: Braiding the hair of a punk hound in 302 pigtails for a blind man.

**沙丝绒**：也比如——在深夜，带着价值昂贵到可以买下我整个公寓的摄影机，趴在满是露水的雨林草丛里等待一种罕见的野生鸟。\
**Desert Flannel**: Or, waiting for a rare bird at midnight, carrying a camera which was expensive enough to pay for my apartment.

**爱兹拉**：我知道这种工作，有时候我在拉普拉斯的同僚也会雇佣别人帮忙收集信息。\
**Ezra**: I know. Sometimes, my colleagues in Laplace would also hire others to help collect information they need.

**爱兹拉**：不过只要有时间，大家还是更愿意自己去森林里转转……\
**Ezra**: But if we have the time, most of us would prefer to take a walk in the forest and try our luck.

**沙丝绒**：是的，那家伙也是这么说的。\
**Desert Flannel**: Yes, that's exactly what my client said.

**沙丝绒**：他给了我一笔丰厚的报酬。丰厚到让我睁着一双满是红血丝的眼睛等待着那只粉鳞火炬蜂鸟出现。\
**Desert Flannel**: He paid me well for the job, so generous that I stared at the dark and waited for that Pink Torch Hummingbird to show up, despite my bloodshot eyes.

**沙丝绒**：一天，两天，三天。\
**Desert Flannel**: One day, two days, and three days passed.

**沙丝绒**：我都没有等到那只粉鳞火炬蜂鸟。\
**Desert Flannel**: I didn't even see anything like it.

**沙丝绒**：但是……我见到了，另一样能与之媲美的“神奇动物”。\
**Desert Flannel**: But I saw a wonder beast, just as extraordinary as the Hummingbird.

停顿几秒，沙丝绒深深地吸入一口气。\
Pausing for a second, Desert Flannel takes a deep breath.

**沙丝绒**：那是一只——粉色闪光鸭嘴兽。\
**Desert Flannel**: A ... Pink Glittering Platypus.

**爱兹拉**：粉色的——闪光的——鸭嘴兽……？\
**Ezra**: Pink Glittering Platypus?

**沙丝绒**：它是粉色的，也闪鳞光，谁知道蜂鸟是不是某种“圆圆胖胖的鸭嘴兽”在鸟类爱好者之间的外号呢？——我当然拍下了它。\
**Desert Flannel**: It's pink, and it's glittering, and who knows whether Pink Torch Hummingbird is a strange nickname for that platypus? Of course, I have to take a picture of it.

**沙丝绒**：但是想也明白，一个鸟类爱好者是不需要鸭嘴兽的。\
**Desert Flannel**: But you know, a bird lover won't need the picture of a platypus.

**沙丝绒**：我把那张照片卖给了儿童趣闻杂志……然后嘛……如果你们读过足够多的俗套小说，应该就能猜到……\
**Desert Flannel**: So I sold it to Kidding Fun, a children's magazine. What happened next should be very evident to you, if you read enough bad novels.

**爱兹拉**：难……难道？那就是——\
**Ezra**: Is, is that ...?

**沙丝绒**：……嗯，没错，那只鸭嘴兽就是喝了幻形剂的马科尔。\
**Desert Flannel**: Yes, that's right. That platypus was Makower, who took the Transformation Potion.

**爱兹拉**：啊，这个……马科尔先生为什么要那样做呢？\
**Ezra**: Ah, but why would he do that?

**沙丝绒**：也许是兴趣，也许是意外，总之——据他自己所说，他只是被人所害，绝非个人爱好。\
**Desert Flannel**: Perhaps he was looking for some fun, or maybe it was an accident. Anyway, according to him, someone pulled out a prank on him, and it was definitely not his own choosing.

**沙丝绒**：而那张照片被刊登在杂志上之后，他飞速辞掉了工作。\
**Desert Flannel**: He quit his job the moment that picture was published.

**沙丝绒**：他离开了自己的工作和朋友圈子，成为了一个伟大的复仇者，致力于让我品尝与他相同的痛苦。\
**Desert Flannel**: He left his friends and family, and became a revenger, striving to put me into a miserable situation, just like what he has gone through.

**沙丝绒**：而我呢，在这次赚了大钱之后，买下了我的公寓——还有所有的当期杂志。\
**Desert Flannel**: So, this time, after I made this fortune, I bought the apartment, and every copy of that issue of the magazine.

**爱兹拉**：嗯……你想把他们卖给马科尔先生吗？\
**Ezra**: Mmm. Were you planning to sell them all to Mr. Makower?

**沙丝绒**：不——当然不啦！\
**Desert Flannel**: No, of course not!

**沙丝绒**：你这小子把我当成什么坏人啦！我把他从医院里带出来，找了片空地，把那些东西一把火都烧掉了！\
**Desert Flannel**: Who do you think I am? I picked him up at the hospital, took him somewhere quiet, and burnt all the magazines in front of him.

**沙丝绒**：他当时啊，哭得可大声了，哼哼～听起来真让人开心～\
**Desert Flannel**: He was, oh my gosh, crying so loud! Heh-heh, that was pleasant to hear.

幕布另一侧，年轻的女声传来，打断了对话。\
On the other side of the curtain, a young female voice interrupts the conversation.

**工作人员**：沙丝绒小姐、可燃点小姐、爱兹拉先生！采访的准备已经做好了，请各位移步台前！\
**Staff**: Ms. Desert Flannel, Ms. Spathodea, and Mr. Ezra, the interview is ready to start. Please follow me to the stage!

**爱兹拉**：啊！好的，我们这就来！\
**Ezra**: Ah! Yes! In a minute!

孩子们率先动身，可燃点凑近爱兹拉，小声地询问。\
The kids move before Desert Flannel does. Spathodea gets closer to Ezra and asks a question quietly.

**可燃点**：故事的后半段你听懂了吗？\
**Spathodea**: Did you get the ending of the story?

**爱兹拉**：不……我也不明白。\
**Ezra**: No, not really.

**可燃点**：哈！看来也有神秘学家和人类都不明白的东西存在啊！\
**Spathodea**: Hah! So there IS something neither arcanists nor humans can understand!

**爱兹拉**：或许我们可以问问维尔汀，她只比我们大一点儿，但今天她不在这儿。\
**Ezra**: Perhaps we can ask Vertin later. She's a bit older than us, but she's not here today.

**爱兹拉**：好像是和和平乌鲁女士一同去了乌卢鲁运动场……\
**Ezra**: I think she went to the Stadium with Ms. Ulu.

**和平乌鲁**：……\
**Ulu**: ...

**和平乌鲁**：生吞黄金，歌舞致死，数字的冒险。\
**Ulu**: The gold-swallowing crowd, the apocalyptic hedonism, and the adventure on the island of numbers ...

**和平乌鲁**：原来，在我沉睡的这些年内世界已经变成了这副模样……\
**Ulu**: So this is what the world has become when I was in slumber for all these years ...

**和平乌鲁**：我曾经经历过无数雨季，瞧见乌卢鲁岩之上悬挂彩虹，却从未见过那样的“暴雨”……\
**Ulu**: I have experienced countless rains, and have even seen the rainbow above Uluru, but I've never seen anything like the "Storm" ...

火焰发出了一声温热的叹息。\
The flame lets out a contented sigh.

**和平乌鲁**：它们……竟然能够如此轻易地改变一切。\
**Ulu**: I can't believe ... it just changed everything so easily.

**维尔汀**：但是乌卢鲁运动场没有改变。\
**Vertin**: But the Uluru Stadium is still here.

**维尔汀**：我知道这世界上有些地点是神奇的，它们具有玄而不明的力量，得以在“暴雨”中开辟出一线生机。\
**Vertin**: I know there are spots with mysterious power in this world. They can provide a slim chance of survival in the "Storm."

**维尔汀**：这儿正是这样的地方。这样的地方……总会成为各方争夺的资源。\
**Vertin**: And the Stadium is exactly one of them. Such a place ... will be desired by different forces one day. It's just a matter of time.

**和平乌鲁**：比如你所说的“重塑之手”，他们垂涎乌卢鲁，如同狼垂涎红肉。\
**Ulu**: Like the Manus Vindictae you talked about. To them, the Uluru Stadium is like a piece of meat to a hungry wolf.

**维尔汀**：没错。\
**Vertin**: That's right.

**维尔汀**：基金会已经开展了乌卢鲁保卫队计划，因需要长期驻扎，澳大利亚分部的人员构成无法兼容如此巨大的任务。\
**Vertin**: The Foundation has already launched the Uluru Guarding Project. It will be a long-term mission and involves a heavy workload, and the Australia branch doesn't have enough manpower for it.

**维尔汀**：而后，有许多人前往了基金会澳大利亚分部的会客窗口。\
**Vertin**: Fortunately, a lot of people went to the visitor window of the branch.

**和平乌鲁**：他们……担忧乌卢鲁运动场？\
**Ulu**: They are ... worried about the Stadium?

**维尔汀**：是的。他们很担心这里。\
**Vertin**: Yes, a lot.

**维尔汀**：他们自愿守卫与驻扎在这里，花费时间与精力守卫这里。\
**Vertin**: They volunteered to station here to protect it, even at the cost of their own time and effort.

**维尔汀**：他们成为了一支由31位神秘学家，29名人类构成的“乌卢鲁岩护卫队”，他们之中有医生与作家，也有出租车司机与报刊亭老板。\
**Vertin**: They have built the Uluru Guardians which consists of 31 arcanists and 29 humans. There are doctors, writers, taxi drivers, newsstand owners, and so on.

**维尔汀**：……他们都是这场乌卢鲁运动会的观众。\
**Vertin**: And they are all among the audience of the Games.

**和平乌鲁**：……呵。\
**Ulu**: Heh.

**和平乌鲁**：孩子，你做到了。\
**Ulu**: You made it, child.

**和平乌鲁**：这的确是一个崭新的开端。\
**Ulu**: This is indeed a brand new beginning.

**维尔汀**：所以我想将它留在这里。\
**Vertin**: That's why I want to keep it here.

本耶普化身的巨石已在乌卢鲁的红土上烘得温热。\
The giant rock which the Bunyip turned into has become warm on the red soil of Uluru.

不再能感受到一丝湿冷或是疑窦。\
No more wet, cold, question, or doubt.

由背脊向两侧铺开，巨石与火凿开的细渠汇成数条句文。\
The strokes carved out by gravel and fire run down from the Bunyip's spine to both sides of its body. At the end of each ridge, words are inscribed, turning the rock into a monument.

**维尔汀**：“我们将奔跑，以竞技的精神。”\
**Vertin**: "We shall run in the name of sportsmanship."

**和平乌鲁**：“我们将行走，以人最初的姿态。”\
**Ulu**: "We shall walk in the original form of men."

**和平乌鲁&维尔汀**：“我们彼此比量，参与大过于胜利。”\
**Ulu&Vertin**: "We shall compete against each other, not for victory but for participation."

**和平乌鲁&维尔汀**：——人类与神秘学家共书。\
**Ulu&Vertin**: By both humans and arcanists.

**维尔汀**：无论雨幕多少次将这个世界洗刷一新，\
无论时代、风貌与人们的生活方式如何变幻，\
当一无所知的人群再次开启乌卢鲁运动场之时，\
他们都将会记起它所代表的精神，所传递的信念。\
时代的洪流中，瞬息万变，唯此永存。\
**Vertin**: No matter how many times the Storm reshapes the world from top to bottom ...\
No matter how the times or the lifestyle change ...\
No matter how ignorant people become ...\
Whenever they open the gate to the Uluru Stadium again,\
they will remember the spirit and faith it has been conveying.\
Things will change in the unstoppable river of time,\
yet the Uluru Stadium shall remain forever.
